Nhengo dzeParamende dzekuWales dzainetseka kuti 'dzaizoratidzika semapenzi'
Pane kutya pakati pedzimwe nhengo dzeparamende nezvechikarakadzo chekuti zita ravo rinofanira kuchinja kuita MWPs (Nhengo yeParamende yeWelsh).
Zvabuda nekuda kwehurongwa hwekuchinja zita redare kuve Paramende yeWales.
Nhengo dzeParamende dzemumapato akasiyana-siyana dziri kutyira kuti zvinogona kukonzera kushorwa.
Imwe nhengo yeParamende yebato reLabour akati boka rake range riri kunetseka kuti "zvinonzwika sekuti Twp uye Pwp."
Kune vaverengi vari kunze kweWales: MuWelsh twp zvinoreva hurongwa uye pwp zvichireva tsvina.
Imwe Nhengo yeParamende yakati boka rese zvaro range "risiri kufara" uye rakakarakadza dzimwewo pfungwa.
Imwe nhengo yeWelsh Conservative yakati boka rake rainge "rakajekerwa mupfungwa" pamusoro pekuchinja kwezita asi yakaratidza kuti kwaingova kuchinja kwerevo kudiki kubva pakuti MWP kuenda pakuti Muppet.
Murevo ino vara rechiWelsh w rinotaurwa zvakafanana sekutaurwa kunoitwa vara rechirungu u muYorkshire.
Komishoni yeDare, iyo ichiri kugadzira mutemo wekuti kuchinja kwemazita kutange, yakati: "Chisarudzo chekupedzisira pamusoro petsananguro yekuti Nhengo dzeDare dzichadeedzwa nezita ripi chichatsamira panhengo dzacho pachadzo."
Mutemo weHurumende yeWales Act 2017 vakapa masimba kudare reWelsh ekuti richinje zita raro.
Muna chikumi, Komishoni yakaburitsa zvakabuda patsvakurudzo yakaitwa kune veruzhinji pachikarakadzo icho chakawana tsigiro yakakura yekudaidza dare iri kuti Paramende yeWelsh.
Panyaya yezita reNhengo dzeParamende, Komishoni yakada zita rekuti Nhengo dzeParamende dzeWelsh (Welsh Parliament Members) kana kuti WMPs, asi chisarudzo cheMWP ndicho chakawana tsigiro yakakura patsvakurudzo yakaitwa kune veruzhinji.
Nhengo dzeParamende pari zvino dzine zvimwezve zvikarakadzo, asi nyaya yekusvika pachibvumirano inogona kutemesa musoro Mukurumukuru ari kutarisira nhau iyi, Elin Jones, uyo ari kutarisirwa kuendesa mutemo usati wapasiswa pane chinjo dzakaitwa mukati memasvondo.
Mutemo pachinjo uchabatanidza dzimwewo chinjo mumashandiro edare, kusanganisira mitemo yekudzinga basa Nhengo dzeParamende uye marongerwo emashandiro ekomiti.
Nhengo dzeParamende dzichawana mhinduro yekupedzisira pamubvunzo wekuti vachadaidzwa nezita ripi pavachakweshana pfungwa vachipa maonero avo pamusoro pemutemo uyu.
Vanhu vekuMacedonia vanoenda kusarudzo dzekuona pfungwa dzeveruzhinji pakuchinja zita renyika
Vasarudzi vachavhota musi veSvondo kuti vaone kana vachifanira kuchinja zita renyika kuve "Republic of North Macedonia."
Chisarudzo cheveruzhinji chakarongwa kuti chiitwe nekuda kwekugadzirisa gakava rave nemakumi emakore riripo nenyika yavakavakidzana nayo yeGreece, iyo ine purovhinzi yayo ine zita rekuti Macedonia.
Vatungamiriri muAthens vakabvira kare vachiti zita renyika revavakavakidzana navo nechekuchamhembe rinoreva kuti vari kuti nzvimbo iyi ndeyavo uye kakawanda vakaramba chikumbiro chayo chekupinda muEU neNATO.
Mutungamiriri weMacedonia Gjorge Ivanov, uyo arikupikisa zvikuru kuchinjwa kwezita, akati haasi kuzotambira zvinenge zvabuda pakusarudza.
Zvisinei, vatsigiri vechisarudzo cheveruzhinji, kusanganisira Mukuru weMakurukota Zoran Zaev, vane maonero ekuti kuchinja zita kunongova mubhadharo wekupinda nawo muEU uye NATO.
Mabhero emuSt. Martin's Onyarara Nekuomerwa kweMachechi emuHarlem
"Kare-kare, vanhu vakura vandakataura navo vakati paive nebhawa uye chechi pakona imwe neimwe," VaAdams vakadaro.
"Nhasi, hapana chiripo."
Akati kutsakatika kwemabhawa kwainzwisisika.
"Vanhu vanowadzana nenzira dzakasiyana-siyana mazuva ano", akadaro.
"Mabhawa haasisiri nzvimbo yekutandarira uko vanhu vanoenda pavadira."
Nekuda kwemachechi, ari kunetseka kuti mari inobva mukutengeswa kwemidziyo haizogari kwenguva inenge ichitarisirwa nevatungamiriri, "uye munguva pfupi kana kuti iri mberi vachangodzokera pavakatangira."
Akawedzera kuti, machechi, anogona kutsiviwa nezvivakwa zvine makamuri-kamuri akazara nevanhu vasingazobatsiri kutarisira zvivakwa zviri pedyo navo zvinoyera.
"Chiverengero chikuru chevanhu vanotenga makamuri ezvivakwa izvi ndeverudzi rwechichena," akadaro, "uye naizvozvo zvichakurumidzisa kusvika kwezuva apo machechi ose achavhara nekuda kwekuti panogona kusava nemukana wekuti vanenge vapinda muzvivakwa izvi vazove nhengo dzemachechi aya."
Machechi ose ari maviri akavakwa nenhengo dzechichena Harlem isati yavakugarwa nevatema - Vagari muGuta Guru muna 1870, St. Martin's ichizotevera makore gumi akazotevera
Ungano yekutanga yevachena veMethodist yakabuda makore ekuma1930.
Ungano yevatema yainamatira pedyo yakabva yatora chivakwa chacho.
St. Martin's yakatanga kushandiswa neungano yevatema yaive pasi paMufundisi John Howard Johnson, uyo akatungamirira pakuratidzira kwakaitwa nevatengesi muna125th Street, mugwagwa mukuru wevatengi muHarlem, uyo akaramba kupinza basa kana kusimudzira vechitema.
Moto wakaitika mugore ra1939 vakasiya waparadza zvakaipisisa chivakwa ichi, asi sezvo vateveri vaBaba Johnson vakaita hurongwa hwekuchivakazve, vakakumikidza kuiswa kwemabhero.
Mufundisi David Johnson, mwanakomana waBabaJohnson uye uyo akavatsiva paSt. Martin's, akapa zita mabhero aya kuti "mabhero evarombo."
Nyanzvi yairidza mabhero aya muna Chikunguru akapawo rimwe zita: "Pfuma yenhaka" uye "chiridzwa chechinyakare chisingatsivike."
Nyanzvi, Tiffany Ng weYunivhesiti yeMichigan, akaona kuti aive mabhero ekutanga kuridzwa nemuimbi wechitema, Dionisio A. Lind, uyo akazoenda kune mabhero makuru ekuRiverside Church makore 18 apfuura.
VaMerriweather vakati St. Martin's haina kuvatsiva.
Zvakaitika paSt. Martin's mumwedzi mishoma yapfuura yange iri nyaya yakaoma zvikuru kunzwisisa yevagadziri vemapurani nevanotarisira basa rekuvaka, vamwe vakaunzwa nevatungamiriri zvavo vechechi uye vamwe vacho vakaunzwa neVakuru vemibatanidzwa yemachechi.
Musangano wevanokudzwa - boka rinotungamirira rechechi, rinoumbwa nevatungamiririwo zvavo - vakanyorera boka revatungamiriri vemubatanidzwa wemachechi mumwedzi waChikunguru vachishushikana nenyaya yekuti boka revatungamiriri wemubatanidzwa wemachechi "vaida kutsvaka kupfuudza miripo" kuvatungamiriwo zvavo, kunyange zvazvo vatungamiririwo zvavo vange vasina kubatanidzwa mukupinza basa vagadziri vemapurani nevanotarisira basa rekuvaka avo vakange vaunzwa nevatungamiriri wemubatanidzwa wemachechi.
Vamwe vateveri vakatsutsumwa kuti vatungamiriri vemubatanidzwa wemachechi vakange vaita zvinhu nenzira isina kujeka.
Shaki yakakuvadza mwana anemakore 13 aiita zvekutamba mumvura muCalifornia
Shaki yakaruma ndokukuvadza mukomana ane makore 13 memusi weMugovera apo aisvetukira mumvura achida kubata gakanje muCalifonia mukutanga kwemwaka wemagakanje, vakuru-vakuru vakadaro.
Akarumwa nguva dza7 mangwanani dzisati dzanyatsokwana pedyo neBeacon's Beach muEncinitas.
Chad Hammel akaudza weKSWB-TV muSan Diego kuti paainge achisvetukira mumvura neshamwari dzake kwenguva ingaita chidimbu cheawa Mugovera mangwanana akanzwa mukomana aidaidzira achitsvaka rubatsiro ndokushambira vari mukachikepe kuti vanomubatsira kubuda mumvura.
Hammel akati pakutanga aifunga kuti kwaingove kufarira kubata kwaainge aita gakanje, asi “akazonzwa kuti ange ari kuchema achiti, ‘Ndarumwa!
Ndarumwa!
Bandauko rake rose rainge rarumwa ndokuvhurika, “Hammel anoti akazvicherechedza paakangosvika paive nemukomana wacho.
"Ndakashevedzera kune vose kuti vabude mumvura: 'Mumvura mune shaki!'" Hammel akawedzera kudaro.
Mukomana wacho akatakurwa nendege kuenda kuchipatara cheRady Children’s Hospital chiri muSan Diego uko ari kunzi ari paurwere hwakaipisisa.
Rudzi rweshaki yakamuruma haruna kuzivikanwa.
Mukuru anoona nezvechengeteko Larry Giles akataura pamusangano wevatapi wenhau kuti pane shaki yainge yamboonekwa munzvimbo iyoyo mavhiki mashoma izvi zvisati zvaitika, asi zvakaonekwa kuti shaki yacho yakanga isiri yerudzi rwune ngozi.
Giles akavedzera kuti nyakurumwa akakuvara zvakaipisisa panzvimbo yepachipfuva.
Vakuru-vakuru vakavhara pekupinda napo kumahombekombe tichibva nechekuMahombekombe ePonto muCasablad kusvika kuSwami's iri muEcinitas kwemaawa anoita 48 kuti paitwe ongororo uye kutyira ngozi.
Giles akacherechedza kuti pane marudzi anopfuura 135 emashaki munzvimbo iyoyo, asi mazhinji acho anonzi haana njodzi.
Hurongwa hweSainsbury’s ndehwekupinda mumusika weUK wekutengesa zvishongo zverunako
Sainsbury's ichange iine Magambutsu, Superdrug neDebenhams zvakarongerwa mumasherufu akada kufanana neyemuzvitoro zvikuru zvine vashandi vakanyatsodzidzira basa.
Sechikamu chekunyatsopinda mumusika wezvishongo zverunako wemuUK une hukoshi hwemabhiriyoni £2.8, uyo uri kuramba uchikura panguva apo mwero wekutengwa kwembatya nemidziyo yemumba uri kuderera, masherufu makuru akanaka achaedzwa muzvitoro 11 munyika yose ozoendeswa muzvitoro zvakawanda mugore rinotevera kana izvi zvabudirira.
Bhizimusi rezvishongo zverunako rauya apo masupamaketi ari kutsvaka nzira dzekushandisa nzvimbo dzemasherufu aimbove neMaterevhizheni, microwaves, nemimwewo midziyo yemumba.
Sainsbury's yakati ichapeta kaviri huwandu hwemarudzi ezvishongo zverunako kusvika pa3,000, kusanganisira marudzi akadai seRevlon, Essie, Tweezerman uye Dr. PawPaw kekutanga.
Mhando dzitoripo kubva kuL'Oreal, Maybelline uye Burt's Bees dzichawanawo nzvimbo dzakakura dzinenge dzakaiswa zviratidzo kungofanana nedzinowanikwa muzvitoro zvakadai seBoots.
Supamaketi iyi iri kubura zvakare Dura rayo rezvizoro zvakasiyana-siyana kuitira kuti zvakawanda zvacho zvienderane nezvinodiwa nevasingashandisi zvigadzirwa zvinobva mumhuka - zvinova chinhu chiri kufarirwa chaizvo nevatengi vechidiki.
Mukuwedzera, chitoro chinotengesa zvekufafaidza zvinonhuhwirira cheFragrance Shop chichaedza dzimwe mhando dziri kudiwa nevatengi muzvitoro zviviri zveSainsbury's, yekutanga yacho yakavhura muCroydon, nechekumaodznyemba kweLondon, svondo rapfuura ukuwo yechipiri ichavhura muSelly Oak, iri muBirmingham, nechekunopera kwegore rino.
Zvekutenga paindaneti pamwe nekuchinja kuripo kwekutengwa kwezvokudya zvidiki-zvidiki mazuva ose muzvitoro zviri pedyo zvinoreva kuti masupamaketi avekufanira kuita zvakawanda pakukwezva vanhu kuti vauye kuzvitoro zvavo.
Mike Coupe, anowe mukuru webasa paSainsbury's, akati zvitoro izvi zvichawedzera kuratidzika sezvakaita zvitoro zvikuru sezvo supamaketi iyi iri kushandisa nzira yekutengesa zvinhu zvakasiyana-siyana uye zvisinei nezvokudya pakuedza kukwikwidzana neAldi uye Lidl avo varikuderedza mitengo yezvinhu.
Sainsbury's yange iri kuisa zvitoro zveArgos mumazana ezvitoro uyewo yakatangawo Zvivakwa zvakawanda zvekugara kutangira payakatenga zvitoro izvi zviri zviviri makore maviri apfuura, izvo zvainoti zvakawedzeresa kutengwa kwezvokudya uye kuwanikwa kwemari yakawanda.
Kuedza kwakaitwa nesupamaketi iyi munguva yakapfuura kusimudzira zvitoro zvayo zvinotengesa zvinhu zverunako uye mishonga kwakakundikana.
Sainsbury's yakaedza kuita mubatanidzwa neBoots mukutanga kwemakore ekuma 2000, asi mubatanidzwa uyu wakapera pashure pekunetsana kuti mari yaipinda kubva kuchikamu chezvemishonga chiri mumasupamaketi ayo yaizopatsanurwa sei.
Zano idzva rakazobuda pashure pekunge Sainsbury's yatengesa bhizimusi rayo rine zvitoro zvemishonga 281 kunaCelesio, muridzi wendandanda yezvitoro zvemishonga inonzi Lloyds Pharmacy, nemari inoita mamiriyoni £125, makore matatu apfuura.
Yakati Lloyds yaizove nebasa rekuita pahurongwa uhwu, nekuwedzera marudzi akawanda ezvizoro zvinodhura zvakadai seLa Roche-Posay uye Vichy muzvitoro zvina.
Paul Mills-Hicks, anove mukuru-mukuru wezvokutengeserana weSainsbury’s, akati: "Tavandudza chitarisiko nemarongerwo emasherufu ezvishongo zverunako kuitira kufadza vatengi vedu.
Takaitawo hurongwa hwekuti pave nenyanzvi dzinenge dziripo nguva dzose kuti dzipe mazano.
Ndandanda yezvigadzirwa zvedu yakagadzirirwa kugutsa zvinodikanwa zvevanhu vose nekukwezva uye kuve pedyosa nevatengi zvoreva kuti tave nenzira yekutengesa inokwezva zvikuru kusiyana nenzira yekutengesa yaiitwa kare."
Peter Jones 'otsamwa kwazvo' pashure pekunge Holly Willoughby abuda muhurongwa hwaizobudisa mari inosvika mamiriyoni £11
Dragons Den star Peter Jones osara 'akatsamwa kwazvo' pashure pekunge Mutauri wepaterevhizheni Holly Willoughby amuda muhurongwa hwaizobudisa mamiriyoni £11 mubhizimusi rake rinoshambadzira zvemararamiro akanaka kuti anyatsobatikane nehurongwa hwake hutsva neMarks & Spencer uye ITV
Willoughby haana nguva yekuita zvekushambadzira zvipfeko zvepamba nezvimwewo zvemhando yeTruly.
Bhizimusi revaviri ava rakafananidzwa nerudzi rwebhizinisi raGwyneth Paltrow's Goop.
Mutauri mangwanani ano,ane makore 37, atumira mashoko paInstagram ekuzivisa kuti ari kusiya.
Holly Willoughby osiya nyanzvi yeDragons" Den Peter Jones atsamwa zvikuru nekubuda kwaakangoerekana aita mubhizimusi rine mari yakawanda rekushambadza mararamiro emhando - kuti atarisane nehurongwa hwake hutsva hune mari zhinji neMarks & Spencer uye ITV.
Kuri kubva mashoko vari kuti Jones "akatsamwa kwazvo" apo musikana ane mukurumbira wepaterevhizheni akabvuma mumusangano waitsviriridza nemusi weChipiri pamuzinda webhizimusi rake muMarlow, iri muBuckinghamshire, kuti hurongwa hwake hutsva - hunokosha mamiriyoni £1.5 - hworeva kuti haachisina nguva yakakwana yekuti azvipire kubhizimusi ravo rezvipfeko zvepamba nezvimwewo zvemhando yeTruly.
Bhizimusi iri rakafananidzwa neraGwyneth Paltrow's Goop uye rakanga richitarisirwa kuti raizowana mari inopeta kawiri pfuma yemamiriyoni £11 yaWilloughby
Sezvo Willoughby, ane makore 37, akazivisa paInstagram kuti ave kubuda muTruly, Jones akabuda muBritain akananga kune imwe yemisha yake yekuzororera.
Kunobva mashoko vakati: "Truly yaiwe pamusoro chaizvo pazvinhu zvinokosha kunaHolly.
Yaizova nguva yemberi yakareba chaizvo kwaari yaizoita kuti apfuure mumakumi emakore aitevera.
Chisarudzo chake chokubuda chakasiya munhu wose achikahadzika nazvo.
Hapana aibvuma zvakanga zvichiitika nemusi weChipiri, zuva rekuparura rakange ratove pedyo.
Pane nzvimbo yekuchengetera yakazara nezvinhu zvakamirira kutengeswa paMuzinda Mukuru weMarlow."
Nyanzvi dzinofunga kuti kusiya kwaita Mutauri weChikamu Chekuseni chepaterevhizheni, uyo ari shasha inovimbwa nayo muBritain, kunogona kuita kuti kambani irasikirwe nemamiriyoni nekuda kwekushandiswa kwemari yakawanda muzvinhu zvakadai semakusheni, makenduru kusvika kuzvinhu zvakadai sezvishongo uye zvipfeko zvepamba, uye mikana yekunonoka kuparurwa kwayo.
Uye zvinogona kureva kuparara kweushamwari hwenguva refu.
Willoughby anove mai wevana vatatu uye murume wake Dan Baldwin vaive vanhu vepedyo zvikuru naJones uye mudzimai wake Tara Capp kwemakore anosvika gumi.
Willoughby akavamba Truly pamwe chete naCapp mugore ra2016 uye Jones, uyo ane makore 52, akajoina sasachigaro mumwedzi waKurume.
Zororo remhuri idzi pamwe chete uye Jones uyo ane chikamu chouridzi chinosvika 40 muzana mukambani inobura zvirongwa zvepaterevhizheni yeBaldwin's TV.
Willoughby achave mumiririri weM&S uye achatsiva Ant McPartlin semubiki wechirongwa cheITV chinonzi Ndine Mukurumbira.
Manheru akapfuura vari pedyo naJones vakati "Hatigoni kutaura chinhu pamusoro penhau dzebhizimusi rake."
Kutaura zvakadzama 'tichibva tapinda murudo'
Aitaura majee pamusoro pekushorwa kwaazoitwa nevezvenhau pamusoro pekutaura mashoko aizotorwa se "asingakodzeri mutungamiriri wenyika" uye nekuva anowirirana nemutungamiriri weNorth Korea.
Sei Purezidhendi Trump vabvuma kusarenda zvakadaro?
“Anotaura nhau achitevedzera” Trump akati.
"Hapana chandasarenda."
Akacherechedza kuti Kim arikuda mumwe musangano wechipiri pashure pekunge musangano wavo wekutanga wakaitirwamuSingapore munaChikumi wakarumbidzwa zvikuru naTrump sedanho rakakosha pakusiya mabasa ekugadzirwa kwezvombo zvenyukiriya muNorth Korea.
Asi hurukuro dzokusiya mabasa ekugadzirwa kwezvombo zvenyukireya dzamira.

Tsunami uye Kudengenyeka kuIndonesia Kwoparadza chitsuva, Kuchiuraya Mazana
Pashure pekudengenyeka kwenyika kwakaitika muLombok, semuenzaniso, masangano akazvimirira ega ekunze akaudzwa kuti rubatsiro rwavo rwaisadiwa.
Kunyange zvazvo vagari vanokwana 10 kubva muzana wemuLombok vakange vatamiswa, dambudziko racho harina kuziviswa seraiva guru, izvo zvinodiwa pakutanga kuti rubatsiro runobva kune dzimwe nyika rupiwe.
"Mumamiriro ezvinhu akawanda, zvisinei, vakanga varatidza pachena kuti vakange vasingadi rubatsiro kubva kune dzimwe nyika, saka mamiriro ezvinhu akaoma, Muzvare Sumbung vakadaro.
Nepo sangano rinobatsira vana reSave the Children ririkunganidza chikwata kuti chiende kuPalu, harisati rave nechokwadi kana vashandi vekune dzimwe nyika vachazobvumirwa kushanda imomo.
VaSutopo, vanove mutauririri wesangano rinopa rubatsiro panoitika njodzi, vakati vakuru-vakuru vemuIndonesia vainge vachiongorora mamiriro akaita zvinhu muPalu kuti vaone kuti masangano ekunze angabvumidzwa here kuti ape rubatsiro.
Pachitariswa kudengenyeka kwenyika kunogara kuchiitika muIndonesia, nyika iyi inoramba iine dambudziko rekusanyatsogadzirira njodzi dzinoitika dzoga.
Nepo pekufanogara pevanenge vawirwa netsunami kwakavakwa muAceh, zvivakwa izvi hazvivanzoonekwi mune dzimwe nzvimbo dziri mumhenderekedzo.
Kushayikwa kwegadziriro yesairini inorira ichipa vanhu chenjedzo muPalu, kunyange hazvo nzira yekupa chenjedzo yakange yaitwa, kungangodarowo kwakawedzeresa kufa kwevanhu.
Kunyange munguva dzakanyanyonakisa, kushanya muzvitsuva zvakawanda zvemuIndonesia kunonetsa.
Njodzi dzinongoitika dzoga dzinoita kuti hurongwa hwemafambiro huwedzere kuoma.
Ngarava yepachipatara yainge yakamira muLombok kuitira kurapwa kwevakakuvadzwa pakudengenyeka kwenyika iri kuenda kuPalu, asi inogona kutora mazuva angada kusvika matatu kuti isvike panzvimbo yakaitikira njodzi.
Mutungamiriri wenyika Joko Widodo akapa vimbiso yekuti kugadzirwa kwezvivakwa zvemuIndonesia ndicho chinangwa chake chikuru paaitsvaka rutsigiro musarudzo, uye akashandisa chikamu chikuru chemari mukugadzirwa kwemigwagwa nenjanji.
Asi kuperevedza kwemari kurikushungurudza hurumende yaVaJoko panguva apo vari kutsvaka rutsigiro rwekuti vasarudzwezve mugore rinotevera.

Tarisa: Mutambi weLiverpool anonzi Daniel Sturridge anokanda chibodzwa chekuenzaniosa vachitamba ne. Chelsea
Daniel Sturridge oponesa Liverpool kubva pakukundwa paMutambo weZvikwata Zvikuru wePremier League apo vaitamba neChelsea nekukanda kwaakaita chibodzwa mumaminitsi 89 bhora ratanga musi weMugovera muStamford Bridge iri muLondon.
Sturridge akapasirwa bhora naXherdan Shaqiri ari chinhambwe chinosvika nhanho 30 kubva kugedhi reChelsea apo chikwata chake chainge chakakundwa nezvibodzwa1-0.
Akaendesa bhora kugumbo rake rekuruboshwe asti akanda bara nechemukona chaimo mebango regedhi.
Bara iri rakasimudzwa nechepamusoro pebhokisi repagedhi richienda nechekurudyi kwekona yemaneti.
Bhora rakabva radonhera nechepamusoro paKepa Arrizabalaga uyo aikwakuka achiedza kuribata ndokudonhera mumaneti.
"Kwange kungori kuedza kupinda panzvimbo iyoyo, kuenda pabhora uye vatambi vanenge Shaq vanongotambira nechemberi pese pavanogona, saka ndakangoedza kuzvipa nguva sezvinobvira," akadaro Sturridge achitaura neLiverpoolFC.com.
"Ndakaona Kante achiuya ndichibva ndarova bhora kamwe-kamwe ndisina kufunga zvakawanda nezvazvo ndakabva ndangorova bara."
Chelsea yaitungamira nezvibodzwa 1-0 panguva yekumbozorora mushure mekuwana chibodzwa muminiti yechi25 kubva kushasha yebhora yekuBelgium inonzi Eden Hazard.
Mutambi uyu wekumberi we-The Blues akadzorera bhora kuna Mateo Kovacic pamutambo iwoyo, asati apinda nechepakatikati penhandare ndokumhanya akananga kugedhi reLiverpool.
Kovacic akakurumidza kupasira bhora ndokumhanya achipinda nechepakati penhandare.
Akabva akanda bhora rakanakanaka , richinotambirwa naHazard nechemubhokisi.
Hazard akamhanya kupfuura vatambi vekumashure achipedzisira ave kune rimwe bango regedhi ndokunwisa achikava bara negumbo rake reruboshwe pamberi pa Alisson Becker mubati weLiverpool.
Liverpool ichatamba neNapoli mumitambo yechikwata-zvikwata zveChampions League na3 masikati nemusi weChitatu paStadio San Paolo irimuNaples, Italy.
Chelsea ichasangana neVideoton muMutambo yeUEFA Europa na3 masikati nemusi weChina muLondon.

Uwandu hwevanhu vafa muIndonesia nekuda kwekudengenyeka kwenyika uye tsunami hwakwira kusvika pa832, ajenzi inoona nezvenjodzi munyika iyi yakadaro nemusi weSvondo mangwanani.

Mapurisa osunga murume, ane makore 32, uyo ari kufungidzirwa kuti ndiye akauraya mukadzi nekumubaya kusvika afa
Ongororo yekuponda yakatangwa mushure mekuonekwa kwemutumbi wemudzimai muBirkenhead, Merseyside mangwanani ano.
Mudzimai uyu ane makore 44 akawanikwa nenguva dza7:55 mangwanani aine zvironda zvekubayiwa paGrayson Mews mumugwagwa waJohn Street, uyewo murume ane makore 32 anosungwa achifungidzirwa kuti ndiye akauraya.
Mapurisa akurudzira vanhu vemunharaunda iyi vakaona kana kunzwa chero chii zvacho kuti vamhan’are.
Mukuru-mukuru weVanoferefeta nyaya Brian O'Hagan akati: 'Ongororo iyi ichiri padanho rekutanga asi ndinokumbira kune vose vaive pedyo nemugwagwa unonzi John Street uri muBirkenhead vakaona chero kunzwa chii zvacho chavasina kunzwisisa kuti vatibate.
Ndinokumbirawo kuna ani zvake, zvikuru sei vatyairi vematekisi, vanogona kunge vakatora mifananidzo yezvakaitika vachishandisa makamera edzimota kuti vatibate sezvo vanogona kunge vaine mashoko anokosha muongororo yatiri kuita.'
Mutauriri wemapurisa atsinhira kuti mukadzi ane mutumbi wakaonekwa mugari wemuBirkenhead uye akawanikwa ari munechimwe chivakwa.
Masikati ano veushamwari vanofunga kuti vanoziva mukadzi uyu vasvikawo panzvimbo iyi kuti vabvunze mibvunzo pamusoro pekuti awanikwa kupi mangwanani ano.
Ongororo dzichiri kuenderera mberi sezvo mapurisa azivisa kuti achiri mubishi rekuti vataurire hama yepedyo yemufi.
Mutyairi wetekisi anogara muGrayson Mews ange ari kuedza kudzokera mufurati rake asi audzwa nemapurisa kuti hapana ari kubvumirwa kubuda kana kupinda muchiwakwa ichi.
Akashaya neremuromo paakaona zvakange zvaitika.
Vagari vepo varikuudzwa kuti zvichatora maawa akawanda kuti vazobvumidzwa kupindazve.
Mumwe mupurisa akanzwikwa achitaura kuti nzvimbo yacho yose yakuonekwa senzvimbo yakaparirwa mhosva.
Mumwe mukadzi asvika panzvimbo yacho aine misodzi pamatama.
Airamba achingoti 'inga zvakaoma'.
Nenguva dza2 masikati motokari mbiri dzemapurisa dzange dzave mukati uye imwe iri nechokunze.
Mapurisa akati wanderi akange akamira nechemukati vachiongorora zvikamu-kamu zvefurati iyi.

Mufananidzo wemuCromwell weParamende vakawa chirangaridzo chazvino-zvino “pakunyorwa patsva kwenhoroondo”
Kurambidzwa kwacho kuchava ruramisiro mune zvetsanangudzo nekuda kwekuparadzwa kwayo kwakafanana nekunoitwa nema-Taliban pazvinhu zvechinyakare uye zvechitendero zveEngland zvakaitwa nevateveri vechikwata chevaratidziri chePuritan.
Asi vagari vemuCromwell vakatsanangudza maonero aVaCrick “seasina musoro” uye “ekuedza kunyorazve nhoroondo.”
John Goldsmith, uyo anove sachigaro weVagari wemuCromwell, akati: "Zvange zvisingadzivisiki pahurukuro dziripo dziri maererano nekubviswa kwemifananidzo kuti chimutumbi chaOliver Cromwell chiri nechekunze kwemuzinda weWestminster chirege kutaurwa nezvacho.
Kuparadza zvinhu zvenhoroondo kwakaitwa nehondo dzeEngland hakuna kurairwa kana kuitwa naCromwell.
Zvichida Cromwell uyo ari kunzi ndiye ane mhosva anogona kufira mhosva yatateguru vake Thomas avo vakararama muzana remakore rapfuura.
kumiririra kukuru kwakaitwa neanoremekedzwa William Hamo Thorneycroft neCromwell huchapupu hwemuzana remakore rechi19 uye chikamu chenhoroondo chemunhu uyo vanhu vakawanda vanofunga kuti anokodzera kuyeukwa.
VaGoldsmith vakaudza The Sunday Telegraph kuti: "Cromwell anoonekwa nevazhinji, zvikuru sei mukupera kwezana remakore rechi19 kupfuura zvazvingava nhasi, semudziviriri weparamende kubva kune vanopikisa, panhau yake yemafambisirwo enhau dzoumambo.
Kuti kumiririra kwake kwainge kwakarurama here kana kuti kwete inhau yakabvira kare ichinetsa.
Zviri pachena ndezvekuti kunetsana kwakaitika nechepakati pemazana 17 emakore apfuura kwakaumba budiriro yavepo parizvino yechinyika yedu, uye Cromwell munhu anoonekwa seaimiririra rimwe divi renhau yacho.
Zvaakakwanisa kuita seMudziwiriri waShe kwakakodzera kuti kupembererwe uye kurangarirwe."
Nguruve Yoruma Ndokuuraya Murimi WekuChina
Mumwe murimi akarumwa ndokuuraiwa nenguruve mumusika wekuchambe kwakadziwa kumadokero muChina, mukuwirirana nenhau dzemunzvimbomo.
Murume uyu, akangozivikanwa nezita redzinza rake rokuti "Yuan," akawanikwa akafa aine ronda rekubvamburwa,akazara neropa pedyo nemumwe musika uri muLiupanshui mupurovhinzi yeGuizhou, pepanhau reSouth China Morning Post rakadaro nemusi weSvondo.
Murimi wenguruve anogadziririra kubaya nguruve dzake mishonga padzinochengeterwa musi wa 30 Chivabvu, gore ra2005 muXining iri muPurovhinzi yeQinghai, iri muChina.
Zvirikunzi akange ashanya nemuzukuru wake kubva mupurovhinzi yakavakidzana navo yeYunnan nemusi weChitatu kuti vanotengesa nguruve 15 kumusika.
Mangwanani akatevera acho, muzukuru wake akamuona akafa, ndokucherechedza kuti dhoo redanga renguruve riri pedyo navo rainge rakavhurika.
Akati mudanga maiwe nenguruve hono hombe yainge iine ropa pamuromo wayo.
Ongororo yakadzama yakasimbisira kuti nguruve ine huremu hwemapaunzi 550 ndiyo yakange yaruma murimi uyu ndokumuuraya, mukuwirirana neripoti yakabuda.
"Makumbo asekuru vangu ainge akazara neropa uye akabvamburwa-bvamburwa," akadaro muzukuru wacho uyo ane zita redzinza rekuti "Wu," ,mukuwirirana nemashoko ake akataurwa neGuiyang Evening News.
Vhidhiyo yakabuda pamakamera yakaratidza Yuan achipinda mumusika nenguva dza 4.40 mangwanani nemusi weChina kuti anopa zvekudya nguruve dzake.
Mutumbi wake wakazowanikwa gare-gare mushure meawa.
Mhuka iyi yakauraya Yuan yakange isiri yake kana muzukuru wake.
Mukuru wemusika akaudza weEvening News kuti nguruve iyi yainge yavharirwa kwayo yega kuitira kuti isarumezve mumwe munhu, panguva apo mapurisa aiunganidza mashoko ehumbowo panzvimbo yacho.
Mhuri yaYuan nevakuru-vakuru vemusika varikunzi varikuita hurukuro yekuripa kufa kwake.
Kunyange zvazvo zvisingawanzoitika, nhau dzekurumwa kwevanhu nenguruve dzakamboitika kare.
Mugore ra2016, imwe nguruve yakaruma mukadzi nemurume wake papurazi ravo riri muMassachusetts, zvichisiya murume wacho akuwara zvikuru.
Makore gumi izvi zvisati zvaitika, nguruve ine huremu hwemapaunzi 650 yakadzvanyidzira umwe murimi wechiWelsh kutarakita yake kusvika mukadzi wake azotyisidzira mhuka yacho.
Mushure mekunge mumwe murimi wekuOregon adyiwa nenguruve dzake mugore ra2012, mumwe murimi wekuManitoba akaudza weCBC News kuti nguruve hadziwanzoita hasha asi kuravidza ropa ndiko kunogona "kudzituma."
"Dzinenge dzirikutotamba.
Dzakangofanana nevana, dzinoda kuziva zvirikuitika ... hadzipo pakukukuvadza.
Unongofanira kudzibata nekuziva," akadaro.
Dutu Mupengo reRosa rounza mvura zhinji kuchamhembe kwakadziva kumavirira kweUS
Sekufungidzira kwazviri kuitwa,Dutu Mupengo iri ririkushaya simba sezvarinopfuura nemumvura dzinotonhora dzekumahombekombe ekumaodzanyemba kweMexico.
Zvisinei, Dutu Mupengo iri reRosa richaunza mafashamo munzvimbo dzekumaodzanyemba eMexico uye kuchamhembe kwakadziva kumawirira kweU.S mumazuva mashoma arikutevera.
Dutu Mupengo reRosa rine mhepo dzinomhanya pamwero we85 mph, muchikamu 1 cheDutu Mupengo, panguva dza5 mangwanani. Nguva dzekumaodzanyemba nemusi weSvondo, uye yainge iri mamaira 385 nechekumawirira kwakadziwa kumabvazuva kwePunta Eugenia, iri muMexico.
Dutu Mupengo iri reRosa ririkutarisirwa kufamba richienda nechekumusoro nemusi weSvondo.
Zvichakadaro, dhipuresheni irikutanga kuitika pamusoro penyanza yePacific uye ichifamba nechekumaodzanyemba pedyo ne mahombekombe ekuchamhembe ekuU.S. Sezvo Dutu Mupengo reRosa rinosvika kuBaja California peninsula nemusi weMuvhuro sedutu rotanga kuunza mwando wakasimba nechekumusoro kupinda munzvimbo iri kumawirira kwakadziwa kuchamhembe kweU.S.
Dutu Mupengo reRosa richaunza mvura inosvika mainji10 mune dzimwe nzvimbo muMexico.
Zvadaro, mwando uyu uri mudutu sezvaunosvika panzvimbo isina mhepo yakawanda uchakonzera mvura yakasimba kunzvimbo iri kumawirira kwakadziwa kuchamhembe mumazuva anotevera.
Munzvimbo ino, huwandu hwemvura hunosvika mainji 1 kusvika ku 4 huchakonzera mafashamo, kuwondomoka kwemavhinga kunyangewo nemadhaka mugwenga.
Mwando uri mudutu uchakonzera huwandu hwemvura kuti husvike pamainji 2 kusvika ku 3 paawa panzvimbo, zvikuru sei munzvimbo dzirinechekumaodzanyemba kweNevada uye Arizona.
Mvura inosvika kumainji 2 kusvika ku4 irikutarisirwa kunaya munzvimbo dzekumaodzanyemba kwakadziwa kumadokero kunyanya-nyanya muArizona.
Mafashamo anokwanisa kuitika tichitarisa kuderera kwemamiriro ekunze nekuda kwekunaya kuri kuita mvura ichisiya dzimwe nzvimbo.
Kunenge kuri kusachenjera kupinda mugwenga uchifamba netsoka tichitarisa njodzi inogona kukonzerwa nekunaya kwemvura ine mhepo.
Mvura ine simba inogona kukonzera kuti tumigero tupupume nemvura senzizi dzakakura uye mvura ine mabhanan’ana ichikonzera kuvhuvhuta kwemhepo uye kusimudza guruva munzvimbomo.
Mhepo isina mwando irikuuya ichaunza mvura ine simba munzvimbo dzekumaodzanyemba kwemahombekombe eCalifornia.
Mvura ingangodarika chikamu cheinji inogona kunaya, izvo zvinogona kukonzera mavhinga madiki kuti ayeredzwe uye kuita kuti migwagwa itsvedze.
Iyi ndiyo inenge iri mvura yekutanga kunaya mudunhu iri mumwaka wavo wekunaya.
Mvura inenge ichipfunha-pfunha munzvimbo dzakasiyana-siyana ichazotanga kusvika muArizona nechekunodoka kwemusi weSvondo nemangwanani emusi weMuvhuro, mvura yacho isati yanyanyopararira nechekunodoka kwemusi weMuvhuro neChipiri.
Mvura ine simba ichapararira kumativi ose mana nemusi weChipiri kusvika Chitatu.
Mwedzi waGumiguru uchava nekupisa kwakanyanya muU.S. mose sezvo nyanza yeArctic ichatanga kutonhora, asi nzvimbo dzinopisa dzicharamba dzichidziya.
Dzimwe nguva izvi zvinokonzera kuchinja kwekamwe-kamwe mumapisiro munzvimbo dziri pedyo nepedyo.
Pane muenzaniso mukuru wekuchinja kwekamwe-kamwe mumapisiro ekunze munzvimbo dziri nechepakati-kati peU.S. nemusi weSvondo.
Pane musiyano wemwero wekupisa wemadhigirii angongosvika 20 pakati peGuta reKansas, Missouri, uye Omaha, Nebraska, uyezve pakati peSt. Louis neDes Moines, Iowa.
Mumazuva mashoma ari kutevera, kudziya kunenge kuchikonzerwa nemwaka wekupisa unenge uchiswedera kuchawedzera kusimba nekukura zvakare.
Nzvimbo zhinji dziri nechepakati-pakati uye kumabvazuva kweU.S. dziri kutarisirwa kuti dzichatanga nekudziya mumwedzi waGumiguru nemwero wekupisa ungangosvika kumadhigirii 80 kubva Kumapani Ekumaodzanyemba kusvika kuChamhembe kwakadziva kumabvazuva.
Guta reNew York City rinogona kusvika madhigirii 80 nemusi weChipiri, unova mwero mwero wekupisa ungangosvika madhidirii 10 kupfuura zvakajairika.
Zvatirikutarisira munguva refu iri mberi nezvemamiriro ekunze zvinoratidza kuti pane mukana wekuva nemwero wekupisa unoti pfuurei wakajairika nechekumabvazuva kweU.S. kusvika nechepakati pemwedzi waGumiguru.
Vanhu vanodarika mamiriyoni 20 vakaona kutongwa kwaBrett Kavanaugh
Nemusi weChina, vanhu vanodarika mamiriyoni 20 vakaona panhepfenyuro dzeterevhizheni nhanhatu huchapupu hwakasimba huchipihwa naBrett Kavanaugh uyo akasarudzwa neDare Repamusoro-soro uyewo mudzimai anonzi Christine Blasey Ford uyo aimupomera nezve kumbunyikidzwa mune zvepabonde uko kunonzi kwakaitika mumakore ekuma 1980.
Zvichakadaro, kusawirirana mune zvematongerwo enyika kuchingoripo, nevatepfenyuri vachidimburira hurongwa hwenguva dzose hwemusi weChishanu hwekuchinja kunongoitwa paminiti yekupedzisira: chibvumirano chakatangwa naArizona Sen. Jeff Flake kuitira kuti weFBI vaite ongororo yevhiki rimwe yezviri kupomerwa.
Ford akaudza komiti yeDare reSeneti redzimhosva kuti ane chokwadi chakazara chekuti Kavanaugh akamubata akadhakwa ndokuedza kubvisa mbatya dzake vari pamutambo wepachikoro wekufara.
Kavanaugh, achipa huchapupu hunobata moyo, akati ane chokwadi chakazara chekuti hapana zvakadaro zvakaitika.
Zvingangodaro kuti vanhu vanopfuura mamiriyoni 20.4 sezvakashumwa neNielsen nemusi weChishanu wakazviona.
Kambani iyi yange iri kuwerenga wangangodaro vakaona paCBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, Fox News Channel uye MSNBC.
Uwandu hwevakaona pane dzimwewo nhepfenyuro dzakaburitsa, dzakadai sePBS, C-SPAN uye Fox Business Network hauna kukurumidza kuwanikwa.
Uye Nielsen inowanzove nedambudziko pakuhwerengedza uwandu hwevanhu vanenge vaonera vari mumahofisi avo.
Kuti tinyatsojekerwa, uhwu huwandu hwevateereri hwakafanana nehwevanhu vanouya kunoona mutambo webhora kana Mhemberero dzeKugirajuweta.
Kana iri Fox News Channel, iyo ine vakurukuri vayo vakakokwa vaitsigira zvikuru kusarudzwa kwaKavanaugh, yaive pamusoro pedzimwe nhepfenyuro iine vaiona vaisvika mamiriyoni 5.69, yakadaro Nielsen.
ABC ndiyo yaive pechipiri iine vaoni vanosvika mamiriyoni 3.26.
CBS yaive nemamiriyoni 3.1, NBC yaive nemamiriyoni 2.94, MSNBC yaive nemamiriyoni 2.89 uye CNN yaive nemamiriyoni 2.52, yakadaro Nielsen.
Chido chekuda kuziva zvakaitika chakaramba chakakura pashure pedare.
Flake aive munhu ainyanyotariswa pachinoitika chemusi weChishanu.
Mushure mekunge wekuhofisi yemaRepublican apa mashoko ekuti waizovhota vachitsigira Kavanaugh, akaonekwa pamakamera eCNN uye CBS nemusi weChishanu mangwanani achitukwa nevaratidziri sezvaaiedza kukwira mukeji yekuendesa pamakamuri emudenga mechivakwa kuti asvike kwaitongerwa nyaya neveKomiti Yedzimhosva.
Akamira akatarisa pasi kwemaminetsi akawanda sezvaainyadziswa, achionekwa ipapo-ipapo paterevhizheni yeCNN.
"Ndakamira pano chaipo pamberi pako," mumwe mukadzi akadaro.
"Uri kufunga kuti ari kutaura chokwadi here kunyika?
Akaudzwa kuti, "une simba panguva apo vakadzi vazhinji vasina simba.""
Flake akati hofisi yake yainge yaburitsa mashoko ekuti, keji yekuendesa mudenga isati yavhara, anenge atowe nezvakawanda zvekutaura kukomiti yedare .
Vatepfenyuri venhepfenyuro dzakawanda vaiburitsa pamhepo zvaiitika mumaawa akazotevera, panguva apo Komiti yeDare reDzimhosva yaida kuvhota kuti Kavanaugh asarudzwezve kuve nhengo yakazara yeseneti .
Asi Flake akati aizoita izvozvo chete kana anyatsonzwisisa kuti weFBI waizoita ongororo yake kwevhiki raizotevera, izvo zvaikurudzirwa nevashoma vebato remaDemocrats .
Flake akakurudzirwa neimwe nzira nehurukuro dzaakaita neshamwari yake ,inonzi Sen. Chris Coons webato reDemocratic.
Mushure mekukurukura naCoons uye nedzimwe nhengo dzeseneti gare-gare, Flake akazoita chisarudzo chake.
Chisarudzo chaFlake chaive nesimba, nekuda kwekuti zvange zvave pachena kuti vebato remaRepublicans vaisazovhota vachitsigira Kavanaugh ongororo dzisati dzaitwa.
Mutungamiri wenyika Trump akaraira FBI kuti iite ongororo panhau yaKavanaugh.
Mukuru weMakurukota muBritain anopomera vatsoropodzi kuti 'varikutamba munezvematongerwo enyika' nezveBrexit
Mukuru weMakurukota Theresa May akapa mhosva vashori veurongwa hwake hwekubuda muEuropean Union kuti “varikutamba nezvematongerwo enyika” neramangwana renyika yeBritain uye kushora zvido zvenyika panguva apo vaibvunzurudzwa neveSunday Times newspaper.
Mukuru weMakurukota muBritain Theresa May anosvika paMusangano weBato reConservative muBirmingham, iri muBritain, nemusi waGunyana 29, gore ra2018.
Mune imwe hurukuro iri pedyo nemufananidzo wake uri nechemberi kwepeji yekutanga yepepanhau, aimbova gurukota rake renyaya dzekunze Boris Johnson akasimbisira kutsoropodza kwaaita urongwa hwake hweBrexit, achiti maonero ekuti Britain neEU dzitorerane mitero ainge ”asina musoro zvachose."
Kupfura kwakaitika muWayde Sims: Mapurisa osunga Dyteon Simpson uyo ari kufungidzirwa kuti ndiye akakonzera rufu rwemutambi weLSU
Mapurisa asunga munhu ari kufungidzirwa kuti ndiye akapfura ndokuuraya Wayde Sims, mutambi wemutambo webhora remaoko ane makore 20 muLSU.
Dyteon Simpson, uyo ane makore 20, asungwa ndokuiswa mujeri pamhosva huru yekuponda, Dhipatimendi remaPurisa reBaton Rouge radaro.
Vakuru-vakuru vaburitsa vhidhiyo yekunetsana kwakaitika pakati paSims naSimpson, uye mapurisa anoti Sims akarasikirwa nemagirazi ake pakurwisana uku.
Mapurisa akawana magirazi aya kubva panzvimbo iyi uye vanoti vaona kuti Simpson ndiye aishandisa magirazi aya pahumboo hweDNA, WAFB iyo yakabatana neCBS inodaro.
Pashure pekubvunzurudza Simpson, mapurisa anoti ari kubvuma kuti ndiye akapfura ndokuuraya Wayde.
Mari yake yekuti atongerwe ari kunze inosvika $350,000, Gweta rakadaro.
Hofisi yeKuongorora mafiro emunhu yeEast Baton Rouge Parish yakaburitsa mashoko ekutanga nemusi weChishanu, ichiti chironda chekupfurwa mumusoro kusvika kuhuro nepfuti ndicho chakaita kuti munhu afe.
Chikamu ichi chiri kurumbidza Mapurisa ekuongorora nekubata nhubu eLouisiana State Police, mapurisa anoita ongororo dzemhosva mumarabhoratari, mapurisa eSouthern University uye vagari vemunzvimbo nekubatsira kwavakaita pakuitwa kweongororo yakazoguma nekusungwa kweakapara mhosva.
Mukuru-mukuru wezvekumhanya weLSU, Joe Alleva akatenda wezvemutemo wemunzvimbomo “nehuchenjeri hwavo uye kutsvaka ruramisiro."
Sims ange ave nemakore 20.
Mutambi uyu ange akareba 6-foot-6 achitambira mberi akakurira muBaton Rouge, umo baba vake, Wayne, vakatambirawo chikwata cheLSU.
Akaita zvibodzwa 5.6 uye kusevha kanokwana ka2.6 pamutambo mumwe nemumwe mumwaka wakapfuura.
Nemusi weChishanu, kochi weLSU Will Wade akati chikwata “charwadziwa zvikuru” uye “chavhundutswa” nerufu rwaWayde.
"Izvi ndizvo zvinhu zvaunogara uchinetseka nazvo nguva nenguva," Wade akadaro.
Kuputika kwegomo komwaya madota muGuta reMexico
Kumwayiwa kwemadota kubva mukuputika kwegomo rePopocatepetl kwasvika kunzvimbo dzekuchamhembe eguta guru reMexico.
Bato rinoona nezvekudzivirirwa kwenjodzi munyika reNational Center for Disaster Prevention rakapa nyevero kuvagari wemuMexico nemusi weMugovera kuti vave kure nenzvimbo iri kuputika pashure pekunge chiitiko ichi chatanga nechepakati pegomo ndokuburitsa magasi anokwana 183 nemadota kwemaawa 24.
Bato iri range riri kuongorora ruzha nekudengenyeka kwakawanda.
Mifananidzo kubva panowanikwa mashoko everuzhinji iri kuratidza magirazi edzimota akavharwa nemadota munzvimbo dziri pedyo neGuta reMexico rakadai seXochimilco.
Nyanzvi dzinoona nezvepasi pevhu dzakacherechedza kuvedzera kwezvaiitika panzvimbo yaiputika iri mamayera 45 (makiromita 72) kuchamhembe kwakadziva kumabvazuva kweguta kubvira panguva apo kudengenyeka kwakakura mamaginichudhi 7.1 kwakaitika nechepakati peguta reMexico munaGunyana gore ra2017.
Kuputika kunozivikanwa se"Don Goyo" kwakabvira kare kuripo kubvira muna1994.
Mapurisa onetsana nevatsigiriri veCatalan pamberi pemhemberero yezororo rerusununguko
Vanhu vanokwana vatanhatu vakasungwa muBarcelona nemusi weMugovera pashure pekunge varatidziri vanotsigira rusununguko vanetsana nemapurisa anodzora mhirizhonga, sezvo vanosvika zviuru vakabatana pakuratidzira kwekupikisa kucherechedza mhemberero yekutanga yekubvisa vhoti yeCatalonia yekupikisa kupawo vamwe masimba ekutonga.
Boka revaratidziri vakapfeka zvinovhara kumeso vaidziviswa nemapurisa vakatanga kutema mapurisa nemazai uye kuwamwaya pendi, zvichikonzera gore yehuruva mumigwagwa iyo inowanzoitwa neboka revashanyi.
Makakatanwa akaitikazve pave paya zuva iroro apo mapurisa akashandisa zvamboko zvavo kudzivisa kurwisana uku.
Kwemaawa akawanda zvikuru mapoka anotsigira rusununguko aideedzera achiti "Hazvikanganwiki, hapana ruregerero" vachipikisana nevaratidziri vanotsigira kubatana avo vaideedzera vachiti, "Spain Ngairambe iripo."
Vanhu vanokwana gumi nevana vakarapwa pashure pekukuvadzwa zvisina kunyanya kukura mukurwisana uku, pepanhau remunzvimbo umu rakadaro.
Kusawirirana kwakaramba kwakakura munzvimbo iyi ine vanhu vanoda zverusununguko papera gore mushure mekunge sarudzo yakaitwa muna Gumiguri 1 yakanzi haisi pamutemo muMadrid asi ichikosheswa nevatsigiri weCatalans.
Wavhoti vakatsigira zvine mutsindo kuti wave wakasununguka, kunyange zvazvo wakabuda kunovhota waive vashoma kudivi revaya vaipikisa chaizvoizvo kuri kuramba kunovhota.
Mukuwirirana nevakuru-vakuru wemuCatalan vanhu vanoda kusvika 1000 wakakuvadzwa gore rapera pashure pekunge mapurisa aedza kumisa kuvhota kwange kuri kuitika munzvimbo dzekuvhotera muzvimbo dzakawanda uku kwakaguma nekurwisana.
Mapoka aitsigira rusununguko akaungana usiku hwose nemusi weChishanu achida kudzivisa kuratidzira mukutsigira mapurisa emunyika.
Kuratidzira kwakazoitika asi kwakamanikidzirwa kuitika neimwewo nzira.
Narcis Termes, uyo ane makore 68, anoita basa rekugadzira zvemagetsi nemudzimai wake akati akanga asisina chivimbo chekuti Catalonia yaizowana rusununguko.
"Gore rakapera takararama nguva yakanakisisa yeupenyu hwedu.
Ndakaona vabereki wangu wachichema nemufaro nekuda kwekukwanisawo kuvhota asi parizvino tadzokerazve kumashure," akadaro.
Pasinei nekusiya padiki-diki wahwinha musarudzo dzemunzvimbo mumwedzi waZvita wapfuura, mabato anotsigira rusununguko akatamburira kuti arambe achikura gore rino uyewo wazhinji wevatungamiriri wavo vanozivikanwa vakazviisa muhutiziro kana kuti vakabatwa vachimirira kutongwa nekuda kwekubatanidzwa kwavo pakuronga sarudzo pamwe nekuzivisa rusununguko pakupedzisira.
Joan Puig, makanika ane makore 42 uyo akarekodha pafoni yake maitikiro ekuratidzira mukutsigira mapurisa, akati makakatanwa aya akanga akazara newezvematongerwo enyika kumativi ose.
"Zviri kuramba zvichingoipa," akadaro.
Nemusi weMugovera, Oriol Junqueras, uyo ari mumwe wevatungamiriri wechipfumbamwe weCatalan uye ari kumirira kutongwa ari mujeri kubvira gore rapfuura, akazivisa kuti achakwikwidza musarudzo dzeParamende yemuEurope gore rinouya.
"Kumira senhengo inokwikwidza musarudzo dzemuEurope ndiyo nzira yakanaka yekuratidza kusawirirana nekudzoka shure mune zvekutonga kwegutsaruzhinji nekutambudzwa kwatiri kutarisana nako kubva kuhurumende yeSpain” akadaro.

Shoti yebhora yaMenga yakaita kuti Livingston iwane zvibodzwa1-0 ichikunda Rangers
Chibodzwa chekutanga chaDolly Menga achitambira Livingston chakaita kuti ikunde
Chikwata cheLivingstone icho chakakwidziridzwa chakakunda chikwata cheRangers zvichiita kuti Steven Gerrard akundwe kechipiri mumitambo18 samaneja wekirabhu yeIbrox.
Shoti yaDolly Menga yakakonzera musiyano sezvo divi raGary Holt rakasvika pakuenzana neHibernian iyo iri pechipiri.
Chikwata chaGerrard charamba chisina kuhwinha pamutambo yekunze yePremiership mumwaka uno uye chichasangana nechikwata chiri kutungamirira cheHearts nemusi weSvondo, icho vari kumashure kwacho nezvibodzwa zvisere.
Izvi zvisati zvaitika, Rangers ichatatsurana neRapid Vienna mumitambo yeEuropa League nemusi weChina.
Livingston, parizvino, iri kuramba ichiwedzera isina kukundwa mumitambo inokwana mitanhatu yayatamba, iina kochi wayo Holt uyo asati akundwa kubvira paakatsiva Kenny Miler mwedzi wakapfuura.
Chikwata cheLivingston chakatambisa mikana yakawanda pachakatamba nevashanyi vasingagoni
Chikwata chaHolt chaifanira kunge chatungamira nechekare panguva yachakazogohwesa, nekusapotsa kwacho gedhi uku kwaionesa nhamo chikwata cheRangers.
Scott Robinson akapinda nebhora asi ndokunonoka kushandisa mukana wake pamberi pegedhi, uyewo Alan Lithgow akarovera bhora kure negedhi pashure pekusangana nebhora remusoro raibva kunaCraig pedyo negedhi.
Chikwata chepamba ichi chaigutsikana nekusiya chikwata cheRangers chichitambira nechekudivi kwavo, vachiziva havo kuti vaizoshungurudza vashanyi ava nemabhora emugadzikirwa.
Uye ndiyo nzira iyo chibodzwa chakakosha chakaitika nayo.
Rangers yakakonzeresa bhora remugadzikirwa uye Livingston yakabva yavhurira, Declan Gallagher uye Robinson vachipasirana ndokubikira Menga mukana, uyo akatambira bhora ndokugohwesa kubva nechepakati pebhokisi.
Panguva iyoyo, Rangers ndiyo yaitungamira pakugara nebhora asi yakanetseka kuwana mukana wekupoya watambi wekumashure uye gori Liam Kelly haana kumbove nedambudziko,
Matambiro aya karamba akangodaro kusvika pachikamu chechipiri, kunyange zvazvo Alfredo Morelos akakwanisa kudzivisa Kelly uyo aida kugohwesa.
Scott Pittman yakarambirwa mukana netsoka dzagori Allan McGregor uye Lithgow akarovera kudivi bhora remugadzikirwa rechikwata chake cheLivingston.
Mabhora akaramba achikandwa pedyo nemubhokis reLivingston uye airamba achibviswa, nepo zvikumbiro zviviri zvemugadzikirwa wepena-mushure mekunge kumaka kwaHalkett pane ange achangobva kupinzwa Glenn Middleton, uye chimwe chikumbiro mushure mekunge paine abata bhora - zvose zvakarambwa.
'Zvinodadisa' kubva kuLivingston - ongororo
Alasdair Lamont weBBC anobva kuScotland ari paTony Macaroni Arena
Kutamba uye kukunda kunodadisa kweLivingston.
Mumaonero emunhu, watamba zvakanaka, wachiramba wachipfuura zvaitarisirwa mukubudirira kwavo.
Matambiro avo nevanhu wavainavo zvachinja zvishona kubvira pavakadzoka mumutambo wezvikwata zvepamusoro, asi rumbidzo yakanyanya inofanira kupihwa Holt nenzira yaakabatanidza nayo chikwata ichi kubva paakasvika.
Aive nemagamba akawanda.
Kaputeni Halkett ashanda nesimba, achiita kuti pave nedhifenzi yakarongeka, ukuwo Menga achiita kuti Connor Goldson naoe Worrall warambe vachingomhanya.

Matambiro avo pakupedzisira ange aderera- kanongova kamwe chete kavazama kupinda mugedhi rechikwata chepamba - uye chimwe chinhu chinofanira kuita kuti chikwata cheRangers chifunge nezvazvo, avo vari pakati-nepakati pezvimwe zvikwata.
Erdogan ogashirwa zvakasiya muCologne
Pange paine kunyemwerera uye mafaro nemusi weMugovera (Gunyana 29) apo vatungamiriri weTurkey uye Germany wakasangana kuti vadye kudya kwemangwanani muBerlin.
Izuva rekupedzisira rekushanya kunemutauro kuGermany kweMutungamiriri wenyika Erdogan - uko kwakananga kugadzirisa ukama pakati penyika dzinotsigira NATO.
Vakatadza kuwirirano pamusoro pekodzero dzevanhu, rusununguko mune zvenhau uye kupinda kweTurkey muEU.
Erdogan akazonanga kuCologne kuti anovhura zviri pamutemo temberi itsva.
Guta iri musha wevanhu vazhinji vekuTurkey vanogara kunze kwenyika yavo.
Mapurisa avharira vanhu 25,000 kuti vasaungana pamberi petemberi nekuda kwechikonzero chechengeteko, asi vazhinji vevatsigiri vaungana nechepedyo kuti vaone mutungamiri wavo wenyika.
Mazana evaratidziri ayo aisatsigira Erdogan - vazhinji wacho werudzi rwechiKurdish - vakaitawo kuti inzwi ravo rinzwike, vachishora chaizvo mitemo yaErdogan pamwe chete nechisarudzo chakaitwa nehurumende yeGerman chekumubvumidza kupinda munyika.
Kuratidzira uku kwemapoka maviri kunoratidza kupatsanuka kwakaita maonerwo anoitwa mushanyi uyo anoonekwa segamba nevamwe vagari vanobva kuTurkey ukuwo achishorwa nevamwe sembimbindoga.
Tsaona mumugwagwa wemuDeptford: Muchovhi webhasikoro anofa mushure mekuroverana nemotokari
Muchovhi webhasikoro afa mushure mekuroverana nemotokari muLondon.
Kuroverana uku kwakaitika pedyo nepanoparadzana mugwagwa weBestwood nemugwagwa weEvelyn, mugwagwa unoshandiswa zvikuru muDeptford,nechekumabvazuva kwakadziva kuchamhembe kweguta, nenguva dza10:15 BST.
Mutyairi wemotokari akamira uye vanopa rubatsiro vakabva vatanga kupa rubatsiro, asi murume wacho akabva afira ipapo.
Kuroverana uku kwaitika mushure memwedzi yakati apo mumwewo muchovhi webhasikoro akafa mushure mekurohwa nemota iyo isina kumira muMugwagwa weChilders, inenge mayera kubva pakaitikira njodzi iyi nemusi weMugovera.

Pane migwagwa yakavharwa uye kuendeswa nerimwe divi kwemabhazi uye vanofamba nemota vanzi vasadarika nemunzvimbo iyi.
Jeri reLong Lartin: Mapurisa matanhatu epajeri okuvara mubongozozo
Mapurisa matanhatu epajeri vakakuvara mubongozozo rakaitika pane rimwe jeri revarume rinochengetedzwa zvikuru, akadaro mumwe mupurisa wepajeri.
Bongozozo iri rakatanga paHMP Long Lartin muWorcestershire nenguva dzinenge dza09:30 BST nemusi wesvondo uye richiri kuenderera.
Nyanzvi dzemapurisa"dzeTornado" dzakaunzwa kuti dzipedze bongozozo racho, iro ririkubatanidza vasungwa vasere uye ririkuitika kurutivi rwumwe chete.
Mapurisa aya akarapwa zvironda zvidiki zvekumeso kwavo panzvimbo iyi.
Mutauriri weJeri akati: " Nyanzvi dzakanyatsodzidziswa basa dzinoshanda pajeri dzakatumirwa kuti dzimise bongozozo iri ririkuenderera mberi paHMP Long Lartin.
Vashandi wepajeri vatanhatu vakarapwa zvironda zvekukuwara.
Hatitenderi kurwisana mumajeri edu, uye zviri pachena kuti waya vose varikubatanidzwa vachamhan’arirwa kumapurisa uye vanogona kupedza nguva yakakura vakavharirwa."
HMP Long Lartin ine vasungwa vanopfuura 500, kusanganisira vamwe vakapara mhosva dzakaipisisa munyika.
Muna Chikumi zvakataurwa kuti gavhena wemajeri akarapwawo kuchipatara mushure mekukuvadzwa nemumwe musungwa.
Uye muna Gumiguru gore rakapfuura chikwata chemapurisa anodzivisa bongozozo akadaidzwa kujeri kuti amise bongozozo rakaipisisa iro vashandi vepajeri vakatemwa nemabhora esinuka.
Dutumupengo reRosa Rotyisidzira Kurova Phoenix, Las Vegas, Salt Lake City NeMafashamo (Nzvimbo Dzisinganayi Mvura Dzinogona Kubatsirika)
Hazviwanzoitiki kuti dutumupengo riitike muArizona, asi ndizvo chaizvo zvinogona kuitika svondo rinotevera sezvo zvisaririra zvesimba reDutumuengo reRosa zvichapinda nemuDesert Southwest, zvichiisa njodzi yemafashamo.
Bazu Rinoona neZvemamiriro Ekunze reNyika rakatopa chenjedzo yenjodzi yemafashamo nekuda kweMuvhuro uye Chipiri nechekumadokera kweArizona uye nechekumaodzanyemba uye kumabvazuva kweNavada, kumabvazuva kwakadziva kumaodzanyemba kweCalifonia neUtah, kusanganisira maguta anoti Phoenix,Flagstaff, Las Vegas, uye Salt Lake City.
Dutumupengo reRosa ririkutarisirwa kurova zvakananga muPhoenix nemusi weChipiri, richipinda riine mvura nechekunowira kwezuva kwemusi weMuvhuro.
Bazu Rinoona neZvemamiriro Ekunze reNyika remuPhoenix rakatsinhira padandemutande retwitter kuti "madutumupengo anosvika gumi akaramba achiitika munzvimbo iri mamayera 200 ePhoenix kubvira muna 1950!
Katrina (1967) idutumupengo raive mumamayera 40 kubva pamuganhu weAZ."
Zviratidzo zveBazu Remunyika Rinoona nezveMadutumupengo zvirikuratidza kuti mainji 2 kusvika ku4 emvura ichanaya, uyewo mune dzimwe nzvimbo dzemuMogollon Rim yemuArizona iine mainji 6.
Dzimwewo nzvimbo dzemuDesert Southwest kusanganisira nechepakati peRockies uye Great Basin dzinogona kuwana mvura inosvika mainji 1 kusvika ku2, uyewo nemainji emvura anogona kusvika ku4 nzvimbo nenzvimbo.
Kune avo vasiri munjodzi yemafashamo, mvura ichaunzwa neRosa inogona kuve chikomborero kwavari sezvo dunhu racho risinganayi mvura.
Kunyange zvazvo mafashamo ari nyaya inotemesa musoro, imwe yemvura iyi ichanaya inogona kuve ruyamuro sezvo Southwest iri mumamiriro ezvinhu ekusanaya mvura.
Mukuwirirana neweU.S. Drought Monitor avo vanoona nezvekusanaya kwemvura, zvikamu zvinenge zvinopfuura 40 muzana zveArizona zviri kutarisana nekusanaya kwemvura kukuru, iyo iri pabandiko rechipiri kubva kumusoro," weather.com yakadaro.
Kutanga, mafambiro eDutumupengo reRosa achakonzera kuwondomoka kwenzvimbo dzemuBaja Califonia dzemuMexico.
Dutumupengo reRosa, richine simba redutu nemusi weSvondo mangwanani nemhepo yaivhuvhuta nemwero wokumhanya wemamaira 85 muawa, rave mamayera 385 nechekuchamhembe kwePunta Eugenia, iri muMexico uye richifamba mamayera 12 muawa.
Dutu iri riri kusangana nemvura dzinotonhora dzemuPacific uye zvichiita kuti ripere simba.
Zvakadaro, ririkutarisirwa kuperera muMexico riine simba redutu mumasikati kana manheru emusi weMuvhuro.
Kunaya kwemvura munzvimbo dzakasiyana-siyana dzeMexico kuchange kwakasimba, kuchikonzera njodzi yemafashamo.
"Kunaya kwemvura kunosvika mwero wemainji 3 kusvika ku6 kurikutarisirwa kutangira muBaja Califonia kupinda nechekumaodzanyemba kwakadziwa kumadokero kweSonora, kuine tarisiro yekusvika mwero wemainji 10," weather.com yakadaro.
Dutumupengo reRosa rinobva rafamba richipfuura nechekumaodzanyemba kweMexico sedutu risati rasvika nechepamuganhu weArizona nenguva dzemakuseni semvura, richizosimudzira richipinda nemuArizona uye kuchamhembe kweUtah muusiku hwemusi weChipiri.
"Zvinhu zvikuru zvirikutarisirwa kuunzwa neDutumupengo reRosa imvura ichanaya muBaja California, kuchamhembe kwakadziva kumadokero kweSonora, uye muU.S. NemuDesert Southwest," Bazi rinoona nezvemadutumupengo reNational Hurricane Center rakadaro.
Kunaya uku kurikutarisirwa kuti kungangokonzera njodzi yemafashamo kuvanhu nekuyeredzwa kwemavhinga mumagwenga, uye kuwondomoka kwemadhaka munzvimbo dzakatenuka dzemumakomo.

Mazana ourawa nekudengenyeka kwenyika netsunami muIndonesian, uwandu hwevakafa huchiramba huchiwedzera
Vanhu vangangodarika 384 vakauraiwa, vazhinji vavo vakakukurwa apo masaisai akakura akarova mahombekombe, apo kudengenyeka kukuru netsunami zvakaitika muchitsuwa cheSulawesi chiri muIndonesia, vakuru-vakuru vakadaro nemusi weMugowera.
Mazana evanhu ainge akaungana nekuda kwekupemberera muguta rePalu nemusi weChishanu apo masaisai akareba mamita matanhatu (mafiti 18) akarova mahombekombe kwave kudoka, achikukura kusvika pakuuraya vazhinji uye achiparadza chero chaiwe mugwara rawo.
Tsunami yakatevera kudengenyeka kwenyika kwakakura mamaginichudhi 7.5.
"Apo njodzi yetsunami yakatanga kuoneka nezuro, vanhu vakange vachiri kungoita zvavaiita pamahombekombe uye havana kukwanisa kutiza pakarepo uye vakava pangozi," Sutopo Purwo Nugroho, mutauriri wesangano rinoona nezvekuderedza njodzi muIndonesia reBNPB akadaro paaibvunzurudzwa muJakarta.
"Tsunami haina kungouya iri yega pachayo, yaikukura mota, matanda, dzimba, yaipaza chero chinhu chiri panyika," Nugroho akadaro, achiwedzera kuti tsunami yakange yafamba ichipfuura nemugungwa ichimhanya pamwero we800 kph (497 mph) isati yarova mahombekombe.
Vamwe vanhu vakakwira mumiti kuti vasakukurwa netsumani uye vakapona, akadaro.
Vanhu vangada kusvika 16,700 vakabviswa vachiendeswa munzvimbo 24 dziri muPalu.
Mifananidzo yemuchadenga yakabuditswa neajenzi yekurwisana nenjodzi yairatidza zvivakwa zvakawanda nezvitoro zvakaparadzwa, mabhiriji akamonyororwa uye akadonha uye temberi yakatenderedzwa nemvura.
Kumwewo kudengenyeka kudiki kwakazoramba kuchiitika muguta iri riri kumhenderekedzo nemusi weMugovera.
Kudengenyeka kwenyika kwakatevedzana kwakanzwika munzvimbo ine vagari vanosvika mamiriyoni 2.4.
Sangano remuIndonesia reAgency for the Assessment and Application of Technology (BPPT) rakataura kuti simba rakaburitswa nekudengenyeka kukuru kwakaitika nemusi weChishanu raipfuura kakapetwa ka200 bhomba reAtomu rakadonhedzerwa muHiroshima mukati meHondo yeChipiri.
Nzvimbo ine guta iri, iyo iri nechekunoperera mukaha wakareba, nekutetepa, inogona kudai yakaratidza kukura kwange kwakaita tsunami, akadaro.
Nugroho akatsanangura kuparadzwa kwakaitika “sekwakakura kwazvo” uye akati zviuru zvedzimba, zvipatara nzvimbo dzekutengera nemahotera zvakadonha.
Mitumbi yevakawirwa nenjodzi yakaonekwa yakafushirwa nehungwanda-ngwanda hwemavhinga ezvivakwa zvainge zvadonha, akadaro, achiwedzera kuti vanhu vanosvika 540 vakakuvadzwa uye 29 vaisazivikanwa kwavari.
Nugroho akati kuvadziko uye kuparadza kwakaitika kunogona kunge kwakakura nechekumahombekombe makiromita angasvika 300 (mamayera190) nechekuchamhembe kwePalu, munzvimbo inonzi Donggala, iri pedyo nepakatangira kudengenyeka.
Nzira yekutumirana mashoko "yakavhiringidzwa zvachose pasina kana kufambiswa kwemashoko" kubva kuDonggala, Nugroho akadaro.
Kune vanhu vanopfuura 300,000 vanogara ikoko," veRed Cross vakadaro mumashoko avo, vachiwedzera kuti vashandi wavo uye vazvipiri vakange vachitoenda kunzvimbo dzakakanganiswa.
"Iyi itori njodzi nechekare, asi inogona kutopfuura ipapa," vakadaro.
Sangano iri rakashorwa zvikuru nemusi weMugovera nekusazivisa kuti tsunami yange yarova Palu, kunyange zvazvo vakuru-vakuru vakati masai-sai akanga auya munguva apo chenjedzo yakange iri kupiwa.
Muvhidhiyo isina kunyatsojeka iri kutenderedzwa munzvimbo dzekuwadzana pamafoni dzevanhu murume anenge ari nechepamusor-soro pechiwakwa anonzwika achideedzera mashoko echenjedzo kuvanhu vaiwe mumugwagwa pasi nezvetsunami yaiuya.
Pasina maminitsi akawanda mudhuri wemvura unorova mohembekombe, uchikukura zvivakwa nemotokari.
VeReuters havana kukwanisa kupa mashoko ehuchokwadi hwevhidhiyo iyi nekukurumidza.
Kudengenyeka uku netsunami zvakakonzera kudzima kwemagetsi munzvimbo dzakawanda uko kwakaita kuti kufambiswa kwemashoko kukanganisike munzvimbo dzemuPelu zvichipa dambudziko kuvakuru-vakuru kuti varonge nzira yekununura nayo.
Mauto atanga kutumira ndege dzinotakura zvinhu dziine rubatsiro kubva kuJakarta nemamwe maguta, vakuru-vakuru vakadaro, asi vatamiswi ava vachiri kuda zvekudya nezvimwe zvinhu zvakakosha.
Nhandare yendege yeguta iri yavhurwa nekuda kwekufambiswa kwerubatsiro chete uye icharamba yakavharwa kusvika musi waGumiguru.
Mutungamiri wenyika Joko Widodo akarongwa kuti ashanyire nzvimbo dzakatamisirwa vanhu muPalu musi weSvondo.
Uwandu Hwevakauraiwa neTsunami muIndonesia Hwosvika Pamusoro pe800.
Hazvina Kumira Zvakanaka.
Kunyange zvazvo vashandi wesangano reWorld Vision vanobva kuDonggala vakwanisa kusvika zvakakotsekana kuguta rePalu, uko vashandi vari kugara mumatende akaiswa munzvimbo yepahofisi yawo, vakadarika nemunzvimbo dzakaparadzwa pavaive munzira kuuya, VaDoseba vakadaro.
"Vandiudza kuti vaona dzimba dzakawanda dzange dzakaparadzwa," akadaro.
Hazvina kumira zvakanaka.
Kunyange zvazvo mapoka anopa rubatsiro atotanga kugadzirira kugovera rubatsiro, vamwe vakatsutsumwa kuti vamwe vashandi vanopa rubatsiro vekunze avo vane ruzivo vainge vachirambidzwa kuuuya kuPalu.
Mukuwirirana nemitemo yemuIndonesia, mari dzerubatsiro, zvinhu, nevashandi vanobva mhiri kwemakungwa vanogona kutanga kupinda chete kana nzvimbo yaitikira njodzi yaziviswa senjodzi yenyika.
Izvozvo hazvisati zvaitwa kusvika parizvino.
"Ichiri njodzi inotarisirwa nepurovhinzi," akadaro Aulia Arriani, mutauriri weRed Cross yemuIndonesia.
"Kana hurumende yangoti, "ZVAKANAKA, iri idambudziko renyikar," tinobva tabvumira rubatsiro rwunobva munyika dzose asi izvi hazvisati zvasvika ipapo."
Muhusiku hwepiri muPalu mushure mekudengenyeka uye tsunami yakaitika musi weChishanu, shamwari nehama dzeavo vakanga vasati wavanikwa dzakanga dzachakabatirira patariro yekuti vadiwa wavo vanogona kuonekwa zvikave chishamiso chinonyevenutsa panyaya yenjodzi dzinongoitika dzoga.
Nemusi weMugovera, mumwe mukomana mudiki akabviswa mugomba retsvina.
Nemusi weSvondo,vanunuri vakanunura mukadzi akange akadzvanyidzirwa pasi peungwanda-ngwanda kwemazuva maviri nemutumbi waamai wake uri pedyo naye.
Gendon Subandono, kochi wechikwata chenyika yeIndonesia chemutambo wekubhururuka neparashutu, akange arovedza vaviri wevatambi varikushayikwa vaizotamba muMitambo yemuAsia, iyo yakapera nechekutanga kwemwedzi uno muIndonesia.
Vamwe vevakavharirwa nehungwanda-ngwanda paHotera yeRoa Roa, kubatanidza naVaMandagi, vaiwe vadzidzi wake.
"Semunhu agara nebasa mumutambo wekubhururuka neparashutu, ndine kushushikana kwandiinako mupfugwa," akadaro.
VaGendon vakarondedzera kuti zvakafamba sei, papera maawa mushure mekutenderera kwenhau dzekudonha kwehotera yeRoa Roa pakati pevatsigiri vemitambo yekubhururuka neparashutu, akange aedza kutumira mameseji eWhatsapp kune vakwikwidzi vemuPalu, avo vaibatanidzwa mumhemberero dzekumahombekombe.
Mameseji ake, zvakadaro, akangoratidza tiki imwe chete yegireyi, panzvimbo pematiki maviri ebhuruu.
"Ndofunga kuti izvi zvinoreva kuti mameseji ainge asina kusvika," akadaro.
Mbavha dzotora $26,750 pakuiswa kwemari mumuchina weATM paNewport iri paLevee
Nemusi weChishanu mangwanani mbavha dzakaba $26,750 kubva kumushandi weBrink uyo aiisa mari mumuchina weATM paNewport iri paLevee, mukuwirirana nenhau dzakabudiswa neNewport Police Department.
Mutyairi wemota ainge achibvisa mari mumuchina weATM uri muchiwakwa chekutandarira achigadzirira kuendesa imwe mari, Det. Dennis McCarthy akanyora kudaro mune zvakabuda.
Paakange akabatikana, mumwe murume "akamhanya nechekumashure kwemushandi weBrink" ndokuba bhegi remari raaida kutakura.
Zvapupu zvakaona vanhu vakawanda varikufungidzirwa vachitiza vachibva panzvimbo yacho, mukuwirirana nezvakabuditswa, asi mapurisa haana kutaura uwandu hwevanhu vakabatanidzwa muchiitiko ichi.
Chero ane mashoko pamusoro pavo anofanira kubata mapurisa epaNewport panhamba dzinoti 859-292-3680.
Kanye West: Muimbi ochinja zita rake kuve Ye
Muimbi anonzi Kanye West arikuchinja zita rake - kuve Ye.
Achizivisa nezvekuchinja uku padandemutande reTwitter nemusi weMugovera, akanyora kuti: "Uyo aimbozivikanwa saKanye West."
West, ane makore 41, akapiwa zita remadunhurirwa rekuti Ye kwenguva yakati uye akashandisa zita iri semusoro wedambarefu rake rechisere, iro rakaburitswa muna Chikumi.
Kuchinja uku kwauya panguva apo achava pachinoitika cheSaturday Night Live, apo arikutarisirwa kuparura dambarefu rake idzva rine musoro unoti Yandhi.
Achatsiva muimbi anonzi Ariana Grande pamutambo uyo waakakanzura nekuda "kwehasha," murongi wemutambo uyu akadaro.
Richivazve shoko rekupfupikisa rezita rake rebasa, West akamboti zita iri rine zvarinoreva mune zvechitendero.
"Ndinotenda kuti 'ye' ishoko rinoshandiswa zvakanyanya muBhaibheri, uye muBhaibheri rinoreva kuti 'iwe,'" West akadaro mukutanga kwegore rino,achikurukura nezvedambarefu rake nemukurukuri wepanhepfenyuro anonzi Big Boy.
"Saka ndiri iwe, ndiri isu, ndisu.
Ndakachinja kubva kuzita rekuti Kanye, iro rinoreva kuti iye chete, kuenda kuzita rekuti Ye - iro rinongoratidza kunaka kwedu, kushata kwedu, kuvhiringidzika kwedu, zvese.
Dambarefu iri ringori chiratidzo chezvatiri."
Ndiye mumwe vevaimbi vedu vakakurumbira vakachinja mazita avo.
Sean Combs aizivikanwa nevakawanda saPuff Daddy, P. Diddy kana kuti Diddy, asi gore rino akazivisa chido chake chekushandisa mazita ekuti Love uye Brother Love.
Aimbobatana naWest pakuimba, JAY-Z, akaitawo kuti pawe kana kusawa nekamutsetse kana mavara makuru.
AMLO yeMexico yopikira kuti haizoshandisiri vanhu mauto
Mutungamiri weMexico akasarudzwa Andres Manuel Lopez Obrador apika kuti haazomboshandisiri vanhu mauto sezvo nyika iyi inosvitsa makore 50 ekuyeuka kushandisirwa chisimba kwakaguma nekudeuka kweropa pavadzidzi.
Lopez Obrador akavimbisa nemusi weMugovera paTlatelolco Plaza kuti "regai zvachose kushandisa mauto pakudzvanyirira vanhu wemuMexico."
Zvikwata zvemauto zvakapfura varatidziri vairatidzira zvine runyararo paplaza musi waOct. 2, 1968, zvichiuraya vanoda kusvika vanhu 300 panguva apo boka revadzidzi vanopikisa vakanga varikuwedzera muLatin America.
Lopez Obrador akazvipira kutsigira vechidiki wekuMexico nekupa mari dzepamwedzi nemwedzi kune avo vanenge vachidzidza uye pakuvhura mayunivhesiti everuzhinji asingabhadhariswi.
Akati kushayikwa kwemabasa pamwe nekushaya mikana yekudzidza kunoita kuti vechidiki vapinde muzvikwata zvinopara mhosva.
U.S. inofanira kupeta kaviri mari yainobhadhara kuzvirongwa zve A.I.
Sezvo China iri kuramba ichiwedzera kuita mapurogiramu emakombuyuta ane huchenjeri pakuita zvimwe zvinhu, U.S. inofanira kupeta kaviri mari yainopedzera mukuita tsvakurudzo muchikamu ichi, anodaro Kai-Fu Lee uyo ari mune zvemabhizimisi uye ari mazvikokota muchikamu che-AI, uyo akashandira Google, Microsoft uye Apple.
Mashoko aya auya pashure pekunge zvikamu zvakawanda zvehurumende yeU.S. zvapa zviziviso zvinechekuita neAI, kunyange zvazvo U.S. isina nzira iri pamutemo muchikamu cheAI.
Zvichakadaro, China yakaisa hurongwa hwayo mugore rakapfuura: iri kuronga kuti ive paNhamba 1 muruzivo rweAI panozosvika gore ra2030.
"Kupeta kaviri bhajeti yekuitwa kwetsvakurudzo yeAI panenge pari pekutangira pakanaka, tichitarisa kuti dzimwe nyika dzose dziri kumashure kwazvo kweU.S., uye tirikutarisira mberi pakuburwa kwezvinhu zvitsva muchikamu cheAI," akadaro Lee.
Kupeta kaviri mari inodiwa kunogonawo kupeta kaviri mikana yekuti budiriro huru inotevera muchikamu cheAI iitike muU.S., Lee akaudza weCNBC muhurukuro yavakaita mukati mevhiki rino.
Lee, uyo ane bhuku rinonzi "Vari Kutonga Panyaya DzeAI: Bhuku rinonzi China, Silicon Valley uye Gadziriro Itsva yePasi" rakaburitswa mwedzi uno naHoughton Mifflin Harcourt, uyo ari Mukuru Webasa paSinovation Ventures, iyo yakaisa mari yakawanda mune imwe yemakambani eAI akakurumbira muChina, Face++.
Mumakore ekuma 1980 paYunivhesiti yeCarnegieakashanda pane imwe mhando yeAI yakakunda mhando yepamusoro-soro muAmerica yemutambi weOthello, uye nekufamba kwenguva akava nechigaro chepamusoro paMicrosoft Research uye akava purezidhendi wechikamu cheGoogle chekuChina.
Lee akatenda urongwa hwekare hwehurumende yeU.S hwekuva nemakwikwi akadai seDefense Advanced Research Projects Agency's Robotics Challenge uye akabvunza kuti aitevera aizoitwa riini, kuitira kuti agone kuona nyanzvi dzeramangwana.
Vatsvakurudzi muU.S. kazhinji-kazhinji vanofanira kushanda nesimba kuti vagone kubudirira kuwana rubatsiro kubva kuhurumende,akadaro Lee.
"Haisi China irikutora vatungamiriri mune zvedzidzo; makambani," akadaro Lee.
Makambani akadai seFacebook, Google nemamwewo ari mune zvekugadzirwa kwezvinhu ndiwo arikupinza basa shasha dzinenge dzabva kumayunivhesiti kuti dzishande muzvikamu zveAI mumakore ano.
Lee akati kuchinjwa kwemitemo yekubuda nekupinda munyika kunogona kubatsirawo U.S kusimbaradza zvairi kuita mune zveAI.
"Ndinofunga kuti rezinesi rinobvumira munhu wekune imwe nyika kuti agare zvachose munyika rinofanira kungopiwa pakarepo kune vanePHD mune zve AI," akadaro.
Kanzuru yeNyika yeChina yakapa Hurongwa hwayo hweNext Generation Artificial Intelligence Development Plan muna Chikunguru mugore ra2017.
National Natural Science Foundation yeChina yakapa mari kune vanhu varipazvikoro zvedzidzo yepamusoro kufanana nenzira iyo National Science Foundation nemamwe masangano ehurumende anopa nawo mari kuvatsvakurudzi vemuU.S., asi hunaku hwebasa revakadzidza huri pasi muChina, akadaro Lee.
Kutanga kwegore rino U.S. Defense Department yakaita kuti pave nemuzinda wezveAI weJoint Artificial Intelligence Center,nechinangwa chekushanda pamwe nevari muindasitiri nevezvedzidzo, uye hurumende yeAmerica yakazivisa kuvambwa kweKomiti Yakasarudzwa nekuda kweMapurogiramu Emakombuyuta Ane Huchenjeri Pakuita Zvimwe Zvinhu.
Uye mumwedzi uno DARPA yakazivisa kuti mari inosvika mabhirioni 2 emadhora yaizoshandiswa pahurongwa hunonzi AI Next.
Kana iri NSF, irikuisa mari inosvika mamiriyoni 100 emadhora pagore mumabasa etsvakurudzo dzeAI.
Zvichakadaro, mutemo weU.S. uyo une chinangwa chekuumba Komishoni yeNyika munhau dzeChengeteko mune zveMapurogiramu Emakombuyuta Ane Huchenjeri Pakuita Zvimwe Zvinhu hauna kushanda kwemwedzi yakati.
Macedonia yovhota kuti vaone kuti vochinja here zita renyika
Vanhu vekuMacedonia vakavhota musarudzo dzakaitwa nemusi weSvondo kuti vaone kana vachifanira kuchinja zita kuve "Republic of North Macedonia," chiito chinogona kupedza gakava rave nemakumi emakore neGreece iyo yakaramba kuti ive nhengo yesangano reMubatanidzwa weNyika dzemuYuropu uye NATO.
Greece, iyo ine purovhinzi rinonzi Macedonia, inosimbirira kuti zita renyika remuvakidzani wayo wekuchamhembe rinoreva kuti irikuzviita muridzi venzvimbo yavo uye yakaramba kuti ipinde muNATO uye EU.
Hurumende mbiri idzi dzakaita chibvumirano mumwedzi waChivabvu chakavakirwa pazita idzva, asi vapikisi munyika vari kuti kuchinja uku kunozvidza nhoroondo yekuzivikanwa kwevanhu vechiSlavic vakawanda vemuMacedonia.
Mutungamiri wenyika Gjorge Ivanov akati haasi kuzovhota musarudzo yacho uye nhimbe yekukurudzira vanhu kuramba kundovhota yaita kuti pasave nechokwadi chekuti chiverengero chevanhu vachanovhota chichasvitsa here zvikamu 50 kubva muzana zvinodiwa nekuda kwesarudzo iyi kuti ishande.
Mubvunzo uri pabepa resarudzo waiti: "Uri muchisarudzo chekuti tive nhengo yeNATO uye EU nokubvuma chibvumirano chakavapo neGreece."
Vaitsigira kuti zita richinjwe, kubatanidza Mukuru weMakurukota Zoran Zaev, akapa pfungwa yekuti zvine usoro kuMacedonia kuti ishingirire kuti ipinde mumasangano akadai seEU uye NATO, inova imwe yedzimwe nyika dzakasimuka kubva mukudonha kweYugoslavia.
"Ndauya nhasi kuti ndivhote nekuda kweramangwana renyika, kuti vechidiki vari muMacedonia vararame vakasununguka vari pasi pechengeteko yeMubatanidzwa weNyika dzemuYuropu nekuti zvinoreva upenyu hwakachengeteka nekuda kwedu tose," akadaro Olivera Georgijevska, ane makore 79, ari muSkopje.
Kunyange hazvo tisingamanikidzirwi pamutemo, nhengo dzakawanda dzeparamende dzati dzichatevedzera zvinenge zvabuda musarudzo kuti zvishande.
Kuchinja zita uku kunoda kuti pave nezvikamu zviviri pazvitatu zvevazhinji muparamende.
Komishoni yenyika yesarudzo yakati pakange pasina mishumo yekusafamba zvakanaka kwezvinhu pakazosvika 1 masikati.
Zvisinei, huwandu hwevakauya hwakasvika pazvikamu 16 kubva muzana, zvichienzaniswa nezvikamu 34 kubva muzana musarudzo dzeparamende dzakaitwa mugore ra2016 apo zvikamu 66 kubva muzana zveavo vakanyoresa kuvhota zvakavhota.
"Ndauya kuti ndivhote nekuda kwevana vangu, musha wedu uri muEurope," akadaro Gjose Tanevski, ane makore 62, uyo akavhotera muguta guru, reSkopje.
Mukuru weMakurukota eHurumende muMacedonia Zoran Zaev, mudzimai wake Zorica uye mwanakomana wake Dushko vakavhota vari muMacedonia panhau yekuchinja zita renyika izvo zvaizovhura mukana wekuti ikwanise kuve nhengo yeNATO uye European Union muStrumica, iri muMacedonia munaGunyana 30, 2018.
Pamberi peparamende iri muSkopje, Vladimir Kavardarkov, ane makore 54, aigadzira puratifomu diki achidhonza macheya aiva pamberi pematende akange aiswa nevaisada kuti kuvhota kuitwe.
"Tiri veNATO uye EU, asi tiri kuda kuzviitira chisarudzo chekupindamo tega, kwete sekunge tiri kubatsirwa kuita kudaro" akadaro Kavadarkov.
"Nyika yedu ine hurombo, asi tine chiremera.
Kana vasingadi kuti tishandise zita rekuti Macedonia, tinogona kutendeukira kune vamwe vakadai seChina neRussia tova nhengo dzemubatanidzwa weNyika dzekuEurope uye dzekuAsia."
Mukuru weMakurukota eHurumende Zaev anoti kuve nhengo yeNATO kunounza budiriro mune zvemabhizimisi iyo iri kudiwa chaizvo muMacedonia, iyo ine mwero wekushayikwa kwemabasa kunopfuura zvikamu 20 kubva muzana.
"Ndinovimba kuti vazhinji vachatsigira urongwa uhwu nekuti vanopfuura 80 muzana vevagari wemuno vari pfungwa yekuti tive nhengo yeEU uye NATO," Zaev akadaro pashure pekuvhota.
Akati kana zvichabuda zvikava "hongu" zvinoreva "kusimbisirwa kweramangwana redu."
Zvakabuda muongororo yakaitwa nesangano reMacedonia's Institute for Policy Research zvinoratidza kuti zvikamu 30 kusvika ku 43 kubva muzana zvevavhoti zvaizotora rutivi musarudzo - unowa huwandu huri pasi pehunotarisirwa.
Mune imwe ingororo, yakaitwa neMacedonia's Telma TV, yakawana vanhu vanosvika 57 kubva muzana vakabvunzurudzwa vachiti vaizoenda kunovhota nemusi weSvondo.
Pane ivava, vanosvika 70 muzana vakati vachavhota vachitsigira.
Kuti chisarudzo chiri kuvhoterwa chishande huwandu hunotarisirwa kune vachavhota hunofanira kusvika zvikamu 50 kubva muzana nevhoti imwe chete.
Kukundikana kwechinangwa chesarudzo kuchareva chipangaidzo chikuru kumutemo wehurumende iyi inotsigira nyika dzekuMadokero kubvira apo yakatanga kutonga muna Chivabvu gore rapera.
Tarisa: Mutambi weManchester City anonzi Sergio Aguero opinda nepakati pemadhifenda echikwata cheBrighton achitsvaka chibodzwa
Sergio Aguero naRaheem Sterling vakashaisa basa madhifenda echikwata cheBrighton mumutambo wakapera Manchester City yakunda nezvibodzwa 2-0 nemusi weMugovera munhandare yeEtihad iri muManchester, muEngland.
Aguero akaita kuti zvionekwe sezvaive nyore-nyore zvikuru pamamwisiro aakaita chibodzwa muminiti yechi65.
Mutambi uyo anotambira mberi achibva kunyika yeArgentina akapasirwa bhora ari nechepakati-nepakati penhandare pakutanga kwemafambiro ezvakazoitika.
Akamhanya ari nechepakati pemadhifenda matatu eBrighton, ndokupinda paiva nemukana wakakura.
Aguero akazozviwana aunganirwa nevatambi vaive nahembe dzegirini.
Akasuka dhifenda wekutanga ndokumhanya achisiya vamwe vacho vakawanda nechepamutsetse webhokisi reBrighton.
Akabva asundira bhora nechekuruboshwe kwake, richienda pana Sterling.

Havakwanisi kushivirira vanhu vanoburitsa maonero avo
Apo avo vanorwira kodzero dzevanhu veMomentum vari mubato remunzvimbo yedu vakasarudza kuti ndiongororwe, hazvina kundishamisa.
Zvakadaro, ndini wekupedzisira pandandanda yemaMP eLabour kuudzwa kuti hatisi kugamuchirwa - nekuda kwekungotaura maonero edu.
Mumwe wandinoshanda naye muparamende anonzi Joan Ryan akabatwa zvakafanana nekuda kwekuti akamira zvakasimba achishora rusaruraganda.
Panhau yangu, vakapa pfungwa yekuongororwa vaishora kusawirirana kwangu naJeremy Corbyn.
Nezvekukosha kwemitemo yezveupfumi yakanaka, pakudzivirirwa kwenyika, paEurope, zvinova zhinhu zvimwe chetezvo izvo Jeremy asina kuwirirana nevatungamiriri vaimbovepo.
Chiziviso nezvemusangano weLabour wekuNottingham East nemusi weChishanu chaiti "tiri kuda kuti musangano uyu ubatanidze pfungwa dzese uye uvake."
Kweanenge makore angu ose masere ndiri MP weLabour, musangano weGC wakaitwa manheru eChishanu wainge usina musiyano.
Zvinosuruvarisa kuti nhasi, haasiriwo maitirwo ari kuitwa misangano yakawanda uye chivimbiso chekuva "ane mutsa”, munyoro" munhau dzezvematongerwo enyika kwakasokanganwika kare kana kuri kuti, zvakatomboitika.
Zviri kuramba zvichijairika kuti kupa maonero akasiyana hakugamuchirwi mubato reLabour uye mafungiro ega-ega anopenengurwa kuti aonekwe kuti anogamuchirwa here nevatungamiriri webato.
Izvi zvakatanga munguva pfupi mushure mekunge Jeremy ava mutungamiriri, apo shamwari dzangu dzandaifunga kuti taive nemaonera akafanana mune zvematongerwo enyika dzakatanga kutarisira kuti ndingoerekana ndachinja ndobvuma zvinhu izvo zvichida zvandaisambofa ndakawirirana nazvo - pangava pari panhau yekudzivirirwa kwenyika kana kuti yezvemusika mumwe chete weEU.
Pose pandinotaura paruzhinji - pasinei nezvandataura - panobva patotevera kushoropodzwa pamadandemutande anowadzana vanhu vachida kuti ndibviswe, vachishora maitirwo ezvinhu mune zvematongerwo enyika munzvimbo, vachindiudza kuti handifaniri kuve nhengo yebato reLabour.
Uye izvi hazvina kuitika kwandiri ndega.
Chaizvoizvo, ndinoziva kuti ndine rombo rakanaka kupfuura vamwe vanhu sezvo zvaitaurwa nezvangu zvaingove zvematongerwo enyika.
Ndinoshamiswa chaizvo nemashandiro uye hushingi hweshamwari idzodzo vakasangana negomo rekukura kwerusaruro zuva rimwe nerimwe asi vasingaodzwi mwoyo nazvo.
Chimwe chinhu chinorwadza chaizvo pamaitirwo ezvematongerwo enyika panguva ino ndechekutora kumbunyikidzwa sekusina basa.
Jeremy Corbyn svondo rakapfuura akati bato reLabour rinofanira kukudziridza tsika yekugamuchirana zvakanaka.
Cokwadi chiripo ndechekuti hatichagamuchirani uye pachisarudzo chimwe nechimwe “chekushaya chivimbo” kana kuchinja kwemitemo yekusarudza nayo zvinhu bato rinobva ramanikidzika.
Ndakapiwa mazano akawanda mumakore maviri apfuura ndichikurudzirwa kuti ndirege kusimudza musoro, ndisataurisa zvoreva kuti ndinenge "ndave munhu kwaye."
Asi izvi handizvo zvandakapindira mune zvematongerwo enyika.
Kubvira apo ndakapinda mubato reLabour makore 32 apfuura ndichiri mwana wechikoro, ndaodzwa mwoyo nekuregeredza kwehurumende yaThatcher uko kwakasiya kirasi yepachikoro yandaidzidzira ichiparara, ndakasarudza kutanga kuita mabasa anobatsira veruzhinji zvikuru sei kune avo vaida kubatsirwa nenzira iyi - ndiri kanzera wemunzvimbo kana kuti gurukota rehurumende.
Handina kumbobvira ndahwanza mafungiro angu mune zvematongerwo enyika, kusanganisira musarudzo yakapfuura.
Hapana kana nemumwe muNottingham East aigona kunge akavhiringidzwa munzira ipi zvayo nemaonero ezvinhu andaiita uye zvandaipikisana nazvo nehutungamiriri huripo.
Kune avo vakatsigira chisarudzo ichi nemusi weChishanu, zvandinongotaura chete ndezvekuti panguva apo nyika ichanangana neBrexit iyo ichakanganisa mhuri, mabhizimusi uye mabasa ehurumende, handinzwisisi chido chekupedza nguva nesimba rangu ndichitsigira mutungamiriri webato reLabour.
Asi chaizvoizvo shoko iri randinaro handisi kuritaurira Nottingham Momentum, ndirikutaurira nzvimbo yandinomiririra, vangave vari nhengo dzeLabour kana kuti kwete: Ndinonzwa kudada nekukushandirai uye ndinovimbisa kuti hapana mwero wekutyisidzirwa kuti ndibviswe kana maonero munezvematongerwo enyika zvichandidzorera shure mune zvandinotenda zvakakunakirai.

Kuzama kwaitwa naGrant Anderson paminiti yechi14, kwazopedzeredzwa naFrazier Climo, kwaita kuti chikwata cheAyr chitungamire, asi, kadhi reyero rapiwa kaputeni wekuScotland anonzi Rory Hughes, raburitswa pamutambo naWarriours, raita kuti chikwata cheMelrose chione kukosha kwehuwandu uye Jason Baggot awana mukana usina kuzopedzeredzwa zvakanaka.
