John Edward: Unyanzvi mune zvemitauro hwakakosha kuvagari vepasi rose
Zvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende muScotland zvoramba zviri padanho repamusoro mune zvedzidzo, uye izvi zvakapfuurira mugore ra2018 nekubudirira mubvunzo kwemhando yepamusoro, uko kwaisimbaradzwa nekushanda nesimba kwemunhu mumwe nemumwe uye seboka mune zvemitambo, zveunyanzvi, zvemimhanzi uye mune zvimwe zvirongwa zvekubatsira vanhu munharaunda.
Nevana vechikoro vanopfuura 30,000 kupota nemuScotland yose, zvikoro izvi, zvichimiririrwa neScottish Council of Independent Schools (SCIS), zvinovavarira kupa ruyamuro rwakakura kuvadzidzi wavo uye kuvabereki.
Zvikoro izvi zvisiri zvehurumende zvine chinangwa chekugadzirira vadzidzi wavo kuti vaenderere mberi nedzidzo yepamusoro, kuwana basa ravanoda uye nzvimbo yavanoda mupasi rose.
Sechikamu chedzidzo chinokwanisa kugadzira uye kushandisa purogiramu inoyemurwa yedzidzo, tiri kuona mitauro yechizvinouno ichipfurira kuve chikamu chakakurumbira uye chinodiwa kwazvo nevakawanda muzvikoro.
Nelson Mandela akati: "Kana ukataura nemunhu mumutauro waanonzwisisa, izvozvo zvinopinda mumusoro make.
Kana ukataura naye mumutauro wake izvozvo zvinosvika pamoyo pake."
Ichi chiyeuchidzo chakasimba chekuti hatigoni kungotsamira pamutauro weChirungu kana tichizoda kuvaka ukama uye kuvimbana nevanhu vekune dzimwe nyika.
Kubva mune zvakabuda mubvunzo dzegore rino, tiri kuona kuti chikamu chezvemitauro ndicho chiri kutungamirira pane zvimwe nekubudirira kukuru kwazvo muzvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende.
Vadzidzi vanosvika zvikamu 68 kubva muzana vaidzidza mitauro yekune dzimwe nyika wakavana giredhi Yepamusoro A.
Mashoko, akatorwa kubva kunhengo dzezvikoro 74 dzeSCIS, akaratidza kuti zvikamu 72 kubva muzana zvevadzidzi wakavana giredhi repamusoro A mumutauro weMandarin, kwozotiwo zvikamu 72 kubva muzana zveavo vaidzidzira mutauro wekuGerman, zvikamu 69 kubva muzana kune waidzidzira chiFrench uye zvikamu 63 kubva muzana kune vaidzidzira chiSpanish wakavanawo giredhi A.
Izvi zvinoratidza kuti zvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende muScotland zviri kutsigira chaizvo mitauro wekune dzimwe nyika sehunyanzvi hunokosha uhwo vana nevechidiki pasina mubvunzo vangada mune ramangwana.
Iye zvino mitauro, sechidzidzo chinodiwa, chavekuonekwa nenzira imwe chete sezvinoitwa zvidzidzo zveSTEM (sayenzi, zvekugadzirwa kwezvinhu, zvehuinjiniya uye zvemasvomhu) mumapurogiramu edzidzo ezvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende uye kumwewo.
Ongororo yakaitwa neKomishoni yaMabasa uye Unyanzvi muUK yakaona kuti zvikonzero zvinopihwa nevashandirwi zvinoita kuti vaomerwe nekuwana vanhu vakakodzera basa, zvikamu 17 kubva muzana zvange zvakanangana nekushayikwa kwevane hunyanzvi mune zvemitauro.
Zvakadaro zviri kuwedzera zvikuru kuti, unyanzvi munwe zvemitauro hudiwe kuitira kugadzirira vana vadiki nekuda kwemabasa avo emunguva yemberi .
Paine kudiwa kweunyanzvi mune zvemutauro pamabasa, unyanzvi uhwu hwakakosha mupasi rose rakabatana.
Pasinei nekuti munhu asarudza basa ripi, kana kuri kuti akadzidza mumwe mutauro, anova padanho riri nani mune ramangwana nekuva nehunyanzvi seuhwu kwakakosha muupenyu hwemunhu.
Kukwanisa kutaura zvakananga nevanhu vanobva kune dzimwe nyika kunovhurira pakarepo munhu anokwanisa kutaura mitauro yakawanda kuti ave nemukana wakakura pane vamwe.
Mukuwirirana neongororo yakaitwa neYouGov yevanhu vabva zera vanopfuura 4,000 vekuUK mugore ra2013, zvikamu 75 kubva muzana vakanga vasingakwanisi kutaura zvakanaka mitauri yekune dzimwe nyika kuti vagone kuita hurukuro uye mutauro wechiFrench uchingova ivo bedzi unotaurwa nechikamu chinosvika, 15 kubva muzana.
Ndicho chikonzero nei kutsigirwa zvakasimba kwekudzidzisa vana mitauro kwakakosha zvikuru kuvana vanhasi.
Kukwanisa kutaura mitauro yakawanda, zvikuru sei iya yenyika dzichiri kusimukira, kunoshongedzera vana kuti vazove nemikana yakakura yekuwana mabasa ari nani.
MuScotland, chikoro chimwe nechimwe chinosiyana mitauro yachinodzidzisa.
Zvikoro zvakawanda zvinonyanyosimbirira mitauro yepamusoro yechizvinouno, nepo vamwe vachidzidzisa mitauro inoonekwa seinonyanyokosha kunyika yeUK kana tichitarira mberi panozosvika 2020, yakafanana neMandarin kana kuti chiJapanese.
Pasinei nezvinofarirwa nemwana wako, kwagara kunongori nemitauro yakawanda yekusarudza muzvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende, nevadzidzisi vari nyanzvi muzvikamu izvozvo.
Zvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende muScotland zvakazvipira kugovera mamiriro ezvinhu anoita kuti mwana ave akagadzirira uye akashongedzerwa nehunyanzvi hunodiwa kuti abudirire, pasinei nekuti ramangwana rakamira sei.
Hazvigoni kurambika panguva ino, mumabhizimusi pasi rose, kuti mitauro inoramba yakakosha chaizvo mune ramangawana renyika, uye izvi zvinofanira kuratidzwa mune zvedzidzo.
Chaizvoizvo, mitauro yazvinouno inofanira kuonekwa “seunyanzvi hwekutaura pasi rose."
Zvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende zvicharamba zvichipa chisarudzo ichi, zvekusarudza zvakawanda, uye humhizha kuvana vadiki vekuScotland.
Il faut bien le faire.

Nguva yeMusangano Wekutsvaga Rutsigiro waTrump muWest Virginia, paDandemutande reYouTube
Mutungamiriri weNyika Donald Trump otanga misangano yekutsvaga rutsigiro muWheeling, iri muWest Virginia.
Uyu musangano wekutanga waTrump pamisangano mishanu yakarongerwa kuitwa muvhiki rinouya, kusanganisira kumbomira munzvimbo dzine ushamwari dzinosanganisira Tennessee neMississippi.
Nekumiswa kwekuitwa kwevhoti yekusimbisira kusarudzwa kwemunhu waakadoma kuti atore basa remuDare Repamusoro, Trump arikuedza kusimbisa rutsigiro nekuda kwesarudzo dzepakati pemwaka dziri kutevera sezvo webato remaRepublicans vangangogona kurasikirwa nekukwanisa kudzora mudare reKongiresi pachaitwa sarudzo munaMbudzi.
Musangano wekutsvaga rutsigiro waTrump muWest Virginia uchaitwa nguvai nhasi manheru uye unokwanisa kuuona sei paindaneti?
Musangano wekutsvaga rutsigiro waTrump muWheeling, muWest Virginia wakarongwa kuitwa nenguva dza7. ET nhasi manheru, Mugovera, Gunyana 29, 2018.
Unogona kuona musangano uyu wekutsvaga rutsigiro waTrump muWest Virginia paindaneti pasi apa uchidhaunirodha zvakananga padandemutande reYouTube.
Trump anogona kutaura nezvenhau yekutongwa kweakasarudzwa pabasa reDare Repamusoro Brett Kavanaugh, iyo yanetsa yekupomerwa kwake kuti akambunyikidza munhu mune zvepabonde pachimirirwa chisarudzo cheSeneti icho chichapiwa mushure mevhiki panguva apo FBI ichiita ongororo.
Asi chinangwa chikuru chemisangano iyi ndechekutanga kutsvaka rutsigiro kwebato remaRepublicans iro richasangana nesarudzo dzakaoma zvikuru idzo dzichatanga muna Mbudzi.
Zvadaro, varongi vemisangano yeMutungamiri weNyika Trump vakati chinangwa chemisangano iyi mishanu "ndechekusimbiradza vazvipiri uye vatsigiri sezvo bato reamaRebublicana rinoedza kuchengetedza uye kuwedzera uwandu hwavo mudare reSeneti uye neParamende," mukuwirirana neReuters.
"Kuve nesimba rakakura muKongiresi ndiko kwakakosha pamusoro wehurukuro dzake zvekuti mutungamiri wenyika avhafamba mumaguta akawanda sezvinobvira sezvatinopinda mumwaka wakabatikana wekutsvaka retsigiro," mutauriri wevarongi vemisangano yekutsvaka rutsigiro waTrump uyo akaramba kudomwa nezita akaudza weReuters.
Musangano wakarongwa kuitwa paWesbanco Arena muWheeling, wanhasi manheru unogona kuunza vatsigiri kubva "kuOhio uye Pennsylvania uye kuonekwa nevateereri muPittsburgh," mukuwirirana neveWest Virginia Metro News.
Mugovera uchave nguva yepiri mumwedzi wapfuura kuti Trump ashanyire West Virginia, guta raakakunda nezvikamu 40 kubva muzana mugore ra2016.
Trump ari kuedza kubatsira Patrick Morrisey uyo arikuda kukwikwidza semumiririri webato remaRepublican mudare reSeneti muWest Virginia, uyo ari nechekumashure musarudzo.
"Hazviratidziki zvakanaka kunaMorrisey kuti mutungamiriri wenyika auye kuzomubatsira kuwana rutsigiro musarudzo," akadaro Simon Haeder, nyanzvi mune zvematongerwo enyika paWest Virginia University, mukuwirirana neReuters.

Europe yotungamira nezvibodzwa 10-6 mumakwikwi eMukombe weRyder wezuva rekupedzisira
Europe ichapinda yakakotsekana muzuva rekupedzisira remakwikwi eMukombe weRyder pashure pekupedza iri mberi nemusi weMugovera pamakwikwi emabhora mana nevatambi vana apo yaitungamira nezvibodzwa 10-6 mberi kweUnited States.
Vaviri vainzwa manyukunyuku Tommy Fleetwood uye Francesco Molinari vakarwisa mumakwikwi aya ndokukunda kaviri Tiger Woods uyo ainetsekawo zvake vachipedza nezvibodzwa zvina paLe Golf National.
Chikwata chekudivi reEurope chaThomas Bjorn, chichivavarira kutorazve mukombe uyo wachakatorerwa kuHazeltine makore maviri apfuura, chakange chichionesa chimoto chikwata chekuAmerican icho chaipotsa zvikuru mumakwikwi ekuseni emabhora mana, zvichiisa zvibodzwa pa3-1.
Chikwata cheU.S. chakaita sungadzisimbe mumakwikwi evatanbi vana ndokukunda mitambo miviri asi havana kukwanisa kudzora zvibodzwa zvavainge vakasaririra nazvo.
Divi raJim Furyk raida zvibodzwa zvisere mumutambo wezvikamu 12 wemusi weSvondo kuti vatorezve mukombe.
Fleetwood ndiye mutambi wekutanga muEurope kutanga kuhwinha zvibodzwa zvina zvakateveedzana mumwaka wake vekutanga panguva apo iye naMolinari, vakarakasha "Molliwood" pakupera kwevhiki zvichiita kuti vave vechipiri kuhwina zvibodzwa zvina pamitambo yavo yekutanga mina muRyder Cup history.
Mushure mekusakadza Woods naPatrick Reed mumutambo wemabhora mana vakabva vatamba zvinomwisa mvura ndokukunda Woods uyo ange apera basa nemutambi mutsva mumwaka wekuAmerica anonzi Bryson Dechambeau nezvibodzwa zvakasimba 5&4.
Woods, uyo akashingirira kupedza mitambo miviri nemusi weMugovera, akaratidza hunyanzvi hwake apo neapo asi kusvika parizvino aruza zvibodzwa 19 kubva mumitambo yake 29 yemabhora mana nevatambi vana uye vanomwe zvichitevedzana.
Justin Rose, uyo ange ari pabhenji pamutambo wemangwanani wemabhora mana, akadzoka ndokubatana naHenrik Stenson mumutambo wevatambi vana ndokukunda nezvibodzwa 2&1 Dustin Johnson naBrooks Koepka - avo vari panhamba yokutanga uye yetatu pari rose.
Zvinhu hazvina kufamba sekutarisira kwaiita Europe kunyange zuva raive rakanaka, richifefetera nechekuchamhembe kwakadziva kumadokero.
Shasha yakahwina kanokwana katatu Jordan Spieth naJustin Thomas vakapa muenzaniso wemaitirwo ezvinhu kudivi rekuAmerica nekutora zvibodzwa zviviri nemusi weMugovera.
Wakahwinha nezvibodzwa 2&1 vachitamba naSpain's Jon Rahm uye Ian Poulter mumutambo wemabhora mana ndokudzokazve pava paya kunokunda Poulter naRory McIlroy nezvibodzwa 4&3 mumutambo wevatambi vana pashure pekutadza kudonhedzera mutukomba twuviri.
Kanongova kaviri bedzi munhoroondo weMukombe weRyder kuti chikwata change chakasara nezvibodzwa zvina chisimukezve chichipinda mumitambo yakazviirira, kunyange zvazvo vaive nemukombe wekudivi raFuryk's vaingoda kudhirowa kuti watorezve mukombe.

North Korea yakati 'hazvibviri' kungosiya zvombo pasina chivimbo
Gurukota rinoona nezvekudyidzana nedzimwe nyika reNorth Korea rakaudza Mubatanidzwa Wenyika dzepasi rose nemusi weMugovera kuti kusiiwa kwezvirango zveupfumi kuripo kurikuita kuti pasambowe nechivimbo neUnited States uye hapana nzira ingatarisirwe nayo yekuti nyika iyi yaizorega kuva nezvombo zvenyukireya pasina kubvumirana mumamiriro ezvinhu akadaro.
Ri Yong Ho akaudza dare iri remusangano wenyika dzepasi rose wepagore kuti North Korea yakatora "matanho makuru akanaka" mugore rapera, akafanana nekumira kuyedza zvombo zvenyukireya nezvinoita zvekuposherwa muchadenga, kupaza paiyedzerwa zvombo zvenyukireya uye kupa mhiko yekusagadzira zvombo zvenyukireya kana zvimwe zvigadzirwawo zvenyukireya.
"Zvisinei, hatisi kuona chido chakafanana chiri kuratidzwa neU.S.," akadaro.
"Pasina chivimbo neU.S. panenge pasinawo gutsikano izere nezvekuchengeteka kwenyika yedu uye mumamiriro ezvinhu iwayo hapana nzira yatingabva tarasa zvombo zvedu pakutanga."
Kunyange zvazvo Ri asina kusimbisira nyunyuto dzeNorth Korea dzenguva dzose nezvekuramba kweWashington kuti kugadzirwa kwezvombo zvenyukiriya kumiswe “zvishoma nezvishoma” izvowo North Korea inofanira kuripwa sekutora kwainenge ichiita matanho zvishoma nezvishoma, mashoko ake airatidza kuve echokwadi mukuti haina kuramba kusiya kugadzira zvombo zvenyukiriya pakarepo sezvakamboitwa naPyongyang munguva yakapfuura.
Ri akanangidzira kumashoko akafanana akapiwa naKim Jong Un uye Donald Trump pamusangano wekutanga munhoroondo pakati pemutungamiriri weU.S. aripo nemutungmiriri weNorth Korea uyo wakaitwa muSingapore mwedzi waChikunguru 12, apo Kim akapika kuti aizoshanda "pakuparadza zvombo zvenyukiriya munyika yeKorea" ukuwo Trump achivimbisa chengeteko yeNorth Korea.
North Korea yange iri kuda kuti hondo yeKorea yemakore ari pakati pa1950 kusvika 1953 inzi yakapera zviri pamutemo, asi nyika yeUnited States yakati Pyongyang anofanira kutanga asiya zvombo zvake zvenyukiriya.
Washington yakaramba zvakare kurerutsa zvirango zveupfumi zvikukutu zvayakapa North Korea.
"Nyika yeU.S. inosimbirira kuti "tanga maparadza zvombo zvenyukiriya" uye inowedzera moto nekupa zvirango zveupfumi kuti zvavarikuda zviitike nenzira yekumanikidzira, uye kunyange kuramba kupa "chiziviso chekupera kwehondo,"" Ri akadaro.
"Mafungiro ekuti zvirango zveupfumi zvinogona kuita kuti tigwadame zviroto zvisina maturo zvinoitwa nevanhu vasinganyatsotiziva.
Asi dambudziko riripo nderekuti zvirango zveupfumi zviri kuwedzeresa kusavimba kwedu navo."
Ri haana kutaura nezveurongwa hwekuitwa kwemusangano wechipiri pakati paKim naTrump uyo mutungamiriri weU.S. akanga ataura nezvavo kuSangano reMubatanidzwa weNyika Dzose mukutanga kwevhiki.
Gurukota iri panzvimbo pezvo rakataura nezvemisangano mitatu pakati paKim nemutungamiriri weSouth Korean Moon Jae-in mumwedzi mishanu yapfuura uye akawedzera kuti: "Dai varikubatanidzwa munhau iyi yekuparadzwa kwezvombo zvenyukiriya vaiveSouth Korea kwete U.S., kuparadzwa kwezvombo zvenyukiriya muKorea kungadai kusina kusvika pamakakatanwa aya."
Kunyange zvakadaro, matauriro aRi paaipa mashoko ake anga akasiyana zvikuru nematauriro aakaita gore rapera, paaitaura kuU.N. Pamusangano wavo kuti hurongwa hwekukanda zvombo munyika yeU.S. nemichina yokuposhera zvombo yeNorth Korea kwange kusingadzivisiki pashure pekunge "VaPurezidhendi Vakaipa" Trump ati Kim "murume ari muchimutundumusere" ari parwendo kuenda kunozviuraya.
Gore rino paMusangano weNyika Dzepasi Pose, Trump, uyo gore rapera akavimbisa "kuparadza zvachose" North Korea, akatura mashoko ekurumbidza panaKim nekuda kweushingi hwake mukutora matanho ekusiya zvombo, asi akati pachine basa rakakura rinoda kuitwa uye zvirango zveupfumi zvinofanira kuramba zviripo kusvikira North Korea yaparadza zvombo zvayo zvenyukiriya.
Nemusi weChitatu, Trump akati akanga asingazivi kuti izvi zvaizotora nguva yakareba sei, achiti "Kunyange zvikatora makore maviri, matatu kana mwedzi mishanu - hazvina basa."
China neRussia dzinokurudzira kuti U.N. Security Council inofanira kuripa Pyongyang nekuda kwematanho akatorwa.
Zvisinei, U.S. Secretary of State Mike Pompeo akaudza weU.N. Security Council nemusi weChina kuti: "Kuiswa zvizere kwezvirango zveupfumi zveSecurity Council kunofanira kuitwa zvakasimba pasina kukundikana kusvikira taona kuti kuparadzwa kwezvombo zvenyukiriya kwaitwa zvizere, kwapedzwa uye kwatsimikidzirwa."
Sangano reSecurity Council rakaita chisarudzo chekupa North Korea zvirango zveupfumi kubvira mugore ra2006 nechinangwa chekuvhiringidza kupinda kwemari inofambisira mberi mabasa aPyongyang ekugadzira zvombo zvenyukiriya, uye zvinoputika.
Pompeo akasangana naRi vari kunze kwemusangano weU.N. General Assembly uye mushure maizvozvo akataura kuti aizoshanyira Pyongyang zvakare mwedzi unotevera kugadzirira musangano wechipiri.
Pompeo akashanyira North Korea katatu nechekare gore rino asi rwendo rwake rwekupedzisira haruna kufamba zvakanaka.
Akasiya Pyongyang mwedzi waChikunguru achiti fambiro mberi yakaitwa, pangopera maawa mashoma North Korea yakatanga kumushora ichiti aipa "zvikumbiro sezvematsotsi."
North Korea yakatsidzira mumusangano wavakaita naMoon mwedzi uno kuti yaizoparadza nzvimbo yezvombo zvinoitwa zvekukandwa uyewo muzinda wenyukiriya kana nyika yeUnited States ikatora "matanho anoenderana."
Akati Kim akange amuudza "matanho anoenderana" aaida anotii vimbiso yechengeteko iyo Trump akatsidzira muSingapore uye zviito zvekugadzirisa ukama neWashington.
Vadzidzi vepaHarvard voita kosi mukutora zororo rakakwana
Kosi itsva paYunivhesiti yeHarvard gore rino ndeyekuti vasati vagirajuweta vawane nguva yekurara yakawanda nechinangwa chekurwisana netsika yekushandisa zvinwiwa zvinopedza hope kuti vaverenge 'husiku hwose.'
Nzvimbo iyi yedzidzo yakaona kuti vadzidzi vepayunivhesiti iyi yemberi pasi rose kazhinji havana chavanoziva panhau yezvinhu zvakakosha nezvekuzvitarisira pachavo.
Charles Czeisler, muzvinafundo panhau dzekurapa kwehope paHarvard Medical School uye achishandira paBrigham and Women's Hospital, akaronga kosi iyi, iyo yaanofunga kuti ndiyo yekutanga yerudzi urwu muUS.
Akakurudzirwa kutanga kosi iyi mushure mekunge apa hurukuro yezvazvinoita mune zvedzidzo kana munhu akasawana nguva yakakwana.
'Mushure mekunge yapera mumwe musikana akauya kwandiri ndokuti: 'Sei ndakutanga kuudzwa izvi ikozvino ini ndatove mugore rangu rekupedza?'
Akati hapana mumwe munhu akange ambomuudza nezvekukosha kwekurara - izvo zvakandishamisa,' akaudza The Telegraph.
Kosi iyi, yauya kekutanga gore rino, inotsanungura kuvadzidzi kukosha kwekuti kuva netsika dzakanaka pakurara kunobatsira sei mune zvedzidzo uye pakumhanya, kubatanidzawo pakuvandudza hutano hwavo.
Paul Barreira, muzvinafundo anoona nezvemashandiro epfungwa wepaHarvard Medical School uye ari muridzi wechikamu chezveutano cheyunivhesiti iyi, akati yunivhesiti yasarudza kutanga kosi itsva pashure pekunge vaona kuti vana vakanga vachishaiswa nguva yekurara mukati mesvondo.
Kosi iyi inoitwa kweawa imwe chete inobatanidza kuitwa kwetumabasa twekukurukurirana
Mune chimwe chikamu pane mufananidzo wekamuri rakakura rinorarwa nevadzidzi, umo vadzidzi vanogona kudzvanya pamakapu ekofi, maketeni, vadzidzisi nemabhuku vachifanira kuudzwa nezvekushata kwezvimwiwa zvinodzinga hope nemwenje uye kuti kukwanisa kwemunhu kuita zvekumhanya kunokanganiswa sei nekusarara zvakakwana, uye kukosha kwekuva nepurogiramu yakanaka yekurara.
Mune chimwe chikamu, varikutora rutivi vanoudzwa nezvekuti kusawana nguva yakakwana yekurara kunowedzera sei mikana yekubatwa nezvirwere zvemoyo, kusituroka, kuora mwoyo uye gomarara.
Mepu yenzvimbo yechikoro, ine mavanotandarira, pashure vari kutora rutivi vokurudzirwa kuti vafunge nezvepurogiramu yavo yezuva nezuva.
'Tinoziva kuti hazvichinji maitiro evadzidzi pakarepo.
Asi tinodavira kuti vanekodzero yekuziva - sekodzero yauinayo yekuziva kuti kusarudza kusvuta fodya kwakaipirei kuutano,' akawedzera kudaro muzvinafundo Czeisler.
Katsika kekudada nekuti 'ndinopedza usiku hwose' kachiripo, akadaro, achiwedzera kuti zvigadzirwa zvemazuva ano nekuwedzera kwezvinotarisirwa pavadzidzi kunoreva kuti kushayikwa kwenguva yekurara chinetso chiri kukura.
Kuva nechokwadi chekuti warara zvakakwana, zvakanaka, kunofanira kuva ‘chombo chepachiwande’ pakurwisana nekuzvidya mwoyo, kupera simba nerutyo, akadaro - uye kudzivisa kuisa mutoro, sezvo kusarara zvakakwana kuchiisa pfungwa pakuziya kuchiita kuti igare nenzara.
Raymond So, uyo ane makore 19 achibva kuCalifornia ari kuita zvidzidzo zvechemical and physical biology, akabatsira Muzvinafundo Czeisler kuronga kosi iyi, pashure pekuita chimwe chezvidzidzo zvake gore rapera pagore rake rekutanga paHarvard.
Akati kosi iyi yakamuvhura maziso uye yakamukurudzira kuti kosi yacho iitwe pachikoro chose.
Danho rinotevera, anovimba kudaro, nderekukumbira vadzidzi vakambogurajuweta kuti vapedze kuita kosi yakadai vasati vauya pachikoro ichi chine mukurumbira.
Muzvinafundo Czeisler akakarakadza kuti vadzidzi vanofanira kuisa bhero rinovayeuchidza nguva yekurara, uye yekumuka, uye kungwaririra ngozi yekushandisa ‘mwenje webhuruu’ unobuditswa nezvigadzirwa zvemagetsi neMASIKIRINI, uyo unobvisa chido chekurara, zvichikonzera chinetso chokubatwa nehope.
Livingston 1 - 0 Rangers: Chibodzwa chaMenga chodonhedza vakomana vaGerrard
Rangers yokundwa zvakare pamutambo wayakashanya apo bhora rakaroverwa mumambure naDolly Menga rakaita kuti divi raGerrard iro range rakasekesa rikundwe nezvibodzwa1-0 paLivingston.
Divi rechikwata cheIbrox raitarisira kukunda kwekutanga kubvira pakukundwa kwarakaitwa nezvibodzwa 4-1 munaKukadzi paSt Johnstone, asi chikwata chaGary Holt chakawedzera kukundwa kwepiri kwechikwata chaGerrard mumitambo 18 semurayiridzi kuchisiya divi rake rave shure nezvibodzwa zvisere kune chikwata chiri kutungamirira pamutambo weLadbrokes Premiership cheHearts.
Menga akaroverera mumambure mumaminitsi manomwe vasati vaenda pachikamu chepiri uye vatambi vechikwata cheRangers avo vainge vasisina tariro vaitaridzika kuti zvaizovaomera kudzorera.
Panguva apo chikwata cheRangers chaderera chichiva panzvimbo yechitanhatu, chikwata cheLivingston chakwira kuve panzvimbo yechitatu uye chingori kumashure kwechikwata cheHibernian nemusiyano wezvibodzwa chete.
Uye panogona kuve nerimwe dambudziko kuchikwata cheRangers sezvo anotambira nechepamutsetse Calum Spence aifanira kurapwa chironda chemumusoro pashure pekunge chimwe chinhu chakandwa kubva nechekunze chichimutema.
Gerrard akachinja vatambi muchikwata chake kanokwana kasere icho chakatsvaira chikwata cheAyr mumutambo wechikamu chekupedzisira cheMukombe weBetfred.
Holt, kune rimwe rutivi, akapinda nevatambi weLivi 11 avo vakatora chibodzwa kuchikwata cheHearts svondo rapfuura uye anogona kunge akafadzwa nenzira iyo mazano ake pakutamba akatambudza vavaikwkwidzana navo pachikamu chimwe nechimwe.
Chikwata cheRangers chaigona kunge chakatungamira pakugara nebhora asi chikwata cheLivingston chakaita zvakanakisa nekushandisa mukana webhora rachaivana.
Vaigona kunge vakakanda chibodzwa pamaminitsi maviri panguva apo Menga akapinda nepakati pevakwikwidzi ndokukandira Scott Pittman bhora richitambidzwazve kunaAllan McGregor uyo aifanira kugohwesa asi mutambi uyu anotambira nechepakati akatambisa mukana nekukandira bhora kure.
Bhora rakakawiva naKeaghan Jacobs richipinda nechemukati-kati rakasvika panaCraig Halkett asi dhifenda wake Alan Lithgow ndokurivhikira nechekure kwebango rekumashure.
Rangers yakadzikamisa zvinhu pamatambiro ayaiita vachiratidza kuva netariro kupfuura kuzvivimba pamatambiro avo mumutambo wetatu wechikamu chekupedzisira.
Alfredo Morelos ainyatsogutsikana kuti aifanira kupiwa pena muchikamu chechina cheawa apo iye naSteven Lawless vakaroverana asi muzvinapembe Steven Thomson akaramba chikumbiro chemutambi uyu wekuColombia .
Rangers yakangokwanisa kurovera zvakananga kugedhi kaviri bedzi muchikamu chekutanga asi gori uyo aimbotambira Ibrox anonzi Liam Kelly haana kumbovhiringidzwa nebhora rakatungwa naLassana Coulibaly uye nekabhora kakaroverwa naOvie Ejaria .
Kunyange chibodzwa chekutanga chechikwata cheLivi chemaminiti 34 chaiita sechaipesana nenzira inodiwa yematambiro, hapana anogona kuramba kuti vaikodzera kuchiwana tichitarisa matambiro avaiita.
Zvakare chikwata cheRangers chakatadza kushandisa nemazvo bhora rakabva kunaJacobs.
Scott Arfield haana kutirimuka apo Declan Gallagher akapira bhora kunaScott Robinson, uyo akanonoka kuona Menga kuti angomwisa zvirinyore.
Gerrard akachinjanisa Coulibaly naRyan Kent panguva yekuzorora uye kuchinjanisa uku kwakapotsa kwaunza pundutso nekukurumidza sezvo mutambi uyu wekumapeto akapira bhora kuna Morelos asi Kelly uyo aitamba zvaimwisa mvura akamhanya achibva pagedhi kuti anovhara bhora.
Asi Livingston yakaramba ichidhonzera chikwata ichi chevashanyi kuti vatambe nenzira yayaida iyo, sezvo Lithgow naHalkett vairamba vachisimudza mabhora marefu mushure merimwe.
Divi raHolt ringadai rakawedzera kutungamirira kwaro muzvikamu zvekupedzisira asi McGregor akatamba zvakanaka kurambidza Jacobs mushure mekunge Lithgow atunga bhora richibuda kunze ari nechepakona.
Mutambi akatsiva mumwe mutambi wechikwata cheRangers anonzi Glenn Middleton akachemera kupihwa pena mutambo watofamba paakavhiringidzana naJacobs asi Thomson akaramba zvakare.
Karenda yezviitiko zvinokosha: Mugadziri weGeiger Counter
Parizvino peji yepaKarenda yedu yezviitiko zvinokosha "yeMangwanani eSvondo": Gunyana 30, 1882, makore 136 apfuura, uye PACHIVERENGWA ... zuva iro aizove nyanzvi yephysics Johannes Wilhelm "Hans" Geiger akaberekwa muGermany.
Geiger akatanga kugadzira nzira yekuyera nayo simba rinoburitswa neatomu, hunyanzvi hwakaita kuti pave nechigadzirwa chinonzi Geiger Counter.
Turusi yezvesayenzi kubvira kare, chigadzirwa cheGeiger Counter chakavawo chigadzirwa chinomiririra tsika nemagariro, sezviri mumutambo wekumakore ekuma 1950 unonzi "Bells of Coronado," vakaburitsa vatambi vaisaratidzika kuve nyanzvi dzesayenzi Roy Rogers uye Dale Evans avo vakagadzira turusi raisungirirwa pamombe:
Murume: "Ndochii ichocho pasi pezuva?"
Rogers: "Iyi iGeiger Counter, inoshandiswa kuona pane masaisai anobudiswa nematombo, akadai seyureniyamu.
Ukaisa magudzanzwi aya, unogona kunzwa zvinoitika panobuditswa simba remaatomu nemasaisai ari mumatombo."
Evans: "Iti, chokwadi zvave kunzwika manje!"
"Hans" Geiger akafa mugore ra1945, kwangosara mazuva mashomanana kuti zuva rake rekuzvarwa rechi63 risvike.
Asi chigadzirwa chine zita rake chichipo.
Nhomba yegomarara itsva inodzidzisa masoja emuviri ‘kuona’ masero akaipa
Nhomba yegomarara itsva inodzidzisa masoja emuviri ‘kuona’ masero akaipa omauraya
Nhomba iyi inodzidzisa masoja emuviri kuziva masero akaipa senzira yekurapa
Nzira yacho inobatanidza kutora masero emasoja emuviri kubva pamurwere, ochinjwa murabhoratari involves
Anobva ‘aona’ puroteini inowanzowanikwa mumagomarara akawanda obva adzorerwa mumuviri
Nhomba iri pakuedzwa iyi iri kuratidza kushanda zvakanaka muvarwere vane ndudzi dzegomarara dzakawanda.
Mumwe mukadzi akarapwa pachishandiswa nhomba iyi, iyo inodzidzisa masoja emuviri kuziva masero akaipa, anoti gomarara rake remuchibereko rakapera kwemwedzi inodarika 18.
TNzira yacho inobatanidza kutorwa kwemasero emasoja emuviri kubva kumurwere, ochinjwa murabhoratari kuitira kuti “aone” puroteini inowanzowanikwa mumagomarara akawanda inonzi HER2, uye masero acho odzorerwa mumuviri.
Muzvinafundo Jay Berzofsky, weUS National Cancer Institute muBethesda, iri muMaryland, akati: "Zvakabuda zviri kuratidza kuti tine nhomba iri kuratidza kuti ichashanda zvakanaka."
HER2 "inobvisa kukura kwemhando dzegomarara dzakawanda," dzinosanganisira dzemazamu, muchibereko, mapapu uye dzemumatumbu, Muzvinafundo Berzofsky akatsanangura.
Nzira yakafanana yekutora masero emasoja emuviri kubva kuvarwere “kwavekumadzidzisa” kurwisa masero egomarara yakashandawo mukurapa mhando inonzi leukaemia.
Kanye West Otanga Kukanda Mashoko eKushora Mukutsigira Trump, Akapfeka Heti Yakanyorwa kuti MAGA, Mushure Mekuonekwa paSNL.
Hazvina Kufamba Zvakanaka
Kanye West akasvereredzwa ari munotepfenyurwa panguva yechirongwa cheSaturday Night Live pashure pekuridza zvine mutinhimira achirumbidza mutungamiri wenyika weU.S. Donald Trump uye achiti achakwikwidza kupinda pachigaro zvakare mugore ra2020.
Pashure pekuridza mhanzi yake yechitatu pausiku uhwu, inonzi Ghost Town apo ange akapfeka kepesi yakanyorwa kuti Ita Kuti America Ive Nemukurumbira, ndokutaura achishora webato remaDemocrats uye achisimbisirazve kutsigira kwaanoita Trump.
"Nguva zhinji pandinotaura nemunhu werudzi rwechichena vanoti: "Sei uchifarira Trump, ane rusaruraganda?"
Zvisinei, dai ndainetseka nezvenhau yerusaruraganda ndingadai ndakabuda muAmerica kare kare," akadaro.
SNL yakatanga shoo iyi nekamutambo kaibuditsa Matt Damon uyo ari shasha muHollywood achitsvinyira zvakaitwa naBrett Kavanaugh paaipa huchapupu paDre reSeneti reDzimhosva nezvepomerwo dzaari kupihwa naChristine Blasey Ford dzekubatwa zvisina kunaka mune zvepabonde.
Kunyange zvazvo kwaisawe kutepfenyura, zvakaitwa naWest zvakadhaunirodwa padandemutande rekutandara kwevanhu naChris Rock.
Hazvina kujeka kana Rock aida kutsvinyira West mune zvaakatumira izvi.
Uyewo, West akanyunyuta kuvateereri achiti akasangana nenguva yakaoma asati akwira panhandare nezvemapfekero aainge akaita mumusoro.
"Vakandibata zvisina kunaka ndisati ndakwira pano.
Vakati, 'usaenda kunevanhu wakapfeka heti iyoyo.'
"Vakandibata zvisina kunaka ndisati ndakwira pano.
Uye vakati ndiri panzvimbo inonyudza," akadaro, mukuwirirana neWashington Examiner.
West akapfuurira: "Ndichaona nzvimbo inonyudza?" achiti "ndichachapfeka kepisi yegamba rangu, nekuti izvi zvinoreva kuti hamugoni kundiudza zvekuita. Munoda kuti nyika yose ifambire mberi here?
Edzai kuva nerudo."
Zvaakataura zvakaita kuti pave nekusvereredza kubva kuvateereri kanokwana kaviri uye nhengo dzeSNL dzaibudisa purogiramu yacho vakaratidza kunyara nazvo, yakashuma kudaro Variety, mumwe munhu pakati pavo achiudza vakaburitsa mashoko aya: "Nhepfenyuro yese yakati zii kunyarara."
West akaunzwa kwatosara mazuva mashoma kutsiva muimbi Ariana Grande, uyo ane mukomana waaimbodanana naye, muimbi Mac Miller uyo akange afa mazuva mashoma apfuura.
West akakanga mate mukamnwa vakawanda nenziyo yake inonzi Ndinoida, akapfeka seBhodhoro rePerrier.
West akatsigirwa nemutungamiriri weTPUSA, Candace Turner uyo akanyora paTwitter kuti: "Kune uyo anemoyo wakashinga: TINOKUTENDA NEKUMIRISANA NEVERUZHINJI."
Asi aitungamira chirongwa ichi Karen Hunter kanyora patwitter kuti West "ange ari kungova sezvaari uye izvi zvakanaka zvikuru."
"Asi ndakasarudza KUSAPEMBEDZA mumwe munhu (nekutenga mimhanzi yake kana zvipfeko kana kutsigira "hunyanzvi" hwake) uyo wandinofunga kuti ari kugashira nekuparadzira mafungiro ane ngozi kunharaunda yangu.
Akasununguka.
Sezvatingorivo," akawedzera.
Shoo isati yatanga, muimbi uyu akanga azivisa paTwitter kuti akanga achinja zita rake, achiti parizvino “akange ave uyo aimbozivikanwa saKanye West."
Haasi muimbi wekutanga kuchinja zita rake uye anotevera matsimba aDiddy, uyo anozivikanwa zvakare saPuff Daddy, Puffy uye P Diddy.
Mumwe wake mune zvekuimba, Snoop Dogg aimbova nezita rekuti Snoop Lion uye chaizvoizvo mushabvu aive gamba mune zvemimhanzi Prince, akachinja zita rake kuve chiratidzo uye panguva iyo aizivikanwa sekuti Prince.
Mutongo wemhosva yekuda kuuraya pashure pekubaya kwakaitika munzvimbo yekudyira iri muBelfast
Murume ane makore 45 akapiwa mhosva yekuda kuuraya pashure pekubayiwa kwemumwe murume mune imwe nzvimbo yekudyira iri kumabvazuva kweBelfast nemusi weChishanu.

Shasha mumutambo weGame of Thrones anonzi Kit Harington oshora maonero ane ngozi ekuratidzika semurume chaiye
Kit Harington anozivikanwa nekuda kwekuvheyesa bakatwa kwaaiita ari Jon Snow mumutambo wemasimba masimba weHBO wezvikamu zvikamu zveGame of Thrones.
Asi mutambi uyu, ane makore 31, ataura achishoropodza mashoko ekuti anoda kuonekwa semurume akasimba chaizvo, achiti maitiro iwayo mumaterevhizheni anoita kuti vakomana vechidiki vafunge kuti vanofanira kunge vasingajairiki kuti varemekedzwe.
Achitaura neveThe Sunday Times Culture, Kit akati anotenda kuti 'pane zvisina kumira zvakanaka' uye ndokubvunza nzira yekugadzirisa chinetso chemaonero ane ngozi ekuratidzika semurume chaiye munguva ino pa #MeToo.
Kit, uyo achangobva kuroora shasha biyake mumutambo weGame of Thrones anonzi Rose Leslie, uyo anewo makore 31, akabvuma kuti anonzwa 'zvakasimba' kuti nyaya iyi inoda kugadziriswa.
'Pachezvangu, ndinonzwa zvakasimba, parizvino kuti - tiri kurasika papi panyaya yekuva murume akasimba?,' akadaro.
'Zvii zvatange tiri kudzidzisa varume pavainge vari kukura, pamusoro pedambudziko ratiri kuona izvozvi?'
Kit anofunga kuti terevhizheni dzinogona kuti dziinewo chekuita nekuwedzera kwemaonero ane ngozi ekuva murume chaiye tichitenda chaizvo vanhu vayo avo vari varume chaivo.
Akawedzera: 'Ndezvipi zviri muropa uye zvekuita zvekudzidziswa?
Zvii zviri kudzidziswa paTV, uye mumigwagwa, zvinoita kuti vakomana vechidiki vanzwe sekuti vanofanira kuratidzika nenzira iyi semurume?
Ndinofunga kuti uyu ndiwo mumwe wemimwe mibvunzo mikuru munguva yedu - tingazvichinja sei?
Nekuti kutaura zvazviri pane chimwe chinhu chisina kumira zvakanaka pavarume vechidiki.'
Mubvunzurudzo iyi akabvumawo kuti akange asisachavaniki pamitambo yakarongerwa mberi uye yakatopedzwa yepaGame of Thrones apo mutambo wacho uchapera mumwaka wekupisa unotevera, achiti 'akanga asisachaiti zvehondo uye zvemabhiza'.
Kubvira mumwedzi waMbudzi Kit achatamba mukumutsiridzwa kwemutambo wakanyorwa naSam Shepard unonzi True West unova nyaya pamusoro pemubiki wefirimu iri nemukoma wake, anova mbavha.
Mutambi uyu munguva pfupi yapfuura akazivisa kuti anoona kusangana kwaakaita nemudzimai wake Rose sechinhu chakanyanya kunaka chakabuda mumutambo weGame of Thrones.
'Ndakasangana nemudzimai wangu mumutambo uyu, nenzira iyi wakandipa mhuri yangu yemunguva yemberi, uye upenyu hwangu kubva ipapo,' akadaro.
Rose aitamba saYgritte, uyo aidiwa naKit uyo aitamba saJon Snow, mumutambo uyo une zvikamu-zvikamu wekudanana wakahwinha mubayiro weEmmy.
Vaviri ava vakaroorana mumwedzi waChikunguru 2018 pamusha pemhuri yaLeslie muScotland.
HIV/Aids: China yoshuma kuwedzera kweuwandu hwevanhu vane utachiona nezvikamu 14 kubva muzana
China yazivisa kukwira nezvikamu 14 kubva muzana pauwandu hwevagari wayo vari kurarama nehutachiona hweHIV neAids.
Vanhu vanopfuura 820,000 vakabatwa nehutachiona uhwu munyika iyi, vakuru-vakuru mune zveutano vakadaro.
Vanoda kusvika 40,000 vakabatwa vaine hutachiona uhwu mumwedzi mitanhatu yekutanga yegore ra2018 chete.
Vazhinji vakatapurira utachiona uhwu kupfurikidza nekuita zvebonde, zvichisiyanisa nezvaiitika kare.
Sekuziva kwazvinoitwa, utachiona hweHIV hunopararira nekukurumidza chaizvo mune dzimwe nzvimbo dzeChina nekuda kwekuisirwa ropa rine utachiona.
Asi vanhu vanotapurirwa utachiona hweHIV nenzira iyi hwaderedzwa zvekuda kusvika pazero chaipo, vakuru-vakuru munezveutano wekuChina vakadaro pamusangano wakaitirwa mupurovhinzi yeYunnan.
Gore negore, zvisine, uwandu hwevanhu vari kurarama neutachiona hweHIV neAids muChina hwawedzera nevanhu 100,000.
Kutapurira utachiona hweHIV kupfurikidza nekuita zvebonde inyaya huru pavagari veLGBT wekuChina.
Hungochani hwakabvumirwa zviri pamutemo muChina muna 1997, asi kusarurwa kwevanoita zveLGBT kuri kunzi kuri kuramba kuchikwira.
Nekuda kwekuomerera patsika dzechinyakare dzenyika iyi, tsvakurudzo dzakapa fungidziro yekuti zvikamu 70 kusvika ku90 muzana zvevarume vanorara nevarume vanozongopedzisira varoora munhukadzi.
Kutapurira zvirwere kwakanyanya kunobva pakusashandiswa zvizere kwezvinodzivirira mukuitwa kwebonde kwendudzi idzi.
Kubvira mugore ra2003, hurumende yeChina yakavimbisa kuwaniswa kwemishonga yekurapa HIV kumunhu vese senzira yekurwisana nedambudziko iri.

Kuongorora muvhi inonzi Johnny English Strikes Again - inyaya isinganyatsosetsa yekusora kwaRowan Atkinson
Yave setsika parizvino kutarisa nezvekukosha kweBrexit mufirimu chero idzva iro rakarerekera kuBritain uye rinoratidzika serinoshanda pakumutsiridzwa uku kwemutambo weJohnny English wokusetsa une masimba-masimba wakadzokororwa - wakatanga mugore ra2003 naJohnny English uye kuchuchiswa mugore ra2011 naJohnny English Azvarwazve.
Kuti mashoko ekutsvinya panhau yekuva mapenzi kwedu kuri pachena ichava nhau itsva yemukana wekutengesa kunze wenyika?
Chero pamwero upi zvavo, Johnny English uyo ane maziso akabuda, ari dofo rine uso husina kumira mushe akapiwa zvakare mvumo patsva yekuvhiringidza zvinhu kepiri - zita rake pachake richiratidza kupfuura zvose kuti chisikwa chinosekesa chakagadzirirwa vanhu vasingatauri Chirungu vanoenda munzvimbo dzinoonekwa mafirimu.
Angoriwo zvake mumiririri wemadzenga vepachivande uyo pasinei nevavariro dzake dzisiri dzechokwadi dzekunaka kwakada kufanana zvishoma nekwaClouseau, kumhanya kwaVaBean uye hukuru hwemarara iwayo kuchibatanidza mashoko mamwe chete kumusoro wekuti Chariots of Fire pakuvhurwa kwemutambo weOlympics muLondon wa2012.
Anobvawo zvakare pamurume asingazivikanwe anoshanya uye vepasirose Atkinson uyo akambotamba mumitambo yekushambadzira yakanganwika yeBarclaycard TV, kuchisiya zvinhu zvisina kumira zvakanaka kwaari.
Pane chiitiko chimwe chete kana zviviri chinofadza nekuda kwekushanya uku kweJE kuchangobva kuitwa.
Ndakafarira Johnny English achienda kune chikopokopo akapfeka sutu yekuzvidzivirira kuzvombo yachinyakare uye mabhemba echikopokopo achitenderera pamusoro peheremeti yake.
Chipo chaAtkinson pakuita mitambo yekungoita zvinhu akanyarara ichisetsa kuri kuonekwawo, asi maiitiro ake haana simba uye anoratidzwa pamwero wekuwedzeredza, zvikuru pamafirimu "asingaitwi zvekuseka" akadai se007 uye Mission Impossible ayo pachayo anoratidza mitambo yekusetsa seyokushandisa.
Manzwikiro ayo akanyanyokodzera vechidiki kupfuura vanhu vakuru, uye kwandiri mafirimu aJohnny English ekuedza zvinhu zvinosetsa haana kunyatsorongerwa zvitsva uye kuva nemusoro kusiyana neya Atkinson yaanenge akasingatauri achiekita saBean.
Maonero akadzika midzi parizvino ndeekuti Great Britain iri mudambudziko guru.
Mbavha inoshandisa makombuyuta yakapinda pachivande mumawebhusaiti ezvakavanzika zvikuru yesori, ichiburitsa mazita evarikushandira hurumende yeBritain pamabasa ekusora, izvo zvakagumbura vashandi ava - rinova basa diki rinonzwisa urombo raKevin Eldon.
Ndiro dambudziko guru rarova mukuru wemakurukota ehurumende uyo anozvikudza uye ari kurwiswa, uyo atorasikirwa nechekare nemukurumbira wake mune zvematongerwo enyika: Emma Thompson anoita zvaanokwanisa zvakanaka paanoita saTeresa May asi hapana zvakanyorwa zvizhinji zviripo zvekushanda nazvo.
Vapizano vake vanomutsvakira mashoko akavanzika vakamuudza kuti sezvo mashandiro emusori mumwe nemumwe akanganisika, anofanira kudzosa kubasa mumwe munhu akasiya basa kare.
Uye izvi zvinoreva kuonana naJohnny English pachake, uyo ave kushanda semukuru wechikoro pahurongwa hwekubhadharana hwakanaka zvikuru, asi kudzidzisa pasina zvinyorwa kuti munhu angava sei mushandi vepachivande: pachazonakidza ipapa, sezvo English achipa mhando yeSchool of Rock yezvidzidzo zvekusora.
English akangoerekana atorwa kuWhitehall pamusangano wekukurumidzira ndokusanganiswa neakambomubatsira kwenguva refu Bough, uyo akashandiswazve naBen Miller.
Bough ave murume akaroora parizvino, akatorana nemukuru wemauto emumvura, mukadzi wepamusoro-soro uyo Vicki Pepperdine akashandiswa zvishoma.
Saka mabasa ehushamwari hwekuvhiringidza zvinhu kune vanoshandira Anoremekedzwa kuita Mabasa Ekusora ave kuratidzwa, pachionekwa musikana waOlga Kurylenko uyo anengozi anonzi Ophelia Bulletova.
Panguva ino, mukuru wemakurukota ari kunyengedzwa zvine ngozi nemurume ari mubhizimusi rezvemakombiyuta anemabhiriyoni emari anoremekedzwa uyo ari kuti anogona kugadzirisa nyaya dzanetsa dzemakombiyuta muBritain: munyengedzi Jason Volta, yakatambwa naJake Lacy.
English naBough vanotanga basa ravo vachiita sevadiri muresitorendi yezvokudya zvechiFrench; vanokonzera bongozozo vachotora zvisina tsarukano kachikepe kanodhura keVolta; uye English anokonzeresa batawabata apo anoedza kushandisa magunzanzwi emunzeve anoita kuti Aonekwe Pamakombiyuta kuti azive mamiriro akaita chivakwa cheVolta.
Kumira-mira kwose kwakabviswa pachikamu ichocho chekupedzisira, asi pasinei nehushamwari uye mhururu zviripo, pirogiramu yacho yose yakada kufanana neyevana yekid’s TV.
Yakakodzera zvikuru.
Uye pandinofunga nezvemamwe mafirimu aJohnny English ndinongofunga kuti: indasitiri yezvemafirimu muBritain ingatadza here kupa basa Rowan Atkinson rinonyatsoenderana nechipo chake?
Labour yoramba kuti iri kuita hurongwa hwekuti vanhu vekuBritain vashande kwemazuva mana pavhiki asi vobhadharwa mazuva mashanu
Bato raJeremy Corbyn reLabour riri kuda kuona hurongwa husina kujairika uhwo huchaita kuti vanhu vekuBritain vashande kwemazuva mana pasvondo - asi vobhadharwa mazuva mashanu.
Bato iri ririkunzi ririkuda kuti mashefu pamakambani ayambutsire kuvashandi mari inowanikwa nekushandiswa kwemapurogiramu epamakombiyuta e(AI) nekuvapa rimwe zuva rekuzorora.
Izvi zvinoita kuti vashandi vanakidzwe nekuva nekupera kwesvondo kwemazuva matatu - asi vachipiwa muhoro wakangofanana.
Kuri kubva mashoko kunoti pfungwa iyi ‘ichapindirana’ nepfungwa dzebato iri mune zveupfumi uye hurongwa hwavo hwekuchinja maitirwo ezvinhu munyika kuti zvinakire vashandi.
Kuchinjira kupfungwa yekushanda mazuva mana pavhiki kwakatsigirwa paMusangano weMasangano Anomiririra Vashandi senzira iyo vashandi vanogona kushandisa mukana wekuchinja kwehupfumi nemashandiro.
Nhengo yakabvira kare iri muBato reLabour yakaudza weThe Sunday Times: 'Ongororo yemutemo uyu iri kutarisirwa kuziviswa gore risati rapera.
'Hazviitiki muhusiku humwe chete asi kushanda mazuva mana pasvondo ipfungwa inoenderana nemaonero ebato pakuenzanisazve upfumi kuti hunakire vashandi kusanganisira hurongwa hwebato panhau dzezvemaindasitiri.'
Bato reLabour handiro rekutanga kusarudza pfungwa iyi, sezvowo Bato reGreen Party rakavimbisa kushandwa kwemazuva mana pasvondo panguva apo raitsvaka rutsigiro musarudzo dzemutungamiriri wenyika dza2017.
Zvisinei, pfungwa iyi haisi kutsigirwa nenhengo dzose dzeBato reLabour.
Mutauriri weBato reLabour akati: 'Kushanda mazuva mana pasvondo hausi mutemo webato uye pfungwa iyi haisi kufungwa nezvayo nebato.'
Shadow Chancellor John McDonnell akashandisa mukana wemusangano wakaitwa svondo rapfuura weLabour kupa maonero ake ekuti mafambisirwo ebasa munyika achinjwe kuti anakire vanhu.
VaMcDonnell vakati vakanga vakazvipira kudzosa masimba kubva 'kuvaridzi vemakambani vasingazivikanwi' uye 'vari kuwana mhindu' pamakambani anotengesa zvekushandisa.
Hurongwa hwachancellor uyu hunoreva kuti varidzi varipo iko zvino wemakambani emvura vanogona kusapihwa huridzi huzere sezvo hurumende yeLabour ichigona 'kuhutapudza' nekuda kwezvikonzero zvekuitwa kwezvinhu zvisina kunaka.

Chii chinonzi Mutambo weGlobal Citizen Festival uye Pane Zvawakaita Kuderedza Hurombo Here?
Mugovera uno New York ichaitirwa mutambo weGlobal Citizen Festival, mutambo wepagore wezvemimhanzi uyo une ndandanda yeshasha dzevaimbi dzinonakidza dzicharidza uyewo nedonzvo rinofadza; rekupedza horombo pasi rose.
Parizvino mugore rawo rechinomwe, mutambo uyu weGlobal Citizen Festival uchaunganidza makumi ezviuru evanhu paCentral Park's Great Lawn kwete kunonakidzwa chete nemabasa aJanet Jackson, Cardi B uye Shawn Mendes, asiwo kunosimudzira inzwi ravo nekuda kwedonzvo guru rechiitiko ichi rekupedza hurombo hwakanyanya panozosvika gore ra2030.
Mutambo weGlobal Citizen Festival, uyo wakatangwa mugore ra2012, wakabatana pamashandiro neGlobal Poverty Project, rinova boka repasirose rinetariro yekupedza hurombo nekuwedzera uwandu hwevanhu vari kurwisana nahwo.
Kuti uwane tiketi repachena rekupindisa pamutambo uyu (kunze kwekunge uchida kutenga tiketi reVanhu Vakakosha Zvikuru), vanopinda mumutambo uyu vanofanira kutanga vapedza ndandanda yetwumabasa, kana "zviito" zvakadai sekuzvipira, kutumira imeiri kumutungamiri wenyika, kufonera kana kutumira mashoko neimwewo nzira kuparadzira ruzivo rwechinangwa chavo chekupedza hurombo.
Asi mutambo uyu weGlobal Citizen vabudirira zvakadii tichitarira kuti vangosarirwa nemakore 12 kuti vapedze chinangwa chavo?
Kuti kupa vanhu mutambo wemahara ipfungwa here yakanaka yekunyengetedza vanhu kuti vakumbire kuti chimwe chinhu chiitwe, kana kuti ungoriwo mumwe muenzaniso "wenhimbe dzepamafoni" - vanhu vachiita sevari kukonzeresa kuti zvinhu zvifambe nekungosaina chikumbiro chepaindaneti kana kutumira meseji patwitter?
Kubvira muna2011, Global Citizen yakati yakanyora pasi “zviito” zvinokwana mamiriyoni 19 kubva kuvatsigiri wavo, kumanikidzira kuti zvinangwa zvavo zvakasiyana-siyana zviitwe.
Inoti zviito izvi zvakabetsera vatungamiri vedzinyika kuti vazivise nezveurongwa uye mitemo inogona kuburitsisa mari inodarika mabhiriyoni $37 iyo inogona kubatsira upenyu hwevanhu vanodarika mabhiriyoni 2.25 panozosvika 2030.
Gore ra2018 richangotanga, boka iri rakadoma mabasa nezviziviso zvinosvika ku390 zvakabva mumabasa avo, kuchitivo mari isiri pasi pemabhiriyoni $10 yayo yakatogoverwa kana kuti kuunganidzwa.
Boka iri rinofungidzira kuti mari iyi yakabatsira kuchinja hupenyu hwevanhu vanosvika mamiriyoni 649 kupota pasi rose.
Mamwe mabasa makuru anosanganisira reThe Power of Nutrition, mubatandzwa wekuU.K hwevari mumabhizimisi nevaiti vebasa vakazvipira “kubatsira vana kuti vakure kusvika pamwero chaivo,” vari kuvimbisa kupa nyika yeRwanda mari inosvika mamiriyoni $35 kubatsira kupedza dambudziko rekushayikwa kwezvokudya zvinovaka muviri munyika iyi pashure pekutumirwa mameseji epatwitter anosvika 4,700 kubva kuGlobal Citizens.
"Nerutsigiro kubva kuhurumende yeUK, vanobatsira nemari, hurumende dzemunyika, uye veGlobal Citizens vakangoita seve, tinogona kuita kuti kusaruramisira kuripo mumagariro evanhu kwekushayikwa kwezvokudya zvinovaka muviri kupere munhoondo," Mumiririri wesangano reThe Power of Nutrition Tracey Ullman akaudza boka raive rakaungana pamutambo uyu muLondon mwedzi waKubvumbi mugore ra2018.
Boka iri rakataurawo kuti pashure pezviito zvinokwana 5,000 zvekukumbira kuti U.K. ivandudze nyaya yekuwanikwa kwezvokudya zvinovaka muviri zvaanamai nevana, hurumende yakazivisa kuti yaizotsigira nemari pachirongwa ichi, chePower of Nutrition, icho chichabetsera vakadzi nevana vanosvika mamiriyoni 5 kuti wavane zvokudya zvinovaka muviri.
Mukupindura mumwe wemibvunzo pachikamu chewebhusaiti yavo cheMibvunzo Inovanzobvunzwa wekuti "chii chinoita kuti mufunge kuti tinogona kupedza hurombo hwakanyanya?"
Global citizen yakapindura kuti: "Richave basa ringuva refu uye rakaoma - pamwe pacho tichadonha uye kukundikana.
Asi, kungofanana nemapoka anorwira kodzero dzevanhu nemasangano anorwisa rusaruro munyia yeus, tichabudirira, nekuti tine simba rakakura kana tikabatana.
Janet Jackson, the Weeknd, Shawn Mendes, Cardi B, Janelle Monáe vari pakati pevachaita mitambo pamutambo wegore rino uchaitirwa muNew York, vachitandadzwa nevashanyi vanoti Deborra-Lee Furness uye Hugh Jackman.
US inogona kushandisa Mauto eMugungwa "kuvhara" kudzivisa kutengeswa kwezvinobuditsa simba remoto zveRussian kune dzimwe nyika - Munyori weHurumende Munyika
Washington inogona "kana zvichidikanwa" kushandisa Mauto ayo eMugungwa kudzivisa kuti zvinobuditsa simba remoto zvenyika yeRussia zvisvike kumisika, kusanganisira wenyika dzekuMabvazuva, Munyori weHurumende yeUS Ryan Zinke akataura kudaro, sezvakaratidzwa neMuongorori muWashington.
Zinke akati mabasa eRussia muSyria - sezvirikuonekwa, apo iri kuita mabasa ayo yapiwa kokero yekudaro nehurumende iri pamutemo - chinangwa chenhema chiri kupiwa kuti ipinde mumisika mitsva inoshandisa zvinobuditsa moto .
"Ndinovimba kuti chikonzero nei vari muNyika dzeKumabvazuva ndechekuti vatengese zvinobuditsa simba remoto sezvavanoita kumabvazuva kweEurope," ari kunzi akadaro.
Uye, mukuwirirana nezvakataurwa nemukuru uyu, pane nzira dzekumisa izvozvo.
"Nyika yeUnited States inokwanisa, ichishandisa Mauto eMugungwa, kuva nechokwadi chekuti nzira dzemugungwa dzakavhurwa, uye, kana zvichidikanwa, kuvhara, kuti vave nechokwadi chekuti zvinobuditsa simba remoto zvavo hazviendeswi kumusika," akadaro.
Zinke ange ari kupa hurukuro kune vange vari pachiitiko chakarongwa neveConsumer Energy Alliance, boka rinoshanda rakazvimirira rinozvitora "seizwi revanoshandisa simba remoto" muUS.
Akabva apinda panhau yekuenzanisa zviri kuitwa neWashington pakubata neRussia uye Iran, achiti zvakangofanana.
"Vavariro dzeIran uye Russia, kazhinji kana kuti kashoma, ndedzekushandisa zvizere uye kutsiva zvinobuditsa simba," akadaro, achidangidzira kuRussia se"inotinetsei zvishoma" ine hupfumi hwakavakirwa pasimba remarasha.
Mashoko aya akauya panguva apo hurumende yaTrump iri pahurongwa hwekuwedzera kutengesera dzimwe nyika huwandu hwegasi rekubikisa kuEurope, ichitsiva Russia, chinova chisarudzo chinoita kuti vanhu vemuEurope vashandise mari shoma pakutenga chigadzirwa ichi.
Nekuda kwechikonzero ichi, vakuru muhurumende yaTrump, kusanganisira Mutungamiriri weNyika yeUS Donald Trump pachake, vari kuedza kumanikidza Germany kuti ibude muhurongwa hwepaipi inotakura zvinhu yeNord Stream 2 “isinakukodzera”, iyo mukuwirirana naTrump, yakaita kuti Berlin ive “musungwa” weMoscow."
Moscow yakaramba ichiratidza kuti hurongwa hwemabhiriyoni $11 emadhora hweNord Stream 2, uhwo hurikutarsirwa kupeta kaviri huwandu hwezvinhu zvinotakurwa nepaipi parizvino kusvika kumabhiriyoni 110 cubic meters, hurongwa hwakanangana nezveupfumi chete.
VemuKremlin vanopikisana nazvo vachiti kushora kwakasimba kweWashington hurongwa uhwu kuri kusundwa chete nezvikonzero zvehupfumi uye muenzaniso wekukwikwidza nenzira isina kururama.
"Ndinovimba kuti tose tine maonero ekuti nhau yesimba remagetsi haifaniri kushandiswa pakumanikidzira uye vatengi vanofanira kusarudza vatengesi vakasununguka," Gurukota reZvemoto Aleksandr Novak akadaro pashure pemusangano waakaita neMunyori mune zveMoto Rick Perry muMoscow mumwedzi waGunyana.
Maonero eUS ashorwa neGermany, iyo yasimbisirazve kuzvipira kwayakaita pahurongwa uhwu.
Bato riri pamusoro munezvemabhizimusi muGermany, reFederation of German Industries (BDI), rataura kuti nyika yeUS inofanira kusiyana nemutemo wemaitirwa ezvinhu mune zvesimba remoto muEU uye zvibvumirano zvekudyidzana kweBerlin neMoscow.
"Ndinova nechinetso chakakura kana nyika yechitatu ikapindira mukufambiswa zvezvinhu zvinobuditsa simba remoto zvedu kuvatengi," Dieter Kempf, mukuru weFederation of German Industries (BDI) akadaro zvichitevera musangano uchangobva kuitwa pakati paGerman Chancellor Angela Merkel nemutungamiri wenyika yeRussia Vladimir Putin.
Elizabeth Warren "Achafungisisa" Nezvokukwikwidza Kuti Ave Mutungamiri Wenyika muna2020, Seneta wemuMassachusetts Anodaro
Seneta wemuMassachusetts Elizabeth Warren nemusi weMugovera akati "achafungisisa" nezvokukwikwidza kuti ave mutungamiri wenyika zvichitevera sarudzo dzevatungamiriri dzekutanga.
Pamusangano wepaHolyoke, muMassachusetts, Warren akasimbisira kuti achafunga nezvokukwikwidza.
"Ndiyo nguva yekuti vakadzi vaende kuWashington kunogadzirisa hurumende yedu yakaparara uye zvinosanganisira mukadzi ari pamusoro," akadaro, mukuwirirana neThe Hill.
"Mwedzi waMbudzi 6 uchingopfuura, ndichafungisisa nezvekukwikwidza kuve mutungamiriri wenyika."
Warren akataura maonero ake neZvemutungamiri weNyika Donald Trump mumusangano uyu, achiti "ari kuendesa nyika ino kusiririko.
"Ndiri kunetseka kusvika pakadzika-dzika pangu nezve zvirikuitwa naDonald Trumb kuhutongi hwedu hwegutsaruzhinji," akadaro.

Zvakabuda mune imwe ongororo nemusi weChina, zvisinei, zvakaratidza kuti vazhinji vari munzvimbo inomiririrwa naWarren pachake havafungi kuti achakwikwidza mugore ra2020.
Zvikamu makumi mashanu nezvisere muzana zvevanhu “vane mukana” vekuvhota muMassachusetts vakati seneta uyu haafaniri kukwikwidza, mukuwirirana nezvakabuda muongororo yeSuffolk University Political Research Center/Boston Globe.
Zvikamu makumi matatu nezvitatu vakatsigira kukwikwidza uku.
Ongororo iyi yakaratidza rutsigiro rwakakura kune Mutongi weDundu Deval Patrick, uyo ane zvikamu 38 muzana zvevaitsigira pfungwa yekukwikwidza uye zvikamu 48 kubva muzana zvevasingavirirani nakwo.
Manwe mazita evakakurumbira mubato remaDemocratic vakakurukurwa nezvavo panhau yevangangokwikwidza mugore ra2020 ndiMutevedzeri Vemutungamiri weNyika Joe Biden uye Seneta wekuVermont Bernie Sanders.
