Nyika 18, D.C. dzotsigira kupikiswa kwemutemo werutiziro mutsva
Nyika gumi nesere uye Dunhu reColumbia vari kutsigira kupikiswa kuri pamutemo kwemutemo mutsva weU.S. uyo unorambidza kuti vanhu vari kutiza zvikwata zvine ngozi kana mhirizhonga mudzimba vagamuchirwe.
Vamiririri venyika idzi 18 vakatura mashoko ezvavarikutsigira kudare nemusi weChishanu muWashington vachitsigira vanenge vachitsvaka hutiziro mukupikisana nemutemo uyu, NBC News yakashuma kudaro.
Zita rizere remukwidzi wenyaya muGrace v. Sessions iro veAmerican Civil Liberties Union vakakwidza mumwedzi waNyamavhuvhu mukupikisana nemutemo uyu wehurumende harina kubuditswa.
Akati murume wake "neboka revanakomana vake vane masimba masimba," vakamubata zvisina kunaka asi vakuru-vakuru veU.S. vakaramba chikumbiro chake cherutiziro mumwedzi waChikunguru 20.
Akachengetwa muTexas.
Vachuchisi vehurumende avo vaitsigira Grace vakatsanangura nyika dzeEl Salvador, Honduras uye Guatemala, idzo dzine zvikumbiro zvakawanda zvekutsvaka utiziro muU.S., senyika dziri kutarisana nematambudziko ezvikwata zvine ngozi uye mhirizhonga mudzimba.
Mutemo mutsva wekutsvaka hutiziro vakabvisa chisarudzo chakaitwa mugore ra2014 neDare Rezvikumbiro Zvevashanyi icho chaibvumira vashanyi vasina marezinesi vanenge vachitiza mhirizhonga mudzimba kuti vaite chikumbiro chehutiziro.
Mukuru weMagweta muDunhu reColumbia Karl Racine akataura nemusi weChishanu kuti mutemo mutsva uyu “unopira gotsi mutemo wenyika, wehurumende uye wepasirose."
"Mutemo wehurumende unotarisira kuti zvikumbiro zvose zverutiziro zvinofanira kukurukurwa nezvazvo pachishandiswa humboo nemamiriro ezvinhu echikumbiro chacho, uye kubviswa kwavo kunorwisana nepfungwa iyoyo," akadaro achipa mashoko ehumboo kudare.
Magweta akawedzera kupa maonero avo achiti kuiswa kwemutemo unorambidza vashanyi munyika kunokanganisa hupfumi hweU.S., vachiti vashanyi ava vanogona kuzoita mabhizimisi uye “kuve vashandi muzvikamu zvakakodzera”."
Mukuru weMagweta Jeff Sessions akarayira vatongi mumwedzi waChikumi kuti varege kugamuchira vanenge vachitiza nyika dzavo nekuda kwenyaya dzekumbunyikidzwa mudzimba uye mapoka ane ngozi.
"Hutiziro hunobvumirwa kune vaya vanotiza nyika dzavo nekuda kwekutambudzwa kana kutya nyaya dzekusiyana kweganda, rudzidziso, nyika, kana kuti kubatanidzwa mune mapoka emunharaunda kana mune zvematongerwo enyika," Sessions akadaro muchiziviso chemutemo chaakapa mumwedzi waChikumi 11.
Kupiwa kwehutiziro kwaisaitirwa kupedza matambudziko ose -- ayo vanhu vanosangana nayo mazuva ose kupota pasi rose.
Mabasa ekununura ekukurumidzira oitwa muPalu pakutsvaka vapukunyuki sezvo uwandu hwevanofa hunopetwa kaviri
Nekuda kwevapukunyuki, mamiriro acho ezvinhu ange achiramba achiipa zvikuru.
"Hazvina kumira zvakanaka," vakadaro vamwe amai vane makore 35 vanonzi Risa Kusuma, vachinyaradza mwanakomana wavo uyo aiita seaipisa muviri vari panzvimbo yakakotsekana yeguta rePalu raive rakasuva kwazvo.
"Miniti imwe neimwe amburenzi yaiuya nemitumbi.
Vhura yakachena haichawaniki nyore."
Vagari vaionekwa vachidzokera kudzimba dzavo dzakaparadzwa, vachinhonga midziyo yavo iyo yaive yati chakwata nemvura, vachiedza kununura chero chavaiwana.
Mazana evanhu akakuvadzwa uye zvipatara izvo zvainge zvaparadzwa nekudengenyeka kwenyika kwakakura mwero we7.5, zvakakurirwa.
Vamwe vevakakuvadzwa, kusanganisira Dwi Haris, uyo akatyoka musana nebendekete, vaive vakazorora panze peChipatara cheMauto ePalu, apo varwere vairapwa nechepanze nekuda kwekudengenyeka kwairamba kuchiitika.
Misodzi yakajenga mumaziso ake apo ndangariro dzakauya dzekudengenyeka uku kune simba kwakazunza uriri hwechishanu hwehotera yaaiva nemudzimai uye mwanasikana wake.
"Paisava nenguva yekuzviponesa.
Ndinofunga kuti, ndakapfekerwa muhungwanda-ngwanda hwemadziro," Haris akaudza veAssociated Press, achiwedzera kuti mhuri yake iyi yaive muguta nekuda kwemuchato.
"Ndakanzwa mudzimai wangu achichemera rubatsiro, kuchizotevera runyararo.
Handizivi zvaitika kwaari uye kumwana wangu.
Ndinofunga kuti vakakotsekana."
Mumiririri weU.S. opomera nyika yeChina mhosva 'yekudenha' ichishandisa 'mashoko ekushambadzira enhema'
Svondo pashure pekunge pepanhau rehurumende yeChina ranyora mapeji mana emashoko ekushambadza mupepanhau reU.S. nezveukama hwekutengeserana pakati peU.S. neChina, Mumiririri weU.S. muChina akapomera Beijing kuti iri kushandisa pepenhau reAmerican kuparadzira mashoko enhema.
U.S. Mutungamiri wenyika Donald Trump nemusi weChitatu wapfuura akataura nezvepepanhau reChina Daily muDes Moines Register - pepanhau rinotengwa zvikuru muIowa - pashure pekupomera China kuti iri kutsvaka kupindira musarudzo dzevamiririri weparamende dzeU.S. dzemusi waMbudzi 6, pomero iyo China iri kuramba.
Pomero yaTrump yekuti Beijing yange iri kuedza kupindira musarudzo dzeU.S. kwakatara uko vakuru-vakuru veU.S. vakaudza veReuters kuti chaive chikamu chekutnga chenhimbe yeWashington yekumanikidzira nyika yeChina.
Kunyange zvakajairika kuti nyika dzekunze dziise mashoko ekushambadzira nechinangwa chekusimudzira mabasa ekutengeserana, Beijing neWashington dziri kunetsana parizvino nekuda kwehondo yekutengeserana iri kutsviriridza iyo yaita kuti nyika idzi dziripisane mari yemutero pazvinhu zvavanotengeserana zvakawanda.
Miripo yekutsividza yakaiswa neChina mukutanga chaiko kwehondo iyi yezvokutengeserana yakanangana nekuvhiringidza vanotengesa zvinhu kunyika iyi vakadai senyika yeIowa iyo yaitsigira Bato raTrump remaRepublican, nyanzvi dzeChina neU.S. dzakadaro.
Terry Branstad, uyo ari mumiririri weU.S. muChina neaimbova gavhena kwenguva refu weIowa, iyo inotengesera zvikuru China zvinhu zvekurima, akati Beijing yakuvadza vashandi wekuAmerica, varimi uye mabhizimisi.
Branstad akanyora pachikamu chemaonero papepanhau reSunday's Des Moines Register, nezveChina kuti, "yave kutowedzera kakapetwa kaviri pakudenha uku nekunyora mashoko enhema ekushambadzira mupepanhau redu rakasununguka."
"Mukuparadzira mashoko ayo enhema, hurumende yeChina iri kushandisa mukana wezvagara zvichiitwa muAmerica zvinoyemurwa zverusununguko rwekutaura nerwemapepanhau nekubhadhara kuti shambadziro dzavo dziiswe mupepanhau reDes Moines Register," Branstad akanyora kudaro.
"Mukupesana naizvozvo, mumapepanhau ekuno kuBeijing, hauoni mashoko akawanda evanopikisa uye hauoni maonero chero api zvavo ezvinhu zvinenge zvichinetsa vanhu vekuChina pahurongwa husinakujeka hweupfumi hweChina,sezvo chikamu chezvokubuditswa kwemashoko chichidzorwa zvakasimba neBato reChinese Communist Party," akanyora kudaro.
Akawedzera kuti "rimwe pepenhau rakakurumbira remuChina rakaramba basa rekunyora chikamu chake chemashoko, kunyange zvazvo asina kutaura kuti raive pepanhau ripi.
Bato remaRepublicans Ririkugumbura Vakadzi Vachavhota Nenyaya yaKavanaugh Apo Rakatarisana Nesarudzo Dzevamiririri,Vaongorori Vonyevera
Panguva apo vakuru vebato remaRepublicans vakawanda vari kumira vachitsigira akadomwa kushanda Mudare Repamusoro-soro Brett Kavanaugh uyo arikutarisana nepomero dzekumbunyikidza vanhu mune zvepabonde, vaongorori vapa nyevero yekuti richarasikirwa nevatsigiri, zvikuri sei vechikadzi, pasarudzo dzevamiririri dziri kuuya.
Vanhu vange vachinetseka zvikuru pamusoro penyaya iyi, uye nhengo dzemaRepublicans dzakatoratidza nechekare kuti dzichaenderera mberi nekusarudza.
Haukwanisi kungosiya nhau idzi dzakadaro," Grant Reeher, muzvinafundo pazvidzidzo zvepolitical science paSyracuse University's Maxwell School akaudza veThe Hill mune chimwe chinyorwa chakabuditswa nemusi weMugovera.
Reeher akati haafungi kana zviri kuedzwa kuitwa naSeneta Jeff Flake (R-Arizona) paminiti yekupedzisira zvekuitwa kweongororo yeFBI zvakakwana kudzora hasha dzevachavhota.
"Vakadzi havazombofa vakakanganwa zvakaitika nezuro - havasi kuzozvikanganwa mangwana uye munaMbudzi," Karine Jean-Pierre, mupizano agara nebasa uye ari mutauriri wesangano rinomiririra vanhu reMoveOn akadaro nemusi weChishanu, mukuwirirana nepepanhau reWashington, D.C..
Nemusi weChishanu mangwanani, varatidziri vaideedzera kuti "Mwedzi waMbudzi uchasvika!" apo vairatidzira paimba inoitirwa basa naSeneta sezvo vebato remaRepublicans vane nhengo dzkawanda muKomiti YeDare Redzimhosva vakasarudza kuenderera mberi nekusarudza Kavanaugh pasinei nehumboo hwaDr. Christine Blasey Ford, Mic yakashuma kudaro.
"Manyukunyuku nekufarira nyaya iyi kwebato reDemocratic kuchawedzera zvikuru," Stu Rothenberg, uyo ari nyanzvi munhau dzezvematongerwo enyika asina kwaakarerekera, akaudza wezvenhau ava.
"Vanhu vari kuti kwakatokwira nechekare; ichokwadi ichocho.
Asi kunogona kutowedzera, zvikuru sei kune vechikadzi vechikuru vachavhota mumasabhabha uye vezera rechidiki, vane makore ari pakati pe18 kusvika kuane 29, avo pasinei nekuti havafariri mutungamiri wenyika, havavanzovhota."
Kunyange pashure pekupupurira pachena kwaFord achitsanangura pomero yaaiita yekumbunyikidzwa mune zvepabonde kwaakaitwa neakadomwa kushandira muDare Repamusoro-soro, vaongorori vanoti vebato remaRepublicans vanogona kurasikirwa nerutsigiro kana vakaenderera mberi nekutsimikidza kudoma uku.
"Ichi chikanganiso chakonzera kuvhiringidzika nekuda kweGOP," akadaro Michael Steele, uyo aimbova sachigaro weRepublican National Committee, kutanga kwesvondo rapfuura, mukuwirirana neNBC News.
"Haisi kungori nyaya yekuvhota kwekomiti kana kuti kuitwa kwevhoti yekupedzisira kana kuiswa kwaKavanaugh pabasa, zvinewo chokuita nenzira iyo webato remaRepublicans vabata nhai iyi uye kuti vamubatawo sei," Guy Cecil, mukuru anoona nezvePriorities USA, boka rinobatsira kusarudza nhengo dzebato remaDemocrats, akaratidza kudaro kune vanoburitsa nhau ava.
Zvisinei, vanhu vemuAmerica vari kuratidza kuti vanenge vati kamukanei panhau yekuti votsigira ani pane humboo huri kupiwa naFord uye Kavanaugh, vazhinji vachiratidza kuti vari kutsigira wekupedzisira.
Ongororo itsva yakaitwa neYouGov yakaratidza kuti zvikamu 41 kubva muzana zvevakapindura vaiti vanotsigira zvizere kana kuti zvisina kuzara humboo hwaFord, kuchitiwo zvikamu 35 kubva muzana vachiti vanotsigira zvizere kana kuti zvisina kuzara Kavanaugh.
Pakuwedzera, zvikamu 38 kubva muzana vakati Kavanaugh anogona kunge kana kuti akatonyepa panguva yaaipa humboo hwake, uyewo vanosvika zvikamu 30 kubva muzana vakataura zvakafanana nezvaFord.
Pashure pechikumbiro chaFlake, FBI iri kuita ongororo yepomero dzakataurwa naFord kusanganisirawo mupomeri mumwe chete, Deborah Ramirez, The Guardian yakashuma kudaro.
Ford akapupurira pamberi peDare Redzimhosva reSeneti achipika svondo rapfuura kuti Kavanaugh akamumbunyikidza akadhakwa paaive nemakore 17.
Ramirez akataurawo achipomera kuti nyakudomwa kushandira Dare Repamusoro-soro uyu akamuratidza nhengo dzake dzekubereka nadzo pavaive pamutambo panguva yavaidzidza paYale mumakore ekuma 1980.
Nyakubura World Wide Web Oronga Kutanga Indaneti Itsva Pakukwikwidzana neGoogle uye Facebook
Tim Berners-Lee, uyo akabura World Wide Web, ari kuparura kuti itange kushanda ichikwikwidzana neFacebook, Amazon uye Google.
Purojekiti ichangoburwa yenyanzvi iyi, inonzi Inrupt, ikambani inoshandidzana newebhusaiti yaBerners-Lee inogona kupinda chero ani yeSolid.
Solid inobvumira vashandisi vayo kuti vasarudze pavanoda kuchengetera mashoko avo uye zvinhu izvo vanhu vanobvumirwa kuona pamashoko api.
Muhurukuro yaakaita neFast Company, Berners-Lee akataura hake jee rekuti chinangwa cheInrupt ndeche kuti "ive mberi munyika yose."
"Tinofanira kuzviita izvozvi," akadaro achitaura nezvekutanga uku.
"Inguva yakakosha munhoroondo."
Apu iyi inoshandisa ruzivo rweSolid pakubvumira vanhu kuti vagadzire akaundi yavo yekuchengetera mashoko paindaneti" iyo inonziwo POD.
Inogona kuve nemazita evanhu, ndandanda yezvichada kuitwa, karenda, dura remimhanzi uye mamwe maturusi angashandiswa emunhu uye ezvebasa.
Yakaita seGoogle Drive, Microsoft Outlook, Slack uye Spotify zvose zviri pabhurawuza reindaneti rimwe chete panguva imwe chete.
Zvinosiyanisa nzvimbo iyi yekuchengetera mashoko paindaneti nedzimwe nzvimbo ndechekuti zviri kune mushandisi kuti asarudze mashoko aanoda kuti aonekwe.
Kambani iyi inokudana kuti "kuzvipa masimba mumashoko."
Pfungwa iripa Inrupt, mukuwirirana na CEO wekambani iyi John Bruce, ndeyekuti kambani iunze zvokushandisa, mashandiro uye hunyanzvi hwakakodzera pakubatsira Solid kuti iwanikwe nevanhu vose.
Pari zvino vari mukambani iyi vanobatanidza Berners-Lee, Bruce, purogiramu inochengetedza yakaunzwa neIBM, nyanzvi dzakakumbirwa kushanda pabasa iri, uye vazvipiri vanogadzira makodzi.
Kutanga svondo rino, vaburi weruzivo rwezvemakombiyuta pasi rose vanogona kugadzira maapu avo pachavo vachishandisa maturusi ari pawebhusaiti yeInrupt.
Berners-Lee akati iye neboka rake havasi kutaura "neFacebook uye Google nezvekuti vachaita kuti pave neshanduko yakazara here kana kuti kwete apo mabhizimisi avo ose achange aiswa zvizere panzvimbo muhusiku humwe.
"Hatisi kukumbira mvumo kwavari."
Mumashoko aakatumira paMedium akabuditswa nemusi weMugovera, Berners-Lee akanyora kuti “chinangwa cheInrupt ndechekupa simba mune zvebhizimisi uye nzvimbo yemashandiro kubatsira kudzivirira tsika uye hunaku hwewebhusaiti itsva iyi yakavakirwa paSolid."
Mugore ra1994, Berners-Lee akachinja indaneti paakatanga World Wide Web Consortium paChikoro cheZvekugadzirwa kwezvinhu cheMassachusetts Institute of Technology.
Mumwedzi ichangopfuura, Berners-Lee aiva nenzwi raiteererwa panhau dzekuitwa kwejekerere mune zveindaneti.
Kunyange ari kuparura Inrupt, Berners-Lee acharamba ari Muridzi uye Mukuru weWorld Wide Web Consortium, the Web Foundation uyewo weOpen Data Institute.
"Ndiri kutarisira mberi nechivimbo chizere kunguva iyi iri kutevera yemawebhusaiti," Berners-Lee akavedzera.
Bernard Vann: Mufundisi wemunguva yeWW1 Uyo akaratidza Kuva Gamba oyeukwa
Mufundisi mumwe bedzi weChurch of England kupiwa mubayiro weKuva Gamba munguva yeHondo yeNyika Yekutanga semurwi akayeukwa muguta raaigara mushure memakore 100.
Mukuru Muuto arizve Mufundisi Bernard Vann akahwinha mubayiro uyu musi wa29 Gunyana 1918 pakurwisa kwakaitika muBellenglise uye Lehaucourt.
Zvisinei, akapfurwa ndokuurayiwa mazuva mana akatevera uye haana kuziva kuti akanga ahwinha mubayiro wakakura seuto reBritain.
Dombo rekuyeuka rakaratidzwa nevazukuru vake vaviri pakufora kwakaitwa muRushden, iri muNorthamptonshire, nemusi weMugovera.
Mumwe wevazukuru vake, Michael Vann, akati chaive "chiratidzo chakazonaka" dombo raizoratidzwa makore 100 chaiwo kubva pachinoitika chekupiwa mubayiro chasekuru vake.
Mukuwirirana nepepanhau reLondon Gazette, musi wa29 Gunyana 1918 Mukuru muuto Vann akatungamira boka rake remauto achipfuura nemuCanal de Saint-Quentin "mumhute yaive yakati zvi-i ukuwo mabara achinaya epfutiwo zvadzo nedziya dzinoita zvekumwaya mabara."
Akazosvika panzvimbo yekurwisira muvengi uye "nehushingi hukuru" akatungamira pakurwisa kwevarwi vemberi asati akurumidza kushandisa zvombo zvidiki ndokukunda zvikwata zvevavengi zvitatu.
Mukuru Muuto Vann akaurayiwa nepfuti nemurwi wekuGerman musi wa4 Gumiguru gore ra1918 - kwangosara mwedzi mumwe chete kuti hondo ipere.
Michael Vann, uyo ane makore 72, akati zvakaitwa nasekuru vake “chinhu icho ndinoziva kuti ndaisakwanisa kuchiita asi chiri chinhu chinoita ndizvininipise."
Iye nemukoma wake Dr James Vann vakazoisa maruva mushure mekufora, uko kwaitungamirwa neChikwata cheBrentwood Imperial Youth Band.
Michael Vann akati "ainzwa aremekedzwa zvikuru kubatanidzwa mukufora uku" ndokuwedzera kuti "humhare hwegamba rechokwadi huri kuratidzwa nerutsigiro rwuchapiwa nevanhu vakawanda.”
Vatsigiri veMMA vakapedza husiku hwose vachida kuona Bellator 206, panzvimbo pezvo ndokuratidzwa Peppa Pig
Pafunge kuti, vapedza husiku hwose uchida kuona Bellator 206 uyo ane mamhasuru obva varambidzwa kuona ichi chiitiko chakakura.
Purogiramu yakabva kuna San Jose yaive nemitambo yezvibhakera 13, kusanganisira mitanhatu yaive mikuru uye yairatidzwa ichiitika husiku hwose muUK paChannel 5.
Nenguva dza6 mangwanani, panguva apo Gegard Mousasi naRory MacDonald vaigadzirira kutatsurana, vaoni vemutambo muUK vakasiiwa varwadziva zvikuru nekuratidzwa Peppa Pig nguva yacho.
Vamwe havana kufara nazvo pashure pekunge vapedza usiku hwose vakasvinura zvikuru sei nekuda kwemutambo uyu.
Mumwe mutsigiri paTwitter akatsanangura kuchinjwa uku kwemakatuni evana "semajee asina basa."
"Zvinhu zvaitwa nehurumende kuti nenguva dza6 mangwanani zvange zviri kuda kuratidzwa zvange zvisina kukodzera saka vachinjira kupurogiramiu yevana, " akadaro Dave Schwartz, Bellator mutevedzeri mukuru wapurezidendi wezvekushambadzira uye kukurukurirana, paabvunzwa nezvekusakazwa uku.
""Nguruve inonzi Peppa," hongu."
Purezidhendi wekambani yeBellator anonzi Scott Coker ati vachaongorora marongero avo kuti vabatanidze vateereri vekuUK munguva yemberi.
"Ndinofunga kuti panyaya yekuti uratidzwe patsva, ndinofunga kuti tinogona kuzvironga," Coker akadaro.
"Asi dzatove nguva dza6 mangwanani musi weSvondo ikoko uye hatikwanisi kuzvigadzirisa kusvikira musi weSvondo tichitarisa nguva dzekuno, musi weMumvuro nguva yekwavo.
Asi tiri kuzvigadzirisa.
Chokwadi, paitika kuchinja uku patumirwa mameseji akawanda uye anga asina mashoko ane rugare.
Tange tiri kuedza kuzvigadzirisa, tange tichifunga kuti pane zvangazvakanganisika pamichina.
Asi pange pasina, yange iri nyaya yaitwa nehurumende.
Ndinokuvimbisai kuti hazvisi kuzoitikazve nguva inotevera.
Tichaderedza kusvika pamitambo mishanu panzvimbo pemitanhatu - sezvatagara tichiita - taedza kupa zvakawanda kuvatsigiri vedu zvinhu ndobva zvakanganisika.
Tine hurombo nezvaitika."
Purogiramu yeMimhanzi Yekudzora Ndangariro: Tom Daley ainzwa 'akaderera' nekuda kwemaonero ake nyaya yekudanana
Nyanzvi yekudhaivha paMitambo yepasi rose Tom Daley anoti akakura achinzwa akaderera kune vese nekuda kwemaonero ake nyaya yekudanana - asi izvozvo zvakamukurudzira kuti abudirire .
Murume uyu ane makore 24 akati haana kuzviziva kutozosvikira paakaenda kusekondari kuti “akanga akasiyana nevamwe."
Achitaura pachirongwa che Radio 4 Chemimhanzi Yokudzora Ndangariro chaipakurwa naLauren Laverne, anoti akataura pachena nezvekodzero dzengochani kuti ape vamwe "tariro."
Akatizve kuva mubereki kwakaita kuti asaitire hanya zvikuru kuhwinha paMitambo.
Aivanzopakura chirongwa ichi, Kirsty Young, ave nemwedzi yakawanda asipo nekuda kwekurwara.
Achitaridzika semombe yemashanga pachirongwa chekutanga chaLaverne, Daley akati ainzwa "seasingakoshi" pane vamwe vaaikura navo nekuti "zvaisagamuchirika mumharaunda kuti munhu anzwe achida vakomana nevasikana."
Akati: "Kusvika nhasi, maonero iwayo ekunzwa wakaderera, uye uchinzwa wakasiyana nevamwe, ndiyo akandipa simba nehushingi kuti ndikwanise kubudirira."
Aida kuratidza kuti aive "chimwe chinhu," akadaro, kuitira kuti asodza moyo munhu vose paaizoziva nezvemaonero ake nhau dzekudanana.
Shasha iyi yakatora mukombe webronze paMakwikwi yakava munhu ane mukurumbira kurwira kodzero dzeNgochani uye achishandisa mukana wekuva paMitambo yeCommonwealth muAustralia kupa chikumbiro kunyika dzakawanda kuti dzibvumire hungochani.
Akati anotaura nekuti anonzwa rombo rakanaka rekurarama achibuda pachena pasina kuzvisarura uye achida kupa vamwe "tariro."
Shasha iyi yakakunda vose katatu pasi rose inoti kudanana nemurume - Mugadziri wemafirimu wekuUS Dustin Lance Black, uyo vaakasangana naye mugore ra2013 - "kwakangoerekana kwaitika."
Daley gore rakapera akaroorana nemutori wemukombe weOscar uyu, uyo akamukurira nemakore 20, asi akati musiyano wemakore uyu haisi nyaya kwaari.
"Paunosangana nezvinhu zvakawanda uchiri mwana mudiki saizvozvi" - akaenda kuMakwikwi epasi rose ake ekutanga aine makore 14 uye baba vake vakafa nechirwere chegomarara makore matatu gare-gare - akataura kuti zvange zvakaoma kusangana nemunhu akaenzana naye akasangana nezvaakasangana nazvo.
Vaviri ava vakava vabereki munaChikumi, vachiva nemwanakomana wavo anonzi Robert Ray Black-Daley, uye Daley akati "maonero ake ose" akachinja.
"Dai vakandibvunza gore rakapera, ndaingoti 'ndinofanira kuhwinha mukombe wegoridhe'," akadaro.
"Unoziva chii, pane zvinhu zvikakosha kudarika mikombe yegoridhe.
Mukombe wangu wegoridhe ndiRobbie."
Mwanakomana wake ane zita rakafanana nerababa vake Robert, avo vakafa mugore ra2011 vave nemakore 40 pashure pekubatwa nechirwere chegomarara remuhuropi.
Daley akati baba vake vaisazvitambira kuti vaizofa uye chimwe chinhu chekupedzisira chavakakumbira ndechekuti matiketi akanga atovapo here ekuti vaenda kuMitambo yemuLondon yegore ra2012 - sezvo vaida kuve pazvigaro zvepamberi chaipo.
"Handina kukwanisa kuvaudza kuti baba munenge musisipo kuti muzova pazvigaro zvepamberi'," akadaro.
"Ndainge ndakavabata ruoko pavakamira kufema uye ndakatozozvibvuma pekupedzisira kuti vaikundika pashure pekunge vamira kufema uye vafa," akadaro.
Gore rakatevera racho Daley akakwikwidza muMitambo yepasi rose ya2012 ndokuhwinha bronze.
"Ndakaziva kuti izvi ndizvo zvandaishuvira muupenyu hwangu hwose - kudhaivha pamberi chaipo pechaunga chenyika yangu paMitamboYepasi rose, hapana manzwiro aidarika aya," akadaro.
Zvakaitawo kuti asarudze rwiyo rwake rwekutanga - rwunonzi Proud rwakaimbwa naHeather Small - rwunofambirana nerwendo rwaakafamba kusvika asvika pakukwikwidza paMitambo yepasi rose izvo zvaanoti akazvifunga anomerera.
Chirongwa cheNziyo Dzekudzora Ndangariro chinoitwa paBBC Radio 4 nemusi weSvondo nguva dza11:15 BST.
Mickelson uyo Asiri Mushe ogadzikwa pabhenji paMutambo weMukombe weRyder nemusi weMugovera
Phil Mickelson wekuAmerica achaita zvinogara zvakadaro nemusi weSvondo paachatamba mumutambo wake wechi47 weMukombe weRyder, asi achafanira kupinda mugiya rebasa kuitira kuti asanyadzisa.
Mickelson, uyo ari kutamba pamutambo unoitwa pagore rimwe nerimwe kechi12, akagadzikwa pabhenji nemurairidzi Jim Furyk pamutambo wemabhora mana nevatambi vana wemusi weMugovera.
Panzvimbo pekubatanidzwa zvizere, sezvaagara achiita nekuda kweUnited States, shasha iyi yakahwinha kashanu yakapedza zuva rayo ichiva semutsigiri mukuru vevatambi uye achironga matambiro ake ari nechekure mukuedza kugadzirisa zviri kumunetsa pamatambiro.
Kunyange panhongonya yematambiro ake, mutambi uyu ane makore 48 haana kunyatsokodzera pamutambo wakaoma wemunhandare yegorofu yeLe Golf National, iyo kusagadzikana kwayo kunowanzokanganisa mabhora asina kurohwa zvakanaka.
Uye dai nhandare yacho pachayo isinganetsi, Mickelson, mumutambo wechipfumbamwe wemusi weSvondo, anotarisana neShasha yekuBritain Yekutanga Francesco Molinari, uyo akabatana naTommy Fleetwood ndokuhwnha mitambo yavo yose iri mina svondo rino.
Dai vatambi ava vekuAmerica, avo vari pasi nezvibodzwa zvina pamitambo yekutanga yakazvimirira 12, vakatanga vachipisa-pisa, mutambo waMickelson vaizobetsera zvikuru.
Furyk akaratidza chivimbo nevakomana vake, kwete kuti aizotaura zvakawanda.
"Ange achinyatsonzwisisa basa raaange achiofanira kuita nhasi, akandipuruzira kumusana ndokundimbundira achiti akagadzirira zuva ramangwana," Furyk akadaro.
"Ane chivimbo chizere maari.
IGamba chairo uye akaita zvakawanda kuzvikwata izvi munguva yakapfuura, uye svondo rino.
Handina kuisa muchiono achitamba mitambo miviri.
Ndakaisa muchiono zvinhu zvakawanda, asi ndiyo nzira yazvakafamba nayo uye ndiyo nzira yatakafuka kuti taifanira kufamba nayo.
Ari kuda kuvewo ikoko, semumwe vese."
Mickelson achapfuudza mukurumbira waNick Faldo pamitambo mizhinji yeMukombe weRyder ichatambwa nemusi weSvondo.
Zvinogona kutema kupera kwekutamba kwake mumitambo yeMukombe weRyder iyo yaasina kunyatsosvitsa mwero yematambiro ake pachake.
Mickelson akahwinha mitambo 18, ndokuruza mumitambo 20 uye kuita matayi mumitambo minomwe, kunyange hazvo Furyk akati kuvepo kwake kwakaunza chivimbo kuchikwata.
"Anosetsa vanhu, anoita zvekutsvinya, ane njere, anoda zvekutaura zvinosetsa vanhu, uye munhu akanaka zvikuru kuve naye mukembi," akatsanangura.
"Ndinofunga kuti vatambi vadiki vanonakidzwa nekumbotaura naye, kungofanana, nesvondo rino, izvo zvainakidza kuona.
Ane zvakawanda zvaanoita zvinopfuura kungotamba."
Keputeni wekuEurope Thomas Bjorn oziva kuti kutungamirira kukuru kwavakaita kuchakurumidza kupera
Thomas Bjorn, Keputeni wekuEurope, anoziva kubva muruzivo rwake rwekuzviwanira kuti kutungamirira kukuru kwavakaita vachipinda mumitambo yemutambi mumwe yezuva rekupedzisira mumitambo yeMukombe weRyder kunogona kungoerekana kwapera nyore-nyore.
Dane akatanga kutamba mumutambo wake vekutanga mugore ra1997 muValderrama, uyo ichi chikwata chaiva nakeputeni Seve Ballesteros change chakatungamira chikwata chekuAmerica nezvibodzwa zvishanu asi vakazopedza mutambo uyu vakatungamira nechikamu chidiki-diki, vachihwinha nezvibodzwa 14½-13½.
"Unoramba uchizviyeuchidza kuti taive takatungamira zvikuru paValderrama; taive takatungamira zvikuru paBrookline, uko takakundwa, uye paValderrama, uko takahwinha, asi nechikamu chidiki-chiki," akadaro Bjorn, uyo ari pamufananidzo, pashure pekuona Chikwata ichi chaive Shasha mugore ra2018 chichihwinha nezvibodzwa 5-3 nemusi weChishanu uye nekutungamira kwavakaita zuro nezvibodzwa 10-6 paLe Golf National.
Saka nhoroondo inondiratidza uye munhu vese ari muchikwata kuti hazvisati zvapera.
Unotamba nesimba rako rese mangwana.
Obva ipapo uchiita zvinhu zvose nenzira yakarurama.
Izvi zvinenge zvisina kupera kutozosvikira vawana zvibodzwa.
Tine chinangwa, chinova chekuedza kutora mukombe uyu, uye ndipo panoramba paine ziso redu.
Ndakagara ndakazvitaura kuti, ndinoramba ndakaisa ziso rangu pavatambi 12 vari kurutivi rwedu, asi tiri kunyatsoziva zvakamira kune rumwe rutivi - vatambi vane mukurumbira pasi rose."
Achifara nenzira iyo vatambi vake vakatamba nayo munhandare yegorofu yaive yakaoma zvikuru, Bjorn akavedzera kuti: "Handisi kuzoronga zvechivhurumukira pane izvi.
Zvamangwana zvinhu zvakatosiyana zvikuru.
Amangwana achange ari matambiro emunhu akazvimirira ega pachake, uye zvinhu zvakaoma zvikuru kuita.
Zvinonakidza kutamba uine mumwe munhu kana zvinhu zvichifamba zvakanaka, asi kana wave vega, ndipo paunoedzwa uchionekwa hunyanzvi hwako hwese semutambi wegorofu.
Saka mashoko aunofanira kuudza vatambi, ndeekuti tamba nesimba rako rose mangwana.
Parizvino, hauchisisina munhu wekubatsirana naye pakutamba uye nayewo, achafanira kutamba nesimba rake rose."
Mukusiyana naBjorn, murayiridzi akabudirira zvakafanana Jim Furyk achange achitarisira kuti vatambi vake vatambe zviri nani vakazvimirira kupfuura zvavakaita pavakatamba vacibatsirana, kusiya kwaJordan Spieth uye Justin Thomas, avo vakawana zvibodzwa zvitatu pazvina.
Furyk pachake pakutamba kwaakaita pakutanga nepakupera kwezuva iroro rakakosha rekupedzisira, akatanga ari pakati pechikwata chaihwinha paBrookline achizopedzisira akundwa sezvo Europe yakazoita "Chishamiso paMedinah."
"Ndinoyeuka shoko rimwe nerimwe rairatidza kutsamwa," akadaro achipindura mubvunzo wekuti sei Ben Crenshaw, aive kaputeni mugore ra1999, ange akurudzira chikwata chake chichikunda pazuva rekupedzisira.
"Tine mitambo 12 yakakosha mangwana,asi unotofanira kutanga zvakanaka sezvavakaona nezuro paBrookline, sezvavakaona paMedinah.
Kana zvikatanga zvakangorerekera divi rimwe chete, zvinoita kuti mitambo iyoyo yepakati ive yakaoma zvikuru.
Tinoronga vatambi vedu vachatamba sezviodiwa, toita kuti vakomana vedu vaite maererano nezviri kudiwa, sezvaunoziva, tiri kuda kuita chishamiso mangwana."
Thomas ndiye akapiwa basa rekuedza kutungamirira pakurwisa uku uye achatamba naRory McIlroy mumutambo wakakosha, naPaul Casey, Justin Rose, Jon Rahm, Tommy Fleetwood uye Ian Poulter vamwe vatambi vekuEuropea vari pachikamu chekutanga pakati pevatambi vachatamba.
"Ndakaenda neboka iri rechikwata vakarongwa nemutoo uyu nekuti ndinofunga kuti vanokwana pakuita zvose zvichadiwa," akadaro Bjorn achitaura nezve vaakasarudza kuti vazotamba pamitambo yemutambi mumwe chete.
Zuva rekuparurwa kwengarava yehondo itsva yeGermany rosundirwa mberi zvakare
Ngarava yehondo itsva-itsva yemauto emuMvura eGerman yaifanira kunge yakaparurwa zviri pamutemo muna 2014 kutsiva ngarava dzehondo dzasakara dzemunguva yeHondo yeMashoko, asi haisi kuzovapo kutozosvikira gore rinotevera nekuda kwekusashanda zvakanaka kwemichina uye kuchinjaichinja kwemitengo, pepanhau remunzvimbo iyi rakashuma kudaro.
Kuparurwa kwe"Rheinland-Pfalz," ngarava itsva yeBaden-Wuerttemberg, kwasundirwa mberi kusvika nechepakati pegore ra2019, mukuwirirana nepepanhau reDie Zeit richitura mashoko akataurwa nemutauriri wemauto.
Ngarava iyi yaifanira kunge yakaitwa kuti ishandiswe neUto remumvura muna 2014, asi nyaya dzematambudziko ekutumirwa kwezvinhu kwakakanganisa hurongwa uhwu hwainge hwakatarisirwa zvikuru.
Ngarava idzi dzina dzerudzi rweBaden-Wuerttemberg idzo Uto remuMvura rakatenga muna 2007 dzichauya dzichitsiva ngarava dzasakara dzerudzi rweBremen.
Zviri kunzwisiswa kuti dzichava ngarava dzine simba zvikuru, dzine zvombo zvekurwisa ndege dzemuchadenga, kurwisa zvombo zvinoposherwa nengarava kubatanidza zvombo zvisiri nyore kuona, zvakadai sezvisingabatwi nyore nemichina yeradha, zvinobuditsa masai-sai pakufamba uye ruzha.
Chimwe chinhu chadzakanakira ndechekuti dzinotora nguva refu kuti dzizogadziriswa zvinenge zvafa - zvichange zvave kukwanisika kutumira kuhondo ngarava itsva kwenguva inoita makore maviri kubva panguva yadzinobva pachiteshi chekunyika kwadzo.
Zvisinei, kuramba kwadzo dzisingaunzwi kunoreva kuti ngarava idzi dzechizvino-zvino - idzo Germany iri kunzi icharatidza masimba ayo mhiri kwemakungwa - dzichange dzave dzechinyakare panguva yadzinozotanga kushandiswa, Die Zeit anodaro.
Ngarava iyi yeF125 iyo iri kunzi ichakundikana zvikuru yaive pamisoro yenhau gore rakapera, apo Mauto eMumvura eGermany akaramba zviri pamutemo kuparura ngarava iyi ndokuidzosera kuzvivanze zvengarava zveBlohm & Voss muHamburg.
Ichi chiitiko chekutanga kuti Mauto eMumvura adzose ngarava kuvagadziri vayo pashure pekunge yaunzwa.
Mashoko mashoma ndiyo aizivikanwa bedzi nekuda kwechikonzero chekudzoswa uku, asi vezvenhau muGerman vainongedzera zvikonzero zvakakura “zvekusashanda zvakanaka kwemapurogiramu uye kwemimwe michina wayo" izvo zvaizoita kuti ngarava iyi ishaye basa kana ikatumirwa kuhondo.
Kusashanda zvakanaka kwemapurogiramu ndiyo yaive nhau hombe sezvo ngarava iyi yendudzi dzeBaden-Wuerttemberg ichange ichishandiswa neboka revanhu 120 mumvura - inova hafu yeuwandu hwevanhu vanodiwa kushandisa ngarava yekare yendudzi dzeBremen.
Zvakare, zvakaonekwavo zvakare kuti ngarava iyi inorema zvakanyanya izvo zvinoderedza mashandiro ayo zvichideredzazve mukana wekuti zvimwe zvinhu zvitsva zviiswe paNgarava iyi mune ramangwana.
Ngarava iyi "yeRheinland-Pfalz" inorema matani 7,000 uye inofungidzirwa kuti inorema zvakapeta kaviri dzimwe ngarava dzakafanana nerudzi rwayo dzakashandiswa neGerman muHondo Yenyika Yechipiri.
Kuwedzera pamimwe michina wayo usingashande zvakanaka, mari iri kudiwa pabasa rayo rose - kusanganisira kurovedzwa kwemauto - inyayawo iri kunetsa.
Mari yacho iri kunzi inoda kusvika €3.1 emabhiriyoni ($3.6bn) - yakakwira kupfuura yekutanga €2.2 emabhiriyoni.
Matambudziko engarava iyi itsva akakosha zvikuru kuziva pachitariswa nyevero dzichangobva kupiwa dzekuti simba reuto remumvura reGermany riri kuderera.
Kutanga kwegore rino, Hans-Peter Bartels, mukuru wekomiti yekudzivirirwa kwenyika muGermany, akabvuma kuti Mauto eMumvura ari kupererwa nengarava dzakakodzera kutumira kuhondo."
Nyaya iyi yange iri kukura mukufamba kwaiita nguva, nekuda kwekuti ngarava dzakare dzaibviswa pabasa ukuwo pasina itsva dzaipiwa kudzitsiva.
Akaratidza zvakajeka kuti pange pasina chero ngarava dzerudzi rweBaden-Wuerttemberg dzakaonekwa dzakakodzera kushandiswa neMauto eMumvura.
VeNational Trust voongorora upenyu hwakavanzika hwezviremwaremwa
Tsvakurudzo itsva iri kuitwa pane imwe imba iri muScottish Highlands iyo yakanangana nekubuditsa pachena nzira iyo zviremwaremwa zvinoshandisa zvakadzipoteredza pakuvhima zvekudya.
Zvchabuda patsvakurudzo iyi zviri kutarisirwa kuti zvibetsere pakunzwisisa mararamiro etwumhuka utwu tunobhururuka uye kubetsera pakuitwa kwemabasa ekuchengetedzwa kwatwo.
Ongororo iyo ichaitwa nemasayindisiti epaNational Trust for Scotland ichaongorora zviremwaremwa zvakajairika uye zvisina kujairika kusanganisira zvine nzeve refu dzebhurawuni uye zviremwaremwa zveDaubenton zvinovanikwa paMapindu ari muWester Ross.
Michina inorekodha ichaiswa munzvimbo dzakakodzera kupota musha uyu kuti itore zvichange zvichiitwa nezviremwaremwa mumwaka wacho vose.
Vashandi vepaNHS uye vazvipiri vachaitawo tsvakurudzo vachiita zvekufamba vachishandisa michina inotora zvinenge zvichiitika yemumaoko.
Ongororo yeruzha runenge rwarekodwa ichaitwa nenyanzvi kuti vaone kuti kuchema kwezviremwaremwa kuri kuitwa kakawanda sei uye kuti imhando ipi iri kuita zvipi.
Mepu yenzvimbo inenge ichigarwa uye ripoti zvichabudiswa kuratidza mashoko azere emaitiro azvo munzvimbo.
Rob Dewar, uyo ari mupizano mune zvekuchengetedzwa kwezvakasikwa weNTS, anovimba kuti zvichabuda zvicharatidza nzvimbo dzinonyanyodiwa nezviremwaremwa uye kuti dziri kushandiswa sei nemhando imwe neimwe.
Mashoko acho achabatsira pakuona kubatsira kwemabasa ekutarisira pazvinogara akadai sekusimwa kwemasora, nenzira yakanaka yekuchengetedza masango anogarwa nezviremwaremwa nedzimwewo mhando dzakada kufanana.
Huwandu hwezviremwaremwa muScotland uye kupota muUK hwaderera zvikuru mukati memakore zana apfuura.
Zviri pangozi kubva kumabasa ekuvaka neebudiriro ayo anokanganisa nzvimbo yazvinorara uye pekugara.
Magwenya emhepo uye chiedza zvinokonzera njodzi kwazviri, kungofanana nemapepa anobata nhunzi uye mimwe mishonga inoiswa pazvinhu zvekuvakisa, kusanganisira kubatwa nekatsi dzepamba.
Hazvireve kuti zviremwaremwa hazvioni chaizvoizvo.
Zvisinei, nekuda kwemaitiro azvo ekuvhima husiku nzeve dzazvo dzinonyanya kushanda kupfuura maziso kana pari pakubata zvekudya.
Zvinoshandisa nzira yakadzama zvikuru yekunanga pari kubva masai-sai eruzha rwetwupukanana uye zvipingaidzo panzira yazvinenge zvichibhururuka nayo.
VeNTS, avo vane basa rekutarisirwa kwezvivakwa zvechinyakare zvinopfuura 270, mapindu akakosha 38 uye mahekita anosvika 76,000 enzvimbo kupota nenyika, vanokoshesa zvikuru zviremwaremwa.
Vane nyanzvi dzakarovedzwa dzinosvika gumi, avo vanogara vachiita tsvakurudzo, vachiongorora nzvimbo dzazvinogara uye dzimwe nguva kuita mabasa ekununura.
Sangano iri rakaisavo nznimbo yekutanga uye ingori yoga muScotland yekuchengetera zviremwaremwa pamusha weThreave uri muDumfries neGalloway, uyo unogara mhando gumi dzendudzi dzezviremwaremwa.
Mukuru webasa pamusha uyu David Thompson anoti nzvimbo iyi yakanyatsokodzera musha yazvo.
"Pano paThreave tine nzvimbo yakanaka yezviremwaremwa," akadaro.
"Tine zvivakwa zvakudhara, miti yechinyakare uye nzvimbo yakanaka yekugara.
Asi pane zvakawanda nezvezviremwaremwa zvisingazivikanwi, saka basa ratinoita pano uye pane mimwe misha richatibatsira kunzwisisa zviri nani zvazvinoda kuti zvirarame."
Akaratidza kukosha kwekuona kana pasina zviremwaremwa pasati paitwa mabasa ekugadzirisa pazvivakwa sezvo kuparadza nenjodzi pekugara nekuberekera zviremwaremwa pamwe chete kuchigona kuuraya zviremwaremwa zvikadzi nevana vazvo zvinosvika 400, zvichigona kutsvaira zvose zvinogara panzvimbo yacho.
Zviremwaremwa zvinochengetedzwa uye kutyora mutemo kuzviuraya, kuzvidenha kana kuti kuzvivhiringidza kana kuparadza pazvinogara.
Elisabeth Ferrell, mukuru weSangano Rekuchengetedzwa Kwezviremwaremwa muScotland, akakurudzira veruzhinji kuti vapindire pakubatsira.
Akati: “Tichiine zvakawanda zvekudzidza kuzviremwaremwa zvedu uye kumhando dzimwe dzatiinadzo hatizivi kuti huwandu hwazvo huri kufamba sei."
Ronaldo oramba pomero dzekubata chibharo apo magweta ari kuda kusungisa magazini yekuGerman
Cristiano Ronaldo ataura kuti pomero dzekuti akabata munhu chibharo "inhau dzenhema," achitaura kuti vanhu "vari kuda kuzvisimudzira" nekushandisa zita rake.
Magweta ake ari kuda kusungisa magazini yekuGerman yenhau Der Spiegel, iyo yakanyora nezve pomero idzi.
Mutambi wekumberi wePortugal uye Juventus akapomerwa mhosva yekubata chibharo mudzimai wekuAmerica, anonzi Kathryn Mayorga, mukamuri rehotera yemuLas Vegas mugore ra2009.
Ari kunzi akazomubhadhara mari inosvika $375,000 yekuti asataura nezvechiitiko ichi, Der Spiegel yakanyora kudaro nemusi weChishanu.
Achitaura pavhidhiyo paInstagram Live kuvatsigiri vake vanosvika mamiriyoni 142 maawa mashoma pashure pekunge iyi pomero yabuda, Ronaldo, uyo ane makore 33, akashora mashoko aya achiti "inhau dzenhema."
"Kwete, kwete, kwete, kwete , kwete.
Zvavataura nhasi, inhau dzenhema," shasha yakahwinha kanokwana kashanu paBallon d'Or yakadaro pakamera.
"Vari kuda kuzvisimudzira nekushandisa zita rangu.
Zvinoitika.
Vari kuda kuzvitsvakira mukurumbira nekutaura zita rangu, asi ndozvimwe zvakabatana nebasa racho.
Ndiri munhu anofara uye zvose zvakanaka," mutambi uyu akawedzera, achinyemwerera.
Magweta aRonaldo ari kugadzirira kusungisa Der Spiegel pamusoro pepomero idzi, idzo dzavati "kubuditswa kwemashoko kusiri pamutemo kwezvirikufungidzirwa munyaya dzakavanzika," mukuwirirana nemaskoko eReuters.
Gweta rinonzi Christian Schertz rakati mutambi uyu achatsvaka kubhadharwa panyaya "yekusvibiswa kwezita rake nemari inoenderana nekukura kwekusvibiswa uku, kunova kukanganiswa kwezita remunhu kwati kwamboitika mumakore ano."
Chiitiko ichi chiri kunzi chakaitika muna Chikumi 2009 mukamuri riri muPalms Hotel and Casino muLas Vegas.
Pashure pekuonana mubhawa, Ronaldo naMayorga vari kunzi vakadzokera kukamuri remutambi uyu, uko akamubata chibharo nekunobuda netsvina, mukuwirirana nemapepa emhosva akakwidzwa kuClark County District Court muNevada.
Mayorga ari kuti Ronaldo akagwadama pasi pashure pechiitiko ichi achimuudza kuti aive "munhu akakwana zvikamu 99 kubva muzana" "murume akanaka" angokanganiswa "nechikamu chimwe chete muzana."
Madhokumendi aya ari kuratidza kuti Ronaldo akabvuma kuti vaviri ava vakaita zvebonde, asi pashure pekunge vabvumirana.
Mayorga ari kuti akaenda kumapurisa uye mapikicha akatorwa ari kuchipatara ezvironda zvaakaita, asi pashure akazobvuma kuti nyaya iyi igadziriswe kunze kwedare sezvo ainzwa "achitya kuzotsividzwa" uye achinetseka nenyaya "yekuzonyadziswa paruzhinji."
Mukadzi uyu ane makore 34 ari kuti ave kuda kuti nyaya iyi ichidzoka kudare sezvo ari kunetseka mupfungwa nechiitiko ichi.
Ronaldo ange ave kuda kubatana nechikwata cheReal Madrid achibva kuManchester United panguva yakaitika nyaya iyi, uye mumwaka uno wekupisa akaenda kuchikwata chiri pamusoro muItaly cheJuve atengeswa nemari inosvika mamiriyoni €100.
Brexit: UK 'icharamba ichizvidemba' nekurasikirwa nevanogadzira mota
Nyika yeUK "icharamba ichizvidemba" ikarasikirwa nemukurumbira wayo senyika iri pakutanga pasi rose panhau dzekugadzira mota kana yabuda muBrexit, Munyori munhau dzezveBhizimisi Greg Clark akadaro.
Akawedzera kuti "zvinosiririsa" kuti Toyota UK yakaudza weBBC kuti kana nyika yeBritain ikabuda muEU pasina chibvumirano chaicho ichambomisa mabasa ekugadzira pafekitori yavo iri muBurnaston, predyo neDerby.
"Tiri kuda chibvumirano chaicho," VaClark vakadaro.
Kambani iyi yekuJapan inoita zvekugadzira mota yakati vhiringidziko yekunonotswa pamuganhu wenyika kana pasina chibvumirano chaitwa nezveBrexit kunogona kukonzera kurasika kwemabasa.
Fekitori yemuBurnaston - iyo inogadzira ndudzi dzemota yeToyota Auris uye Avensis - yakagadzira mota dzinosvika 150,000 gore rakapera uyewo dzinokwana zvikamu 90 muzana dzakatengeserwa nyika dzakapoteredza dzemuEuropean Union.
"Maonero angu ndeekuti kana Britain ikabuda muEU panopera mwedzi waKurume tichaona mabasa ekugadzira achimira pafekitori yedu," akadaro Marvin Cooke, Mukuru webasa pakambani yeToyota iri muBurnaston.
Mamwewo makambani anogadzira mota muUK vakataura zvavarikutyira nekubuda muEU pasina zvibvumirano panhau yekuti kutengeserana nedzimwe nyika kuchafambiswa sei, kusanganisira Honda, BMW uye Jaguar Land Rover.
BMW, semuenzaniso, inoti ichavhara fekitari yayo inogadzira mota dzerudzi rweMini iri muOxford kwemwedzi pashure peBrexit.
Zviri kunyanya kutyirwa ndeizvo vagadziri vemota vari kuti ngozi pakuendeswa kwezvigadzirwa kuvatengi kana Brexit yakaitwa pasina chibvumirano chaicho chaitwa.
Toyota iri kushandisa hurongwa "hwekugadzira mukuwirirana nezviri kudiva", ichiwana mapatsi pashure pemaminitsi 37 ega-ega kubva kuvatengesi vari muUK uye EU nekuda kwekugadzirwa kwemota dzakatotengwa nechekare.
Kana UK ikabuda muEU pasina chibvumirano musi wa29 Kurume, pamuganhu wenyika panogona kuvhiringidza mafambiro ezvinhu izvo vari mumakambani aya vari kuti zvichakonzera kuti mapatsi anonoke kuwanika uye aperevedze.
Hazvibviri kuti Toyota inge iine zvigadzirwa zvezuva rimwe chete pafekitari yayo yeDerbyshire, kambani iyi yakadaro, saka mabasa ekugadzira anotombomiswa.
VaClark vakati hurongwa hwaTheresa May hweUkama hwemunguva yemberi neEU "hwakanyatsorongerwa kudzivisa kuongororwa kunoitwa zvinhu pamuganhu."
"Tinoda kuva nechibvumirano. Tinoda kuve nechibvumirano chakanaka chinotibvumira sekududza kwandaita kwete chete kuti tinakidzwe nebudiriro inoitwa pari zvino asiwo kuti tishandise mukana uyu," akadaro pachirongwa cheBBC Radio 4's Today.
"Humboo huri kubva kwete chete kuToyota asiwo kune vamwe vagadziri ndehwekuti tikwanise kuramba tiine hurongwa hwedu hwekufambisa zvigadzirwa zvedu kuvatengi sezvatagara tichiita."
Toyota haina kukwanisa kutaura kuti kumiswa kwemabasa ekugadzira kwaizoitwa kwenguva yakareba sei, asi, akanyevera kuti nechemberi mari inodiwa pakushanda inenge yawanda inogona kuzoderedza simba rekukwikwidza refekitori iyi uye zvichizoguma nekurasika kwemabasa.
Peter Tsouvallaris, uyo akashanda paBurnaston kwemakore 24 uye ari murongi wemisangano yesangano revashandi reUnite pafekitori iyi, akati nhengo dzake dziri kuramba dzichinetseka nazvo: "Kubva mune zvandakasangana nazvo kana mabasa aya apera haazovaniki zvakare.
Mutauriri wehurumende akati: "Taita hurongwa hwakarurama uye hwakanaka nekuda kweukama hwedu hweramangwana neEU."
Musangano waTrump naRosenstein unogona kunonotswa zvakare, anodaro mashoko kubva kuWhite House
Musangano wakakosha zvikuru waDonald Trump nemutevedzeri vemukuru wemagweta Rod Rosenstein unogona "kusundirwa mberi nerimwe vhiki" sezvo makakatanwa aripo nekuda kweakasarudzwa kushanda kudare repamusoro-soro Brett Kavanaugh ari kuramba achiwedzera, vekuWhite House vakadaro nemusi weSvondo.
Rosenstein anotarisira mabasa emupizano Robert Mueller, uyo ari kuongorora nyaya yekupindira kweRussia mune zvesarudzo, hukama huripo pakati pevanoshandira Trump neRussia uye kudziviswa kweruramisiro uko kunogona kuitwa nemutungamiri wenyika uyu.
Pfungwa yekuti Trump achadzinga here kana kusadzinga mutevedzeri wemukuru wemagweta uyu, uye zvokanganisa rusununguko rwaMueller, yakonzera marehwa-rehwa kwemwedzi yakawanda.
Kutanga kwemwedzi uno, pepanhau reNew York Times rakanyora kuti Rosenstein akaita hurukuro aine kamuchina kekurekodha mashoko nechinangwa chekutapa hurukuro iyi aina Trump uye mukana wekubvisa mutungamiri wenyika pachishandiswa mutemo wakagadziriswa wechinhamba 25.
Rosenstein akaramba mashoko aya.
Asi nemusi weMuvhuro akaenda kuMuzinda wemutungamiri wenyika weWhite House, pashure pemashoko aiti aida kusiya basa.
Panzvimbo pezvo, musangano naTrump, uyo aive kumusangano weMubatanidzwa weNyika dzePasi Rose muNew York, vakaziviswa kuti vaizoitwa nemusi weChina.
Trump akati "aizosarudza" kusadzinga basa Rosenstein asi kubva ipapo musangano uyu vakambosendekwa kuitira kuti pasave nekubonderana nedare rekomiti yeSeneti yedzimhosva umo Kavanaugh nemumwe vevakadzi vaimupomera kuti ainge avambunyikidza mune zvepabonde, Dr Christine Blasey Ford, vose vaipupurira nhau dzavo.
Nemusi weChishanu, Trump akaraira kuti FBI iite ongororo yesvondo rimwe chete yenyaya dzaipomerwa Kavanaugh, zvichisundira mberi zvakare kuitwa kwesarudzo dzaSeneta.
Munyori wenhau dzaTrump, Sarah Sanders, akaoneka paFox News nemusi weSvondo.
Abvunzwa nezvemusangano waRosenstein, akati: "Zuva rekuitwa kwavo harisati ravapo, rinogona kuziviswa svondo rino, ndiri kuona uchisundirwa mberi nerimwe svondo tichitarisa zvimwe zvinhu zviri kuitika kudare repamusoro-soro.
Asi tichaona uye ndichaita kuti vezvenhau vave nemashoko azere."
Vamwe vaburitsi venhau vanogona kupikisa mutongo iwoyo: Sanders haana kuita musangano nevatori venhau paMuzinda wehurumende weWhite House kubvira musi wa 10 Gunyana.
Aitungamira chirongwa ichi Chris Wallace akabvunza kuti nemhaka yei.
Sanders akati kusaitwa kwemisangano kwaisava nekuda kwechikonzero chekusada “kuda kuonekwa” kwevabuditsi venhau dzepaTV, kunyange zvazvo akati: "Handirambi pfungwa yekuti vanoda kuonekwa."
Akazokarakadza kuti misangano yakananga pakati paTrump nevatori wenhau ichawedza.
"Mutungamiri wenyika anoita misangano Yemibvunzo neMhinduro kupfuura zvakaitwa nechero mutungamiri wenyika akamutangira," akadaro, achiwedzera kutaura asina kupa humboo: "Takacherechedza huwandu hwacho."
Misangano ichaitwa, Sanders akadaro, asi "kana vatori venhau vakawana mukana wekubvunza mibvunzo zvakananga kumutungamiri wenyika yeUnited States, zvinenge zviri nani zvikuru pane kutaura neni.
Tinoedza kuita izvozvo kakawanda uye makatoona tichiita izvozvo mumasvondo achangobva kupfuura uye zvichatsiva musangano vekupa mashoko vatori venhau apo muchataura nemutungamiri wenyika yeUnited States."
Trump nguva nenguva anopindura mibvunzo paanobuda paMuzinda wemutungamiri wenyika weWhite House kana paanoita misangano yekukurukurirana kana yevatori venhau nevanoremekedzwa vanenge vashanya.
Misangano yakangonangana nevatori wenhau haivanzoitwa.
Svondo rino muNew York mutungamiri wenyika akaratidza kuti nei, achioneka zvisina kurongeka uye kujairika pavatori venhau vanenge vakaungana.
Munyori muchikamu chezveUtano onyorera vashandi veEU paNHS yemuScotland pamusoro pezviri kutyirwa panhau yeBrexit
Munyori muchikamu chezveUtano akanyorera vashandi veEU vari kushanda paNHS yemuScotland achitsanangura kutenda uye chido chenyika iyi chekuti varambe varipo pashure peBrexit.
Jeane Freeman MSP akatumira tsamba kwangosara mwedzi iri pasi pemitanhatu kuti UK ibude muEU.
Hurumende yeScotland yakatoratidza kuzvipira kwayo kuti ibhadharire mari inodiwa pakuitwa kwezvikumbiro zvakakodzera zvevashandi vanobva muEU vaishanda muzvikamu zvayo zvehurumende zvaive zvave kutarisirwa kumwe.
Mutsamba yake, Muzvare Freeman vakanyora kuti: "Mukutanga kwemwaka wekupisa, nhaurirano pakati peUK neEU nezvekubuda uku dzaive dzichienderera mberi, pachitarisirwa kuti zvisarudzo zviitwe mumwaka wechando uno.
Asi Hurumende yeUK yange iri kuwedzerawo gadziriro yayo nekuda kwekusabuda kwechibvumirano kwaigona kuitika.
Ndinoziva kuti iyi inguva yekusagadzikana kwamuri mose.
Ndicho chikonzero nei ndiri kuda kusimbisira kukoshesa kwandinoita maonero emushandi mumwe nemumwe, pasinei nenyika yaanobva .
Shamwari dzedu kupota muEU yose, uye nechekure, vanounza ruzivo rwavo rwekuzviwanira uye hunyanzvi uho hunosimbisa uye kuvandudza mabasa muchikamu chezveutano, zvichibetsera varwere uye nharaunda dzatinoshandira madziri.
Scotland musha wenyu uye tinoda chaizvo kuti mugare muno."
Christion Abercrombie Ovhiyiwa Zvekukurumidzira Pashure Pekukuvadzwa Mumusoro
Mutambi wekumashure vechikwata cheTigers chemuNyika yeTennessee Christion Abercrombie ovhiyiwa zvekukurumidzira pashure pekukuvadzwa mumusoro pamutambo wemusi weMugovera wavakakundwa 31-27 nechikwata cheVanderbilt Commodores, Murairidzi wechikwata cheTennessean Mike Organ akataura kudaro.
Murairidzi mukuru wechikwata cheTennessee State Rod Reed akaudza vatori venhau kuti akakuvara chikamu chepiri chichangotanga.
"Akangoenda nechedivi ndokungoerekana adonha ipapo," Reed akadaro.
Varairidzi uye vezveutano vakaisa Abercrombie pamuchina weoxygen ari nechepadivi vasati vamutakura pakamubhedha kuti anoongororwa zvizere.
Mumwe mukuru-mukuru kubva ku Tennessee State akaudza Chris Harris weWSMV yeNashville,iri muTennessee, kuti Abercrombie akanga apedza kuvhiyiwa paVanderbilt Medical Center.
Harris akawedzera kuti "pari zvino pangapasina mashoko nezverudzi uye mwero wekukuvara" uye Tennessee State iri kuedza kuona nguva yaitika kukuvara uku.
Abercrombie, uyo aive ari mumwaka wepiri mumutambo pachikoro, ari mumwaka wake wekutanga nechikwata cheTennessee State mushure mekutama achibva kuchikwata cheIllinois.
Akanga apiringisha kanokwana kashanu asati abuda mumutambo nemusi weMugovera, uyo vakaita kuti asvitse kupiringisha kunokwana ka18 mumwaka.
Vatengi vanobva kudzimwe nyika Vachabhadhariswa mutero wakakura kana vachitenga imba muUK
Vatengi vanobva kudzimwe nyika Vachabhadhariswa mutero wakakura kana vachitenga imba muUK uye imwe mari yacho yemuraudzo ichashandiswa kubatsira vasina dzimba mukuwirirana nehurongwa hwaTory
Hurongwa uhwu huchamirisana nehurongwa hwakabudirira hwaCorbyn hwekutsvaka rutsigiro kune vechidiki musarudzo
Mutero uyu vakakwidzwa uchabhadhariswa kune avo vagara vasiri kubhadhara mutero muUK
Vechikamu chezvemari vari kutarisira kuti vachaunganidza mari inosvika mamiriyoni £120 gore rimwe nerimwe- yekubatsira vasina dzimba
Vatengi vanobva kudzimwe nyika Vachabhadhariswa mutero wakakura kana vachitenga imba muUK - uye imwe mari yacho yemuraudzo ichashandiswa kubatsira vasina dzimba, Theresa May achazivisa nhasi
Hurongwa uhwu huchaonekwa senzira yekumirisana nekubudirira kwehurongwa hwaJeremy Corbyn hwekutsvaka rutsigiro mune zvesarudzo kubva kune vechidiki nekuvavimbisa dzimba dzakachipa uye kutsvaka rubatsiro kubva kune vanowana mari yakawanda.
Mutero uyu wakakwidzwa uchabhadhariswa kuvanhu uye makambani agara asingabhadhari mutero muUK, uye mari ichawanikwa yacho ichizobatsira pahurongwa hweHurumende hwekurwisana nekushayikwa kwedzimba.
Mutero wekuwedzera - uyo unobhadharwa pamusoro pemutero uripo izvozvi, kusanganisira mari yemutero inobhadharwa yakaiswa makore maviri apfuura pakutenga nekubhadhara mari zvishoma nezvishoma pakutenga dzimba dzakambogarwa uchange uchisvika pazvikamu zvitatu kubva muzana.
Vechikamu chezvemari vari kutarisira kuti vachaunganidza mari inosvika mamiriyoni £120 pagore.
Zvikamu zvinosvika 13 muzana zvedzimba itsva muLondon zvinofungidzirwa kuti zvinotengwa nevanhu vasiri vemuUK, zvichikwidza mitengo uye kuita kuti zviomere zvizvarwa zvemunyika kuti vazadzise zviroto zvavo zvekuva nedzimba.
Nzvimbo dzakawanda dzinogara mbozha munyika -zvikuru sei muguta guru - dzave "sematongo eguta" nekuda kwekuti vakadzitenga vacho vanenge vari vekudzimwe nyika avo vanopedza nguva zhinji vasiri munyika.
Mutemo uyu mutsva vauya pashure pemasvondo mashoma apo Boris Johnson akazivisa kuti mutero uyu uiswe kubatsira vechidiki vakawanda kuti wavanewo musha wavo vekutanga.
Akapomera makambani mahombe anoita zvekuvaka kuti airamba akakwidza mitengo yedzimba nekukasira kutenga nzvimbo asi vasingaishandise, ndokukurudzira Muzvare May kuti vasiye hurongwa kwedzimba dzinotengeka kuti vagadzirise "zvinosuvisa mune zvedzimba" muBritain.
VaCorbyn vakazivisa nezvezvisarudzo zvakawanda zvinokwezva zvakachinjwa mune zvedzimba, kusanganisira mitemo pamari dzinoripirwa kushandisa dzimba uye kugumiswa kwekudzinga munhu paanogara “pasina mhosva”.
Ari kuda zvakare kupa masimba akakura kumakanzuru ekuti avake dzimba dzitsva.
Muzvare May akati: "Gore rakapera ndakati dzichashandisa simba rangu semukuru wemakurukota ehurumende kudzosa maroto eBritain - ekuti upenyu hunofanira kuve nani kuchizvarwa chimwe nechimwe.
Uye izvi zvinoreva kugadzirisa musika wedu vakaparara wedzimba.
Britain icharamba ichigamuchira vanhu vanoda kugara mairi, kushanda uye kuumba upenyu huri nani muno.
Zvisinei, zvinenge zvisina kunaka kuti zvive nyore kune vanhu vasingagari muUK, kusanganisira makambi asiri emuno, kuti atenge dzimba zviri nyore kufanana nevagari vanoshanda nesimba vemuBritain.
Kune vakawanda pfungwa yekuvawo nemba yangova maroto chete, uye kurara mumigwagwa ndiko kwangosara kuripo chete."
Jack Ross: 'Chido changu chikuru ndechekuva murairidzi weScotland'
Murairidzi mukuru wechikwata cheSunderland Jack Ross anoti "chido chake chikuru” ndechekuva murairidzi weScotland pane imwe nguva.
Murume wekuScotland, ane makore 42, ari kuedza zvishoma nezvishoma kusimudzira chikwata cheNorth-East, icho chiri panzvimbo yechitatu muZvikwata Zvekutanga, chiri pasi nezvibodzwa zvitatu kubva kumusoro.
Akatamira kuStadium of Light mumwaka uno pashure pekubatsira chikwata cheSt Mirren kupindazve muMakwikwi eScottish Premiership mumwaka wapfuura.
"Ndaida kutambira nyika yangu semutambi.
Ndakangokwanisa kupinda muzvikwata B uye ndizvo chete," Ross akaudza veBBC Scotland's Sportsound.
"Asi ndakakura ndichiona chikwata cheScotland paHampden nguva zhinji nababa vangu ndichiri mwana mudiki, uye ndicho chinhu chairamba chichindidzosa .
Mukana iwoyo unozongouya, naizvozvo, kana ndikabudirira semurairidzi wechikwata chisiri chenyika."
Vakateverwa naRoss semurairidzi wechikwata cheSunderland vanosanganisira Dick Advocaat, David Moyes, Sam Allardyce, Martin O'Neill, Roy Keane, Gus Poyet uye Paulo Di Canio.
Aimbova murairidzi weAlloa Athletic uyu anoti haanzwi kutya nekutevera mazita ane mukurumbira akamborairidza chikwata ichi chine mbiri, pashure pekunge amboramba kushandira zvikwata zveBarnsley uye Ipswich Town.
"Kwandiri kubudirira kwangu kuchayerwa nekuti 'ndichadzosa here chikwata ichi muMakwikwi ePremier League?'
Nekuda kwezvinhu zviripo nekuda kwechikwata ichi, hapana mubvunzo kuti chinofanira kunge chiri muPremier League," akadaro.
"Harisi basa riri nyore kuchisvitsa ipapo, asi zvichida ndichazviona sendabudirira chete kuno kana ndikakwanisa kudzosa chikwata ichi ikoko ."
Ross anongori nemakore matatu achishanda semurairidzi , pashure pekutora nguva yakareba ari mubetseri wemurairidzi wechikwata cheDumbarton uye mwedzi 15 ari mushandi muvarairidzi vechikwata cheHearts.
Akazobatsira chikwata cheAlloa kudzoka kubva mukuderedzwa kusvika pamwero wechitatu, uye kubatsira chikwata cheSt Mirren chaive pedyo nekuderedzwa kusvika pakuve Shasha dzakahwinha mumwaka wakatevera.
Uye Ross anoti ari kunzwa kusununguka pari zvino kupfuura kare kose panguva yaaive mutambi muzvikwata zveClyde, Hartlepool, Falkirk, St Mirren uye Hamilton Academical.
"Yaive nyaya chaiyo zvichida yaida kuti ndinyatsoita chisarudzo," anoyeuka, yekutungamirira chikwata cheAlloa.
"Ndainyatsozvinzwa kuti basa rekutungamirira ndiro rainyatsoenderana neni, kutopfuura kutamba.
Zvinonzwika sezvisina musoro nekuti ndakaita zvakanaka, rakandiraramisa zvikuru, uye kunakidzwa neupenyu hwakanaka.
Asi kutamba kunogona kuoma.
Pane zvinhu zvakawanda zvaunofanira kuita svondo rimwe nerimwe.
Ndichiri kunzwa izvozvo panyaya yekuzvidya moyo uye zvinotarisirwa pabasa racho asi kutungamirira kunenge kuri nani zvikuru.
Ndagara ndaida kutungamirira uye pari zvino ndizvo zvandiri kuita, riri nyore zvikuru kwandiri munhoroondo yeupenyu hwangu hwose semunhu mukuru."

Kupisa kwemwaka uno kowedzeresa mari inowanikwa nevanotengesa doro muBritain avo vari kutatarika asiwo kokonzera zvinetso zvikuru kuzvitoro zvinotengesa zvekudya.
Vanotengesa doro uye mabhawa vopupurira kuwedzera kwemari yavanowana mukutengesa nezvikamu 2.7 kubva muzana muna Chikunguru - asi mari yakawanikwa nevanotengesa zvokudya yange yakaderera nezvikamu 4.8 muzana, hwerengedzo dzemanhamba dzoratidza.
Peter Martin, wekuCGA uko kunopiwa mazano mune zvemabhizimisi, uye kunova kwakahwerengedzwa manhamba aya, akati: "Kuramba kuchipisa uye kubatanidzwa kweEngland mumitambo yeMukombe wePasi Rose uko kwatora nguva refu kupfuura zvange zvichitarisirwa kunoreva kuti mwedzi waChikunguru uchaita zvakafanana nezvakaita mwedzi Chikumi wapfuura, apo vanotengesa doro vakange vari pamusoro nezvikamu 2.8 muzana, kusiya kwevanotengesa zvekudya avo vakakanganiswa zvikuru.
Kudzikira nezvikamu 1.8 muzana kwezvakatengwa muzvitoro zvinotengesa zvokudya mumwedzi waChikumi kwakawedzera zvikuru mumwedzi waChikunguru.
Vanotengesa zvinwiwa nedoro vakaita zvakanaka zvikuru pakutengesa kupfuura vanotengesa zvokudya.
Vanotengesa zvekudya nedoro vakaomerwawo zvikuru mumwaka wekupisa, kunyange hazvo vasina kuzosvika pamwero wekuomerwa wevanotengesa zvekudya.
Zvinoratidzika sekunge vanhu vaingoda kuenda kunomwa zvinwiwa.
Munotengeswa doro nemumabhawa kutengwa kwezvinwiwa kwakawedzera nezvikamu 6.6 muzana mumwedzi wacho, ukuwo zvekudya zvakaderera nezvikamu zvitatu kubva muzana."
Paul Newman, muongorori muchikamu chekutandara nekushanya cheRSM akati: "Zvakabuda izvi zviri kuramba zvakafanana nezvatakaona kubva mukunopera kwemwedzi waKubvumbi.
Mamiriro ekunze uye zviitiko zvikuru zvevanhu nemitambo ndizvo zvanyanyokonzeresa kutengwa kwezvinhu kumisika iri kure nemisha.
Hachisi chishamiso kuti zvitoro zvinotengesa zvekudya zviri kuramba zvichinetseka, sezvo mwero wezvikamu 4.8 muzana wekudzikira kwekutengwa kwezvinhu zvavo uchirwadza pamusoro pekudiwa kwemari yokubhadharira zvimwe zvinhu.
Mwaka murefu wekupisa vaisafanira kuuya panguva yakaomera vanotengesa zvokudya uye nguya ichatema kana mamiriro ekunze ekutonhorera atange tiinawo muna Nyamavhuvhu uchaunza zororo iro riri kudiwa zvikuru."
Kuwanda kwezvakatengwa muzvitoro zvinotengesa doro uye zvekudya, kusanganisira zvichangovhurwa, kwaive zvikamu 2.7 muzana mumwedzi waChikunguru, kuchiratidza kudzikira mukutengeswa kwezvinhu izvi .

Mumwe chete pavana vashanu ane akaundi yepachivande yekuwadzana nevamwe paindaneti yaasingaratidzi vabereki
Mumwe chete pavana vashanu - vamwe vari kumakore ekuma11 - vane maakaundi epachivande yekuwadzana nevamwe paindaneti yavasingaratidzi vabereki wavo uye vadzidzisi, ongororo yakaratidza kudaro
Ongororo yakaitwa kuvadzidzi 20,000 vepachikoro chesekondari yakaratidza kuwedzera “kwemaakaundi yeInstagram epachivande”
Nhau iyi yakaratidza kutyirwa kwekutumirwa kwezvinhu zvinoratidza zvepabonde
Zvikamu makumi maviri kubva muzana zvevadzidzi zvakati vane akaundi “chaiyo” yekuratidza vabereki
Mumwe chete pavana vashanu - vamwe vari kumakore ekuma11 - vari kugadzira maakaundi ekuwadzana nevamwe paindaneti avasingaratidzi vanhu vakuru.
Ongororo yakaitwa kuvadzidzi 20,000 vepachikoro chesekondari yakaratidza kuwedzera kukuru “kwemaakaundi yeInstagram epachivande”- kutsamira pamashoko akabva kuInstagram iri webhusaiti inoitwa zvekutumirana mifananidzo.
Nhau iyi yakaratidza kutyirwa kukuru kwekutumirwa kwezvinhu zvinoratidza zvepabonde
Vanosvika zvikamu makumi maviri muzana zvevadzidzi vakati vane akaundi “chaiyoiyo” yakachena yekuratidza vabereki, ukuwo vaine dzimwe dzepachivande.
Vamwe amayi vakawana akaundi yepaindaneti yepachivande yemwana wavo ane makore 13 vakaona mashoko emuyaruki uyu achikurudzira vamwe kuti "ndibatei chibharo."
Imwe ongororo, yakaitwa neDigital Awareness UK neveHeadmasters" and Headmistresses" Conference (HMC) yezvikoro zvisiri zvehurumende, vakawana kuti zvikamu 40 kubva muzana zvevana vari pakati pemakore 11 kusvika ku18 vaive nemaakaundi maviri, kuchitiwo hafu yavo ichibvuma kuti ine maakaundi epachivande.
Mukuru weHMC Mike Buchanan akati: "Zvinosuvisa kuti vachiri kuyaruka vakawanda vari kunyengedzwa kugadzira nzvimbo dzepaindaneti idzo vabereki nevadzidzisi vasingazivi nezvadzo."

Kambani inogadzira muchina wekukama mukaka yokonzera maonero akasiyana paindaneti neshambadziro yayo inoenzanisa anamai vari kuyamwisa nemhou dziri kukamwa mukaka.
Pakuparurwa kweuri kunzi “muchina wakanyarara kukunda yose pasi rose wekukama mukaka unoitwa zvekupfekwa” kambani inogadzira midziyo yekushandisa yeElvie yakaburitsa rwiyo rwune vhidhiyo rwusiri pachokwadi rwekushambadzira rusununguko rwunopiwa nemuchina uyu mutsva kune vanamai vari kuyamwisa.

Mashoko acho anoenderera mberi achiti: "Ukame, ukame, ndiri kuupa vana kuti vadye, ukame, ukame, ndiri kukama madzimai angu."

Yakaonekwa nevanhu 77,000 uye kupiwa mazana epfungwa dzemashoko pamusoro payo, vhidhiyo iyi yatambirwa zvakasiyana-siyana nevakaiona, ukuwo vazhinji vachiti inojekesa "zvinhu zvinotyisa" zvemakambani anotengesa zvigadzirwa zvemukaka.
"Chisarudzo chakapusa kushandisa mhou kushambadzira chigadzirwa ichi.

Muchina uyu wekukama weElvie unokwana zvisingaonekwi muzvinofukidza mazamu aamai vari kuyamwisa (Elvie/Amai)

Vamwe vaitsigira shambadziro iyi, vamwewo amai vachitaura kuti karwiyo kacho "kanofadza."

Ichi chigadzirwa cheshasha," mumwe akanyora kudaro.

Iyi haisi shambadziro yekurumbidza kana kutonga makambani ezvigadzirwa zvemukaka."

Nyika yeSyria youdza ‘mauto ari munyika yayo’ enyika dzeUS, French uye Turky kuti abude nekukurumidzira
Achitaura pamusangano weUN General Assembly, Gurukota reNyaya Dzekunze Walid al-Moualem akaudza vapoteri vekunyika yeSyria kuti vadzoke kumba, kunyange zvazvo hondo munyika iyi yave mugore rechisere ichiitika.
Moualem, uyo anoshandawo semutevedzeri vemukuru vemakurukota ehurumende, akati mauto ekudzimwe nyika aiva munyika iyi zvisiri pamutemo, vachizvivhariridza nenyaya yekurwisa ugandanga, uye "vachashandwa navo zvinoenderana."
"Vanofanira kubuda nekukurumidza uye pasina zvirehwa-rehwa," akaudza dare remusangano uyu.
Moualem akasimbisira kuti "hondo yekurwisana nehugandanga yave kuda kupera" muSyria, umo vanhu vanopfuura 360,000 vakafa kubvira muna 2011, uye vanosvika mamiriyoni vakamanikidzirwa kusiya misha yavo.
Akati Damascus icharamba "ichirwa hondo iyi tsvene kusvikira yatsvaira munzvimbo dzose" mapoka emagandanga uye “chero vekudzimwe nyika vanenge vari munyika iyi zvisiri pamutemo."
Nyika yeUnited States ine mauto anosvika 2,000 muSyria, zvikuru sei vachizvirovedza uye kupa mazano kuvarwi vechiKurdy nemaArabhu emuSyria anopikisana neMutungamiri veNyika Bashar al-Assad.
France ine mauto anodarika 1,000 vari pabasa munyika iyi yasakadzwa nehondo.
Panyaya yevapoteri, Moualem akati mamiriro ezvinhu ange akanaka kuti vadzoke, uye akapomera “dzimwe nyika dzekumadokera” kuti “vari kuparadzira mashoko ekutyisidzira kusina basa” izvo zviri kuita kuti vapoteri vasada kudzoka.
"Takakoka vanhu pasi rose nemasangano anopa rubatsiro kuti vabatsire pakudzoka uku," akadaro.
"Vari kuita zvematongerwo enyika panyaya inongori yekubetserwa kwevanhu."
Nyika yeUnited States neSangano reMubatanidzwa weNyika dzemuEurope vapa nyevero yekuti hapana rubatsiro ruchapiwa rwekuvakwazve kwenyika yeSyria kusvikira pava nechibvumirano chezvematongerwo enyika pakati paAssad nevanopikisa kuti hondo ipere.
Vamiririri veUN vanoti chibvumirano chichangobva kuitwa pakati penyika yeRussia neTurkey chekuiswa kwenzvimbo yakazvimirira yoga munzvimbo yekupedzisira yevapanduki yeIdlib kwakapa mukana wekumanikidzira kuitwa kwehurukuro dzezvematongerwo enyika.
Hurongwa hwenyika yeRussia neTurkey hwakadzivisa kurwisa kwakakura kwemauto eRussia achitsigirwa neyekuSyria mupurovhinzi iyi, umo munogara vanhu vanosvika mamiriyoni matatu.
Moualem zvisinei akaratidza kuti chibvumirano chacho chine “mazuva akatarwa” ndokuratidza kuti ane chivimbo chekuti mabasa ekurwisa achaitwa kuvarwi vechi moziremu kusanganisira varwi veNusra Front avo vakabatana nechikwata che Al-Qaeda, avo "vachatsvairwa."
Nhume yeUN Staffan de Mistura ane tariro yekuti nekukurumidza acharonga misangano yekutanga yekomiti itsva inobatanidza nhengo dzehurumende uye dzevanopikisa kuti vagadzire bumbiro remutemo idzva renyika yeSyria iro richapa nzira yekuitwa kwesarudzo.
Moualem akapa zvinotarisirwa pakubatanidzwa kwehurumende yeSyria mukomiti, achiti basa renhengo idzi nderekutarisisa kana paine zvingada kuchinjwa pazvikamu zvebumbiro remutemo riripo," ndokupa nyevero pamusoro pekuvhiringidza kuitwa kweiri basa.
Nei Trump Achakunda Musarudzo Dzinotevera
Nemafungiro iwayo, VaTrump vachakunda zvakare musarudzo dza2020 kunze kwekunge, vamiswa basa neparamende kana kuti kumiswa basa nemhosva dzavo nguva isati yakwana, sezviri kutarisirwa nevaongorori vakazvimirira vakawanda.

Kubvira muna 2014, kuteererwa kwezvirongwa zvinoitwa pakati pehusiku kwakawedzera zvakapetwa kaviri kusvika pamamiriyoni 1.05 paCNN uye kupetwa katatu kusvika pamamiriyoni 1.6 paMSNBC.

Mari kubva kunze yopinda yakawanda mumakwikwi akaomesesa esarudzo dzevamiririri veParamende
Hazvishamisi kuti dunhu rechi17 rePennsylvania riri kuwana mari yakawanda iri kupinda, nekuda kwekurongwazve kwematunhu eparamende uko kwaita kuti vaviri ava vakwikwidzane nekuda kwedunhu rimwe chete.
Iri dunhu richangobva kuiswa pamepu remasabhabha emuPittsburg roisa pamakwikwi Mumiririri webato remaDemocrat Conor Lamb - uyo akakunda mune rimwe dunhu musarudzo dzakakosha dzakaitwa mumwaka wechando.
Lamb ari kukwikwidzana neimwe nhengo, Keith Rothfus webato remaRepublican, uyo parizvino ari kumiririra dunhu rechi12 rePennsylvania, iro rinopindirana zvikuru nerechi 17.
Mamepu akanyorwa patsva pashure pekunge Dare Repamusoro-soro muPennsylvania rapa mutongo vakarerekera kune zvaidiwa nebato remaRepublican muna Ndira wekuti madunhu aya akudhara akarongwa zvisiri pabumbiro remutemo sezvo marongerwo ayo achivhiringidza zvinobuda musarudzo
Makwikwi edunhu itsva rechi 17 akonzeresa hondo yekushandiswa kwemari pakati pevanotarisira nyaya dzemari mumapato makuru, veDemocratic Campaign Congressional Committee (DCCC) uye veNational Republican Campaign Committee (NRCC).
Zita rekuti Lamb rakava nemukurumbira zvikuru muPennsylvania pashure pekuhwina nepaburi retsono musarudzo dzakakosha dzainge dzakavhurirwa maziso dzaKurume dzeMumiririri weParamende mudunhu rechi 18 rePennsylvania.
Dunhu iri raive remaRepublican kwemakore anopfuura gumi, uye Mutungamiri weNyika Donald Trump akahwinha nemapoinzi 20 mudunhu iri.
Nyanzvi munhau dzezvematongerwo enyika vanofunga kuti vebato remaDemocrats vane mukana uri nani zvishoma.
U.S. Yakaisa Pachikero Pfungwa Yekuranga El Salvador Nekuda Kwekutsigira China, Asi Ndokuzosiyana Nazvo
Vamiririri vedzinyika vakaona kuti Dominican Republic uye Panama dzave kudyidzana nechekare neBeijing, pasina kudziviswa zvakanyanya neWashington.

Vakuru muHurumende yeNyika vakasarudza kudzosa vakuru vekuAmerica parwendo rwavo rwekumiririra nyika kubva kuEl Salvador, Dominican Republic uye Panama pamusoro "zvisarudzo zvichangobva kuitwa zvekusachakoshesa Taiwan," Heather Nauert, mutauriri wedhipatimendi iri, akadaro kutanga kwemwedzi uno .
Asi zvirango zvaingoda kupiwa nyika yeEl Salvador, iyo yakagamuchira zvinhu zverubatsiro zvine hukoshi hwemari inoita mamiriyoni $140 kubva kuAmerica mugore ra2017, kusanganisira kudzivirirwa kwekupinda nekubuda kwezvinodhaka, rutsigiro mune zvebudiriro uye zveupfumi.
Zvirango izvi zvaikarakadzwa, izvo zvaisanganisira kubviswa kwemari dzerubatsiro uye kusapiwa kwemavhiza kune vamwe vanhu, izvo zvingadai zvakarwadza nyika iyi yemuCentral American tichitarisa mwero wayo vakakura vekushayikwa kwemabasa nekupondwa kwevanhu.
Paienderera mberi misangano yemunyika, vakuru vemuNorth America neCentral America vakasundira mberi musangano vakakosha zvikuru vaive vakanangana nenhau yekuchengeteka kwenyika uye budiriro mune zveupfumi uri wekuongorora zvaive zvakakurukurwa pane mumwe vakaitwa gore rakapera uyo vakaonekwa sedanho rakanaka mukudzivisa vanhu kutizira kunyika yeUnited States.
Asi pakazosvika pakati pemwedzi waGunyana, vakuru vehurumende vakajekesa kuti vaida kuti musangano uyu uenderere mberi, zvichimisa pakarepo pfungwa yekupa zvirango nyika yeEl Salvador.
Mutevedzeri veNyika Mike Pence akazarudzwa kuti azotungamirira pamusangano uyu, uyo vakarongwa kuitwa pakati pemwedzi waGumiguru, pachiratidzwa nhau yekutengeserana iyo ichasimbisirwa nevakuru pamusangano uyu, vamiririri vakadaro.
Vamiririri veAmerica vakadzokera chinyararire kuEl Salvador, Panama uye Dominican Republic pasina mashoko makukutu kana zvirango zvakataurwa neWashington kunyika idzi.
Mutauriri veHurumende yeAmerica VaBolton vakaramba kutaura nezve pfungwa dzakabuda muhurukuro yakaitwa nevakuru veAmerica vatatu ava, kusanganisira vamiririri vaviri, avo vakabvumirana kuita idzi hurukuro pachivande.
Nyaya yavo yakasimbisirwa nemuongorori akazvimirira uyo ari pedyo nevakuru ava uyewo uyo akataura asingadi kuzivikanwa.
Nhoroondo Yechidzidzo
Nyaya ichatevera kunyorwa pasina kukundikana iri maererano nezvakanyorwa negweta Robert Mueller pamusoro pekuvhiringidzwa kwekuitwa kweruramisiro kunogona kuitwa naVaTrump, asiwo veruzhinji vave nehumboo hwakakura parizvino.
VaMueller vari kunziwo varikutendeukira pakuita ongororo yekuona kana kutsvaka rutsigiro kwaVaTrump kwakatsigirwa zvisiri pamutemo neRussia mukurwisana nesarudzo dzedu.
Kana Kongiresi ikashanduka, VaTrump vachazviwana vave kutarisana nekuzvidavirira kudare iroro, sezvavave kugadzirira zvakare kumira pamberi pevavhoti, uye zvichida pakupedzisira kutongwa neshamwari dzavo.
Pane pfungwa dzekuti dai dzakawanda, uye handidi kukarakadza kuti kudonha kwaVaTrump hakudzivisiki - kana kuti vakada kufanana naani muEurope.
Pane zvisarudzo zvinofanira kuitwa nesu tose kumativi ose eNyika ari maviri izvo zvichatema kureba kwenguva yekutambudzika.
Muna 1938, mapurisa emuGerman ainge akagadzirira kubvuta masimba kuna Hitler, izvo bedzi zvaizoitika kana Nyika Dzekumadokero dzaizorwisana naye uye kutsigira vekuCzechoslovakia vari paMunich.
Takakundikana, uye kurasikirwa nemukana vekudzivisa kufa kwevanhu kwakazotevera.
Mafambiro enhoroondo akabatwa mumativi ekuchinja iwayo, uye kufora kwekuuya kwehutongi hwegutsaruzhinji kusingadzivisike kuchakurumidziswa kana kunonotswa.
vanhu vekuAmerica vakatarisana nemativi ekuchinja akawanda parizvino.

Amai vangu vaiva muJudha vekunyika yeCzechoslovakia avo vakadzorerwa kuAuschwitz nehurumende yeNazi imwe-cheteyo iyo yaimbove nemumiririri wayo munyika yangu.
